# CHAPTER 2 HULL

## 2.1 HULL CONSTRUCTION

2.1.1 GENERAL

For the materials of hull steel of structures exposed to low air temperatures shall be based on the design temperature tD (the lowest mean daily average air temperature in the area of operation) of -10℃. (refer to IACS UR S6) ***(Rev 9 July 2018)***

#### 2.1.1.1 Scantling

The scantling of hull structure members shall be based on the scantling draught of the Vessel in compliance with the Rules requirements of the Classification Society.

Design stack load in cargo holds to be as follows.

20ft container: 30.5 MT / TEU (152.5 MT/Stack)

40ft container: 30.5 MT / FEU (152.5 MT/Stack)

the design stack load for container on upper deck shall be as follows:

20ft container: **90** MT/Stack

40ft container: **120** MT/Stack

The scantlings, which are not specified by the Classification Society, shall be in accordance with the Builder’s practice.

Finite element analysis and fatigue strength analysis shall be performed according to the Rules requirement of the Classification Society.

**The fatigue life of hull structure to be in accordance with Class requirement for 25 years worldwide service.**

***Still water bending moment and shear force during cargo loading and otherwise must never exceed 92%.***

#### 2.1.1.2 Material

Hull structure members shall be of mild steel and high tensile steel approved by the Classification Society. The steel material including casting and forging shall be of qualities complying with the Rules requirements of the Classification Society.

High tensile steel with minimum yield stress of 315N/mm2 and 355N/mm2 shall be used where necessary.

Steel material not specified by the Classification Society shall be of ordinary commercial quality in accordance with Chinese Industrial Standard as per the Builder's practice.

All frames, beams and stiffeners to be of rolled section, bulb bar, flat bar or built-up section.

#### 2.1.1.3 Workmanship

The works for hull construction shall be carried out in accordance with the Builder's practice and under the survey of the Classification Society.

Chinese Shipbuilding Quality Standard (CSQS) (GB/T34000-2016) and/or Builder's and Maker's Quality Standard shall be applied for workmanship of hull construction and outfitting.

***Builder’s Standards and Practices will submit to owner for review at the beginning of detail design stage.***

#### 2.1.1.4 Welding

Welding procedure including edge preparation shall be executed in accordance with the Builder's practice and approved by the Classification Society except unimportant or attachment weld which shall be carried out as per Builder's practice.

Welding shall be performed for the entire hull structure by manual, gravity, electro gas or any other automatic welding including CO2 semi-automatic shall be applied as per Builder's practice.

Fillet welding for the entire hull structure shall be double side continuous, except in some special area which the double side fillet welding can not be applied. In accommodation area and ventilation pipe, the intermittent or one side continuous fillet welding can be adopted.

Excessive distortion of hull structures due to welding shall be cured by means of cold press, line heating or spot heating. The IACS Rec.47 Shipbuilding and Repair Quality Standard is applicable as reference.

***If needed plate thickness to be increased to meet strength requirement, the treatment shall be according to class requirement.***

#### 2.1.1.5 Slot, Scallop and Hole

Slots, scallops, air holes and drain holes shall be provided where necessary in accordance with the Builder's practice and shall be avoided in high stress areas.

In general, non-watertight structural members shall be provided with access and/or lightening holes as per the Rules requirements of the Classification Society and the Builder's practice, provided that such holes are not detrimental to the local strength of structural members.

***Lightening holes on horizontal surface shall be provided with protections bars as per IACS REC 47.***

#### 2.1.1.6 Access Opening and Temporary Piece

Access opening for Builder’s workers during construction and for future convenience shall be provided for each cellular space in the double bottom and vertical wing spaces as shown on the Midship Section Plan.

Provisional access opening may be opened where required for access, communication and/or ventilation, etc. for the Builder’s workers during construction and shall be closed by welding after completion of the construction work.

Temporary pieces such as staging pieces, lifting lugs and their reinforcements, etc. fitted to the hull structure for construction may remain as per the Builder's practice unless they are inconvenient for the Vessel’s service and/or painting work. If temporary pieces should be removed, they will be cut off near the root and the edge to be properly finished.

***Temporary access opening drawing will be provided to owner and the area where needs inspection to be discussed at site.***

#### 2.1.1.7 Strength and Leak Test for Hull Tanks

Structural strength test and leak test shall be carried out in compliance with the Rules requirements of the Classification Society and the Builder’s practice.

Leak test shall be carried out by pressurized air using soapy water at assembly or erection stages. However, fillet and erection joints of the tank boundaries may be tested locally by a compressed air or vacuum testing device.

Hydrostatic structural strength test shall be carried out for ***the tanks that over 20m3 except cofferdam and void space in accordance with the requirements of Classification Society***, by filling with water during construction or afloat at Builder’s convenience to demonstrate the structural adequacy. However the hydrostatic test may be replaced by the air test subject to the agreement with the Classification Society and the Buyer for the subsequent Vessel(s).

Weather-tight and/or watertight doors, hatches, etc. shall be tested with water hose or pouring in accordance with requirements of the Classification Society.

Rudder shall be leak tested with air after completion of fabrication.

#### 2.1.1.8 Welding Seam Test

Non-destructive test (NDT) shall be carried out in accordance with the requirements of the Classification Society.

The location and extension of the NDT shall be in compliance with the requirements of the Classification Society and NDT plan approved by Classification Society.

2.1.2 MAIN HULL

#### 2.1.2.1 General

The structural details shall be in accordance with the Builder's agreed practice and shall be approved by the Classification Society.

Adequate drain holes and air holes shall be provided in the internal structural members in tanks to ensure free movement of contents to suctions and of air escape to vents and shall keep away from high stress areas.

The reinforcement for docking shall be carried out in accordance with the requirement of the Classification Society.

The decks under machinery and other heavy concentrated loads shall be reinforced according to the Rules requirements of the Classification Society.

Step and hand grips shall be provided for the access opening of which sill height is over 600 mm according to the requirement of the Classification Society and the Builder’s practice.

Lightening holes on the horizontal stringers shall be protected with steel bars to prevent personnel falling through according to the Builder’s practice.

Flat plate keel shall be provided throughout the Vessel’s length and connected to the stem and stern frame.

***All FO tanks with capacity more than 30 m3 shall be protected by double hull structure.***

***Opening in the shell plating, deck girders, etc. to be rounded and reinforced by snipped end flat bar where ever necessary.***

***Hand grip for access manhole according to shipyard standard, yard will supply standard for owner approval.***

#### 2.1.2.2 Aft Body Construction

The stern shall be of open water type to obtain adequate clearance for the propeller and to support the rudder.

Steering gear room shall be arranged on the steering gear platform above the aft peak void.

Necessary eye plates for lifting rudder, shaft and propeller shall be provided.

**The shafting shall be so designed that the propeller can be dismounted without unshipping the rudder, but the steering gear shall be able to turn suitable degree (with dismantle limit stopper/ram pin to release the rudder angle restriction) to enable propeller removal.**

The stern frame shall be consist of steel plates, stern tube unit and weldable cast steel partly.

The stern tube unit shall be fixed to hull structure by stern frame bossing-piece by resin chock.

Aft peak bulkhead shall be of plane type with adequate stiffeners.

Stern tube cooling water tank shall be arranged below the aft peak void.

#### 2.1.2.3 Engine Room Construction

Double bottom

The double bottom in the engine room shall be built on transverse framing system with solid floor in general.

Continuous longitudinal girders shall be provided in the double bottom so that the main engine including thrust block can be set directly on the double bottom. Main engine foundation shall be strengthened in accordance with the main engine Maker’s recommendation.

Double bottom knuckling shall be 50mm away from main double bottom floor.

L.O. sump tank below main engine shall be surrounded by cofferdam at sides and bottom to comply with main engine Maker’s recommendation.

Necessary tanks and bilge wells shall be arranged at suitable place in the double bottom.

Decks, side shell and engine casing, etc.

Upper deck and side shell shall be longitudinally framed and side shell shall be transversely or longitudinally in general.

Platform decks shall be arranged in engine room. These decks shall be extended from side to side with opening around main engine. Openings in the engine room decks shall be fitted with coamings of 100mm height.

Bulkheads and engine casing shall be constructed of steel plate with stiffeners and welded to the decks.

Primary structural member shall be arranged as required by the layout of machinery paying special care to minimize transmission of machinery vibration.

Tanks

Storage, settling and service tanks etc. for fuel oil and lubricating oil shall be arranged in the engine room as shown on the G.A. plan.

However, arrangement of small independent tanks such as service tanks for cylinder oil etc. to be shown on the Machinery Arrangement in E/R, which to be submitted during detail design stage.

***Engine control room***

***Engine control room shall be provided with two windows of size 1.2m x 0.8m to get the direct view of Main Engine from ECR.***

Funnel

The funnel shall be of mild steel construction with vertical stiffeners and horizontal stringers inside, and with top roof, adequate number of eye plate, scupper pipe, and steel door on it. The funnel top shall be sloped slightly aft to aid drainage to the scuppers aft.

Eye plates on the upper part of the funnel shall be provided in accordance with the Builder’s practice.

#### 2.1.2.4 Cargo Hold Area Construction

The Vessel to have four (4) individual cargo holds divided by transverse watertight bulkheads.

Double bottom

Double bottom shall be arranged throughout cargo holds as shown on the G.A. plan.

Double bottom under the cargo holds shall be built with longitudinal framing supported by solid floor fitted at appropriate spacing. Longitudinal girders shall be arranged at appropriate spacing.

***Doublers*** shall be welded on tank top, and local stiffening shall be provided at container corners under the tank top in accordance with the Builder’s practice.

Two (2) bilge wells shall be provided at the aft corner of every cargo hold, outside of container corner area and accessible.

Side construction

Side shell and longitudinal bulkhead to be longitudinally framed, in general.

The ship side shall be of double hull construction in way of the cargo area.

Watertight bulkhead

The watertight transverse bulkheads shall be arranged as shown on the G.A. plan.

The transverse bulkheads shall be of plane type construction with adequate stiffeners and primary members.

Structural bulkhead

The non-tight grillage shaped structural bulkheads shall be fitted in the middle of each cargo hold between 40ft container bays.

The structural bulkheads shall have sufficient strength to support the container load transmitted by cell guides fitted thereon.

Stringer decks to be provided as walkway for each 8'6" container tier in cargo holds. The structure to be strengthened to allow for flexi loading capability for the high cube containers in hold.

***Stiffeners used on bulkhead between ballast tank and fuel oil tank shall be on fuel tank side.***

Deck construction

The upper deck shall be connected to the shell plating by the square gunwale with 100mm extension above. ***Full/Deep penetration weld shall be used for Upper deck to Sheer strake connection (cargo hold).***

Upper deck plating outside of hatch openings shall be longitudinally framed and stiffened with transverse webs in way of cargo hold region.

The corner edge of hatch opening in the upper deck shall be reinforced in compliance with the requirements of the Classification Society.

Hatch coaming

Cargo hatch shall be arranged as shown on G.A plan. Each cargo hatch shall have steel coamings of suitable height for stowing of containers.

The hatch coaming to be of steel construction with stays as required by the Classification Society. ***Hatch end bracket shall be curved with two radius type and not the straight bracket.***

Side hatch coamings shall be continuous from forward to aft of cargo hold area and tapered at each ends according to the requirement of the Classification Society.

#### 2.1.2.5 Fore Body Construction

General

The fore body consists of store space(s), fore peak tank and chain lockers as shown on the G.A. plan.

The shell plating shall be increased in thickness at the anchor rubbing areas as per the Builder’s practice.

Framing at forward end to have deep floors, deep web frames, side stringers and breast hooks as required by the Classification Society.

Side frames in the fore peak tank shall be arranged transversely or longitudinally.

The bulkhead of fore peak tank shall be of flat type stiffened by horizontal or vertical stiffeners supported by vertical webs or horizontal stringers fitted at suitable space.

The strength of the forecastle deck shall consider impacts from green water as per Class requirement.

Fore body construction to be designed against bow flare slamming according to the requirement of the Classification Society.

The forecastle to be arranged as shown on the G.A. plan.

Chain locker and Hawse pipe, etc.

Two (2) self-stowing circular or rectangular type chain lockers with sufficient capacity shall be arranged to stow the anchor chains well clear of deck over.

The lockers shall be of watertight steel construction and fitted with perforated false bottom grating with one removable steel cover at a level approx. 800 mm above the bottom of the locker to make a bilge well space underneath.

Chain pipe with bell mouth shall be led vertically from windlass according to the Builder’s practice. Each one (1) set of chain pipe cover shall be provided.

The chain cable shall be secured by quick releasing type cable clench on the side wall of the chain locker. The cable clench shall be provided for the chain locker in easily accessible position accordance with the Builder’s practice.

One (1) access manhole to be arranged on each chain locker wall in bosun store for inspecting locker and cable.

One (1) pair of hawse pipe with cast steel bell mouse shall be provided at the bow and shall allow acceptable housing of the anchor and easy lead of chain to the gypsy wheel.

For the details, refer to “Chapter 4–Outfitting Part” of the Specification.

2.1.3 Deck House

Deckhouse shall be of welded steel construction.

External walls of deckhouse shall be of flat plate type with vertical stiffeners inside, and the internal walls shall be of flat plate type.

The arrangement of internal webs, pillars and steel bulkheads to be considered to minimize vibration.

Decks shall be transversely and/or longitudinally stiffened with beams and girders.

Bridge wings shall be extended to full beam of the Vessel and be suitably supported with open type construction.

Wheelhouse front wall and side wall with windows shall be inclined outward from navigation bridge deck as shown on the G.A. plan.

***As far as possible super structure exterior plates must be at least 6 mm.***

2.1.4 MISCELLANEOUS

Foundation

Foundation of main engine shall be of welded steel construction in conjunction with bed plate, floors and girders of double bottom structure and shall have adequate strength and rigidity.

Foundation of main engine shall be designed according to the Builder's practice and the manufacturer's recommendation.

Foundation of auxiliary machinery, deck machinery, etc. shall be of welded steel construction and shall be reinforced with girders or carlings underneath as per manufacturer’s recommendation and Builder’s practice.

***Main Engine foundation girders and face plates shall be welded with full penetration weld or deep penetration weld if class approval.***

Bilge keel

Non-continuous type bilge keel shall be fitted on the bilge strake port and starboard with about 25% of the Vessel’s L.B.P. amidships.

Bilge keel to be built up with flat-bar and bulb plate. The bulb plate is welded to a flat-bar attached onto bilge strake by welding. The butt seams on the bilge keel flat-bars and shell plates to be staggered each other as per the Rule.

The flat-bar to be of continuous type.

Fore and aft ends of the bilge keels shall be gradually tapered and discontinued at block butt joint. ***Tapering of the bilge keel at both the ends shall be done as per IACS guidelines. The ends detail to be shown in the detailed BILGE KEEL DWG.***

Sea chest

One (1) high sea chest and one (1) low sea chest shall be provided to side shell in way of engine room. One (1) separate sea chest shall be provided for emergency fire pump.

For details about drainage, air escape etc., refer to “Chapter 6–Machinery Part” of the Specification.

***Nuts and bolts used for sea chest fittings shall be of stainless steel.***

Bottom plug

One (1) bottom plug shall be supplied and fitted at ***bottom*** ballast water tank. Basically, the bottom plugs for oil tank and side ballast water tanks shall not be provided.

The size (M42), material (plug: SUS316, socket: mild steel) and design of the bottom plug shall be in accordance with the Builder’s practice. ***Spare parts of SS plugs to be provided*** ***according to yard practice.***

Bottom plugs shall be fitted as close as possible to the lowest point of each tank and shall be kept clear of points where the keel block is laid beneath in dry dock.

***Bottom plug sockets to be full penetration welded to Shell plate .Weld plug procedure will full weld and test for UT+PT or vacuum box(submit information to owner approval)***

Two (2) spanner wrenches for bottom plugs shall be supplied for opening/closing of bottom plugs. .

Bulwark

The bulwarks of steel plate, suitably stiffened by stays at moderate space, shall be fitted on the forecastle deck and bridge wings as shown on the G.A. plan.

Knuckled wind-deflector shall be provided on the front bulwarks of the navigation bridge wings.

The bulwark plating shall be reinforced in way of openings for fairleaders, etc., if necessary.

Step and safety handrail shall be provided on the bulwark for the inspection of anchor stowage and on the operation position of mooring ropes.

Breakwater

Breakwater to be provided as shown on the G.A. plan. The height of breakwater shall be determined according to ILLC and Class rule’s recommendation.

## 2.2 PAINTING CORROSION PROTECTION

2.2.1 GENERAL

Painting works including surface preparation and inspection shall be carried out based on this Specification.

Painting works to be executed in accordance with the Builder's painting standard, process, practice and paint manufacturer's recommendation.

**Stripe coats to be either sprayed or applied using brush/roller, will be confirmed at painting kick off meeting.**

Following standards shall be performed:

- ISO 8501-1, Preparation of steel substrates before application of paints and related products - Visual assessment of surface cleanliness

Painting works in ballast water tanks shall be carried out in compliance with IMO PSPC requirement as per Resolution MSC.215(82).

Technical supervision shall be provided by the paint manufacturer and the Builder during preparation and application.

Paint shall be applied by airless spray in principle, but air spray, brush or roller may be applied where airless spraying is impracticable.

No paint work shall be applied to the following, unless otherwise specified.

- Non-ferrous materials, i.e. copper, copper alloy (brass, bronze), aluminum, aluminum alloy and any other non-corrosive metals

- Polished fittings

- Galvanized fittings inside **(Galvanized fitting on deck area needs to be carried out same as deck specification)**

- Gaskets and packing

- Wood works in stores

- Inner surfaces of doubling plates

- Permanently enclosed space**(Closed area needs to apply one coat of primer application 100μ as far as possible)**

- Internal steel surface under deck covering **(Under deck covering to be applied with one coat of primer or not as per covering Maker’s requirement)**

Galvanized pipe and vent outside to be painted one finish coat as surrounding and inside not painted.

**Care to be taken to protect all cables during construction to avoid paint spillage on cables.**

The colors of finish coats shall be in accordance with the Buyer’s/Charter’s color scheme and subject to the Buyer’s approval.

All machinery and equipment shall be coated in accordance with manufacturer’s standard and damaged part after installation shall be touched up only in accordance with Builder’s practice. The inside of radar mast and steel vent ducts to be painted with one (1) coat of Builder's standard primer only if not permanently closed.

Painting demarcation line for outside shell shall be as per the Builder’s standard.

Abbreviation:

A/F : Anti-fouling paint

Sa 2.5 : Abrasive blasting to Sa 2.5 grade (ISO 8501-1)

St 2 : Power tool cleaning to St 2 grade (ISO 8501-1)

St 3 : Power tool cleaning to St 3 grade (ISO 8501-1)

2.2.2 SURFACE PREPARATION

2.2.2.1 Primary Surface Preparation

All steel plates and sections equal to or greater than 6 mm in thickness shall be shot blasted

to ISO8501-1:1988 Sa 2.5 or sand blasting to SA 2.5 or pickling or ST3 may be applied instead of shot blasting when shot blasting is considered impractical.

2.2.2.2 Shop priming

Just after primary surface preparation one coat of 15 microns silicate type shop primer to be applied. The shop primer to have good compatibility with the succeeding coats. Different color shop primer to be used for mild and high tensile steel plates and sections.

2.2.2.3 Secondary Surface Preparation

Before the first coat is applied, damages by welding, burning, rubbing, etc. and rusted steel surface shall be prepared in accordance with the following table. Intact shop primer to be sweep blasting or brush disk cleaning.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Area | In Block Stage | In Pre-erection, Dock & Quay Stage |
| Bottom and boot top | Sa 2.5 | ST3 |
| Topsides | Sa 2.5 | ST3 |
| Weather deck and hatch coaming | Sa 2.5 | ST3 |
| Hatch cover | Sa 2.5 (outside) | ST3(outside) |
| Sa 2.0 (inside) | ST2(inside) |
| Deckhouse exterior | ST 3 | ST 2 |
| Deckhouse interior | ST 2 | ST 2 |
| E/R interior | ST 2 | ST 2 |
| Water ballast tanks | Sa 2.5 | ST3 |
| Fresh water tanks | Sa 2.5 | ST3 |
| Cargo holds | ST 2 | ST 2 |
| F.O &.,D.O.tanks | No treatment | ST 1 |
| L.O. tanks | No treatment | Wiping with system oil after cleaning |
| Others | SIS ST 2 | SIS ST 2 |

2.2.2.4 Surface Cleaning Before Over-Coating

The surfaces shall be cleaned of oil, moisture, dust, and other foreign materials with thinner, fresh water, wire brush, or compressed air prior to coating.

2.2.3 PAINTING WORK

The painting shall be carried out by airless spray, in general. Where the spraying is impracticable, the brush or roller shall be used.

**The first full coat shall be spray, then roller and brush can be used. Roller and brush can be used in difficult and narrow area.**

Mixing and thinning of paint material, conditions/methods of application and minimum and maximum over coating time of painting application shall be in accordance with paint manufacturer's recommendation and data sheets.

Free-edges of steel members which have been gas cut and welding slag remains shall be ground in accordance with the Builder's practice, WBT as per PSPC.

After the first coat one (1) stripe coat shall be applied on the edges of holes, scallops and frames in fresh water tanks and water/weather-exposed areas as well as cargo holds behind and between cell guides in accordance with the Builder’s practice. The stripe coat colour same with the full coat colour.

Watertight weld lines by manual welding shall be painted after air test has been finished, but adhesive tape and touch up of shop-primer may be performed during painting application.

2.2.4 INSPECTION OF THE FILM THICKNESS

**Paint work will not start unless a block has been accepted or a written waiver is given by the Buyer’s representative.**

**For the paint, date of manufacture, batch number, shelf life and expiry dates to be provide as per paint maker’s standard.**

**Paint samples will be taken by Buyer’s site team and sent to paint Maker factory for analysis to confirm Maker’s formula is used.**

The checking of final paint dry film thickness shall be carried out by the Builder in the presence of Buyer's representative and paint manufacturer.

Measuring

The cleaning condition and dry film thickness between coats shall be inspected by two (2) parties, the Builder and the paint maker. **Builder will provide daily schedule to Buyer’s site office in the morning time.** The Buyer will carry out the patrolling inspection.

In general, two (2) separate spot measurements shall be made over every 10 m2 in tanks, and for each 20 m2 in other spaces. The average of five (5) separate spot measurements must be within the specified thickness. For PSPC areas and fresh water and technical water tanks areas, rule 90%-90% shall apply as acceptance criteria for DFT measurement. **Total**

**DFT specified in painting schedule shall be attained in at least 85% of the painted area and balance 15% measured should be not less than 85% of specified DFT.**

In any measurement there is a certain level of uncertainty. Two inspectors using the same gage will not necessarily record the exact same number for given spot measurement. To allow for this natural fluctuation, an individual spot measurement is permitted to be below the 85% of specified minimum thickness, however The average of the means(3 points in the same 4cm diameter circle) shall not be less than the specified 85% of minimum thickness.

No measurement shall be made for about 100mm breadth from free edges of painted steel members, machinery, equipment, outfitting, pipes with nominal diameter of 250 mm and below, pipe supports, machinery seats, small fittings, etc.

***Dry Film thickness always to be measured at every stage of coating, final confirm will be done after anti-corrsion paint finish.***

2.2.5 control

2.2.5.1 Painting Work

Mixing and thinning of paint material, conditions/methods of application and time interval between each coat shall be observed to the paint manufacturer's recommendation.

Paint works shall not be performed in the open air during the periods of rain, snow, fog or mist and also shall not be carried out when the weather conditions may cause condensation i.e., relative humidity above 85% and steel temperature is lower than the dew point by three (3) degrees in centigrade except the case that paint maker has confirmed that a particular paint can be applied at such weather condition.

During coating processes, when dispute happen, the final arbitration shall come from the painting maker.

**Any condition deviation from Paint’s MDS for application in relation to RH and Steel temperature must be given by Maker’s Office in writing and stamped. E-Mail correspondence is not acceptable.**

2.2.5.2 Dry Film Thickness

In general, two (2) spot measurements for each 10 m2 in tanks and holds, and for each 20m2 in other spaces shall be measured.

2.2.6 Painting Scheme

Painting scheme for the parts and spaces, which are not specified herein, shall be similar to surrounding space or comparable spaces.

Epoxy finishes will chalk and exposed deck to have a Polyurethane finish coat.

Final dry film thickness and painting system shall be as listed below in the specification, changeable according to paint manufacturer’s recommendation subject to the Buyer’s approval.

Notes:

1. Dry film thickness of tin free type antifouling paint shall be in accordance with manufacturers’ standard for 60 months life time.
2. Non-slip paint shall be applied for upper deck passageway and mooring surrounding, forecastle deck, and for the deck in steering gear room, other anti-slip method may instead.
3. Painting scheme to be in accordance with the following specification or equivalent products, from the makers in Maker’s List. The positions not mentioned hereinafter should be painted same as the surrounding area or similar positions. Number of coats and total DFT (dry film thickness) might be adjusted according to paint manufacturer’s recommendation.
4. Welding defect such as blow hole or pore and undercut where not affect the structure strengthen will be applied the epoxy filler which recommended by paint maker.
5. The paint on the shell outside will be finished before launch, if the period between the launch and delivery is not more than 8 months and if paint manufacturer will give anti fouling system a guarantee for five(5) years, no final dry docking to be carried out for the vessel.
6. In any measurement there is a certain level of uncertainty. Two inspectors using the same gage will not necessarily record the exact same number for given spot measurement. To allow for this natural fluctuation, an individual spot measurement is permitted to be below the ***85%*** of specified minimum thickness, however The average of the means(3 points in the same 4cm diameter circle) shall not be less than the specified ***85%*** of minimum thickness.
7. Dry film thickness shall be measured after each coat for quality control purpose and the total dry film thickness shall be confirmed after completion of final coat. The quality control shall be carried out by shipyard and paint maker.
8. The E/R, accommodation, free board, cargo hold，main deck etc. area only apply one coat, ***No DFT measurement for E/R, ACC C/H etc., only one primer as holding primer at block stage. Final DTF to be measured and confirmed at erection/dock/quay stage,*** ***Void, WBT , shellplate etc., which will be finished final coat at block stage need to be DFT measurement.*** **Buyers should be informed the final coat before equipment installed on board.**
9. Time schedule for application of each coat to be decided according to builder's construction schedule, all inspections without disturbing builder's construction schedule. Painting inspection schedule to be submitted to Buyer at the same day morning.
10. Some outfitting, some small area painting job which will affect other department schedule will be carried out de-rusting and painting by shipyard self. **Shipyard to carry out the final coat for cable tray/cable supports and control panel supports before installation of the cable/panels.**
11. The intermediate coat and stripe coat to be inspected by Builder QC and Paint Manufacturer's representative , the inspection of final coat/surface preparation are to be done by Builder QC and Paint Manufacturer's representative and owners supervisor .
12. The spray dust of adjacent painting may be left as it is where it is considered harmless to the performance or to the appearance.
13. When owner chose the Scrubber maker, the discharge PH in tanks should be >5.
14. Minor paint contamination need not to be cleaned.
15. **The fore mast inside to be painted as far as possible (no blasting due to grit can clean inside).**
16. **If maker require, Report providing data of surface roughness will submit as per Anti Fouling maker’s standard after application of anti-fouling paint prior launching. Shipyard will assistant maker if maker required.**
17. **PSPC Tri-Partite Agreement to be developed by the Builder and submitted for the Buyer’s review and acceptance prior to final signing by the Builder, Buyer and Paint Maker.**
18. **Coating Technical File (CTF) will be developed by the yard and sent to the Buyers for review.**
19. **The painting of the exposed structural steel surface such as outsides of shell, deckhouse, funnel, etc., and of living space and passages in living quarters to be free from obvious sags and runs.**
20. **The steel structure surfaces including all welded seams to be painted before the leak test, in general. However, fillet welding joint and erection butt joint forming tank boundary to be painted after joint has been examined either by compressed air test, vacuum test or tank air test as appropriate.**
21. **Pre-erection joint of hull block which is erected at any location, to be painted before leak test and not to be considered as block erection joint.**
22. **Under water hull paint thickness to be checked before and after application of antifouling paint and recorded at dock stage.**
23. **For the F.W.TK ventilation and washing, the Builder will accord paint maker's recommendation. The chemical component analyzes of water sample in these tanks to be carried out by authorized office and the report should be submitted to owner together with the delivery certificates.**
24. **Main sea water filter body internals will be coated with anti-fouling paint.**
25. **Exhaust pipes outside will be coated with temperature resistant paint before placing the insulation,** **the area under insulation no need to paint.**
26. **PSPC blocks will be treated as PSPC requirements.**
27. **All the bilge well in passageway/cargo hold/Chain locker to be applied 150\*2.**
28. ***Maker of Anti Fouling to submit a report providing data of surface roughness after application of anti fouling paint if maker has this requirement.***
29. ***TSL: outfitting / cable/supports and some small area Owner will be informed the plan before install the equipment.***
30. ***Minor/spots paint need not to be removed if under insulation/lining.***

2.2.7 GALVANIZING

Galvanizing shall be applied for items as described throughout this Specification and following outfitting shall also be galvanized:

* Handles and clips of steel doors
* Small chains (8mm dia. and below)
* Small shackles and thimbles (8mm dia. and below)
* Hinges, small bolts and nuts under 12mm dia. exposed to weather
* Standing rigging for masts
* Ventilator ducts (thickness below 2 mm) (refer to galvanized thin plate spire ducts, mainly used for accommodation etc.)
* Steps of inclining and vertical ladders on weather deck
* Chain pipe and hawse pipe covers
* ***outfitting in WBT to be galvanized.***

Outfitting may apply one universal epoxy coat according to Builder’s practice.

The galvanizing shall be done by hot dip method in general except bolts, nuts, screws, etc. which are to be electroplated, unless otherwise specified in this Specification. Damaged area of galvanizing part caused by the electric welding, mechanical damage, etc. shall be touched-up by one (1) coat of Zinc Rich or epoxy primer as far as practicable.

In general, the steel outfittings to be painted with one (1) coat of the Builder’s standard epoxy primer.

* + 1. CATHODIC PROTECTION

1. The underwater hull and appendages shall be protected by an automatically controlled Impressed Current Cathodic Protection (ICCP) system.

Mean current density: 35 mA/m2for underwater hull

600 mA/m2for propeller

120 mA/m2for rudder

1. Aluminum alloy anodes shall be fitted inside sea chests and bow thruster tunnel.

Mean current density: 35 mA/m2

Life time: five (5) years

Sea chest filter shall be protected by MGPS aluminum and copper anodes.

The size, quantity and fitting method of ICCP system and anodes shall be as per the Builder’s practice and/or Maker’s recommendation.

# CHAPTER 3 ACCOMMODATION

Cabin arrangement shall be as shown on G.A. plan.

The clear height of accommodation spaces between the deck surface covering and the underside of deck head beam or ceiling shall be about 2,100 mm in general, except that to be about 2,030 mm in sanitary, catering spaces, refrigerated provision stores, ***2300mm for Gymnasium if possible.*** However, the protruding parts shall be excluded from the measurement.

In wheelhouse, the clear height between the bridge deck surface covering and the underside of the deck head beam or ceiling shall be at least 2,200 mm, and the lower edge of deck head mounted equipment shall be about 2,100 mm.

## 3.1 COMPLEMENTAND CLASSIFICATION OF ACCOMMODATION

| Petty officer | 1-Boatswain | 1-Chief Motorman | 2 |
| Rating | 5-Seaman  1-Cook | 5-Motorman | 11 |
| Others | 1-Pilot (Junior officer class) | | 1 |

|  | | | |
| Suez crew (not included in the complement ) |  |  | 6 |

## 3.2 JOINER WORK

### 3.2.1 DIVISIONAL BULKHEAD, LINING AND CEILING

The arrangement of all walls, bulkheads, lining and ceilings in living quarters shall be in accordance with Method “IC” as specified in SOLAS.

Corridor bulkheads, except steel wall shall be constructed of “B” class fire retarding panel.

Internal division bulkheads between cabins shall be “C” class panel. Non-combustible ceiling shall be provided in all cabins, public space and wheelhouse and “B” class non- combustible ceiling shall be provided in corridor of living space.

Partition wall, lining and ceiling shall be according to Rule’s requirement.

Watertight coaming with one side continuous welding to be applied for water-tightness in way of wet space and exterior steel boundary bulkhead.

Wall panels to be jointed and installed shall be in accordance with the Maker’s standard. Other detail of securing and construction shall in accordance with the Builder’s practice, unless otherwise required by the Rule and Regulation.

The Builder shall provide color samples for the Buyer’s selection of panel finishing.

3.2.1.1 Partition Bulkhead

The material and thickness of partition bulkhead to be as follows.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Corridor bulkhead (“B” class) and division bulkhead | Rock wool insulation of 50 mm thickness furnished with galvanized steel sheet of 0.6 mm thickness decorated with PVC film on both sides. |
| Partition bulkhead between two adjacent cabins (without neighboring bed), cabin and public space | Rock wool insulation of 50mm thickness furnished with galvanized steel sheet of 0.6 mm thickness decorated with PVC film on both sides. |
| Partition bulkhead between two adjacent cabins with neighboring bed. | Double 25mm thick rock wool board with 30mm clearance, (the total thickness to be 80mm), Rock wool insulation of 25mm thickness furnished with galvanized steel sheet of 0.6 mm thickness decorated with PVC film on visible sides. |

3.2.1.2 Lining and Ceiling

The lining and ceiling to be applied as follows.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Compartment | Lining | Ceiling |
| Living space  Public space  Office space  Control space (only for Wheelhouse and ECR)  Corridor space  Private toilet  Dispensary bath room | Rock wool insulation of 25mm thickness furnished with galvanized steel sheet of 0.6 mm thickness decorated with PVC film on visible side. | Rock wool insulation of 25mm thickness furnished with galvanized steel sheet of 0.6 mm thickness decorated with PVC film on visible side. |
| Catering space | Rock wool insulation of 25 mm thickness furnished with SUS304 sheet of 0.5mmthickness on visible side. | Rock wool insulation of 25 mm thickness furnished with SUS304 sheet of 0.5mmthickness on visible side. |
| Stevedore’s toilet, Public toilet, Changing room, Laundry and drying room | Paint finish in case of steel fabrication | Paint finish in case of steel fabrication |
| Dry provision store  Machinery space  Fire control station  Sundry space (except lockers and store-rooms having area less than 4m2) | Paint finish in case of steel fabrication | Paint finish in case of steel fabrication |

### 3.2.2 FIRE INSULATION, HEAT INSULATION AND SOUND ISOLATION

Fire insulation, heat insulation and sound insulation shall be applied to accommodation quarter in accordance with relevant Rules and Regulations as follows.

Approximate bulk density of insulation material shall be as follows or according to

Maker’s recommendation:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Heat and sound insulation | ***Rock wool (abt.100 kg/m3) or Glass wool (abt.40 kg/m3)*** |
| Fire insulation | Ceramic fiber ***(as per maker's standard )*** |

#### 3.2.2.1 Fire Insulation

Fire insulation shall be provided according to requirements of SOLAS.

#### 3.2.2.2 Heat Insulation

The parts of steel walls and decks of compartment in accommodation space exposed to weather shall be insulated in accordance with the following table:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Material | Application |
| 50 mm Glass wool with 25 mm beam cover. | Deck head where exposed to weather of living space |
| **100** mm Glass wool with 25 mm beam cover | Deck head of wheelhouse |
| 50mm Glass wool with 25 mm stiffener cover. | Bulkhead exposed to weather of living space |

The other spaces not mentioned on the above table shall have no insulation.

As for the spaces partially exposed to weather, the insulation shall be extended by 450mm inside beyond the boundary as far as practicable. The structural members greater than 450mm in depth shall be insulated by 450mm in depth and the remaining parts shall be left bare.

#### 3.2.2.3 Sound Isolation

Sound isolation shall be designed to fulfill the requirement of IMO Res. MSC.337 (91).

About 50mm glass wool covered with glass cloth shall be fitted if necessary. Attachments of beams, girders, stiffeners etc. to be completely insulated with 25 mm glass wool.

Sound insulation shall be provided in Air conditioning unit room, Engine control room and E/R fan rooms.

Detailed solutions of sound isolation shall be decided based on results of noise analysis and prediction during detail design stage.

#### 3.2.2.4 Coverage of Insulation

The surface of insulation material shall be covered with as follows:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Material | Application |
| Glass cloth | Protected insulation by wall/ceiling panels or galvanized steel sheet |
| Glass cloth coated with aluminum foil | Unprotected insulation, which is covered by neither wall/ceiling panels nor galvanized steel sheet |

### 3.2.3 DECK COVERING

Deck covering shall be applied as per following list:

| Material | Application |
| --- | --- |
| A-60 deck covering | according to  SOLAS requirement |
| 5 mm thick full synthetic carpet on 10 mm latex type deck composition, | Captain class bed room |
| 2mm PVC on 10mm latex type deck composition, | Other living space, corridors, public spaces and office space |
| 3mm thick rubber tile including studs (non-slip type) on 10mm latex type deck composition | Wheelhouse ***and ECR*** |
| Ceramic tile on 30 mm cement  (Anti-slip type) | Galley, pantry, laundry and drying room, all toilets, and lavatories (as per maker’s standard) |
| Paint (steel deck ) | Store and locker space, deck workshop, machinery space, all exposed steel decks and other similar spaces (except mentioned above.) |

Deck covering shall not be applied on all the weather deck surfaces.

The floor top covering or finished coat on latex type deck composition shall not be applied under fixed furniture with baseboard such as bed, wardrobe, locker etc.

Floating floor shall be applied for Engine control room.

The type of floating floor maybe apply according to noise and vibration analyses suggestion.

Gutter ways shall be fitted for galley which formed by stainless steel plate and covered by stainless steel cover.

The space applied with joiner lining and partition shall be provided with approx. 60mm high plastic skirting. The space applied with tile shall be provided with approx. 150mm high tile skirting.

The deck covering for wet space shall slope to scupper.

Non-slip type rubber mat with 1,000 mm breath and 3mm thickness shall be provided to the front and back side of the Main Switchboard (MSB), Transformers, emergency switchboard and local group starter panel. ***These mats will be certified.***

Perforated rubber mat of 15 mm thickness shall be provided on navigation bridge wing area.

## WINDOW, DOOR, STAIRWAY, ETC.

### 3.3.1 WINDOW

The quantity of windows for cabins and rooms to be provided according to the following standard.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Location | Number |
| Captain class dayroom (one window size will be 800x700) | 2 |
| Senior officer class dayroom | 2 |
| Captain / Senior officer class bedroom,  Junior officer / Petty officer / Rating class cabin | 1 |
| Crew’s mess room, Ship office | 3 |
| Officer’s mess room, Gymnasium Recreation room , Meeting room, Hospital, Galley | 2 |
| pantry | 1 |
| Engine control room | 2 |

The size, shape and material of windows as shown in following table.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Size(mm) | Shape | Material | Location |
| 800 x 700 | Rectangular | Steel | Recreation room, mess rooms |
| 450x630 | Rectangular | Steel | All living space, public space (except above), office space and catering space |
| abt. \* 1,900 x 1,200  fixed type | Rectangular | Steel | Wheelhouse front wall |
| abt. \* 1,500 x 1,200  fixed type | Rectangular | Steel | Wheelhouse aft and side wall |
| abt. 1,200 x 650 | Rectangular | Steel | Engine control room |

\* Size and quantity of wheelhouse window may be adjusted in accordance with the wheelhouse arrangement in detail design stage.

No mosquito screen to be provided.

The glass for windows shall be of safety glass ***(tempered and or shatter proof)***. The frame of windows shall be of painted steel and welded to steel wall, in general. Coaming to be steel type. The glass retaining frame to be aluminum alloy. Steel window box to be fitted except that wheelhouse windows..

All opening type windows should be opened inward. Where two windows or three windows adjacent, only one to be of the opening type.

Center line height of windows to be about 1,500 mm from steel deck.

Cleaning stage or access way of about 600 mm width for wheelhouse front windows shall be provided. A door shall be provided for access from navigation bridge wing to cleaning stage respectively for port side and starboard.

Wheelhouse front windows shall be washed by spraying fresh water from the pipe outside the windows.

The sun screens of roller type to be fitted on front windows of wheelhouse.

***The ‘Blind Sector’ roller type to be fitted on Placement of chart table and radio station.***

Three (3) windows in front of wheel house shall be provided with electric heater.

Two (2) rotary clear view screens to be provided in front of wheel house window.

### .3.3.2 DOOR

Doors shall be arranged according to G.A. plan.

Mosquito screen will not be fitted.

#### 3.3.2.1 Steel Door

Steel doors shall be hinged type, except specified, and shall be provided as follows:

| Type | Material | Clear width  (mm) | Location |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Weather tight | Steel plate | 800 | * Entrance from exposed deck to corridor （except wheel house） * Entrance from exposed Upper deck to CO2 room * Entrance from exposed deck to Dispensary * Entrance from exposed deck to Bosun store, paint store |
| Weather tight | Steel plate | 700 | * Entrance from exposed Upper deck to Garbage store * Entrance from exposed A deck to Emergency generator room * Entrance to Bosun store, Safety equipment store * Entrance from exposed deck to Refrigerated chamber * Entrance from exposed deck to Gym * Entrance from exposed deck to Steering gear room stair * Entrance from exposed deck to engine room escape |
| Weather tight | Steel plate | 650 | * All other weather tight door form expose deck to cabin. |
| Watertight, | Steel plate | 700 | * Entrance from E/R to steering gear room (subject to Rule requirement), |
| Watertight, | Steel plate | 650 | * Entrance from E/R to side void space, (subject to Rule requirement) |
| Steel door with ventilation grille | Steel plate | 650 | * Oxygen/acetylene bottle store |
| Sliding type, hollow with square window | Stainless steel | 1,000 | * Entrance from exposed Bridge deck to Wheelhouse |
| Wire mesh door | Steel | 700 | * ER spare room, elec. store |

Notes:

\*1) watertight door to be provided with open/close indication on wheelhouse.

2) The tightness of the steel doors (weather-tight or watertight) may be adjusted based on requirement of damage stability.

All steel doors shall be of rectangular, hinged type with round corner, except otherwise specified.

Steel hinged single handle weather door with fixed rectangular window shall be provided for entrance door to accommodation corridor, cylinder lock will be install for the entrance door that fulfill with ISPS rules. .

Weather tight steel doors shall be of welding of seal channels continuous with synthetic rubber gasket, and pad lock eye plate( or cylinder lock) and fixing hook and door stopper according to the purpose intended, and shall be provided in accordance with the requirement of the Rule/Regulations and the Builder’s standard.

The height from covering of the deck to the top of steel door opening shall be of 2,000 mm.

Height of weather tight steel door sill shall meet ICLL requirement. Door sill of entrance from weather deck shall be abt. 150 mm high above steel deck where there is no Rule requirement.

Sill height shall be measured from top of deck plate, even where deck covering is applied subject of LL requirement.

Foot step to be installed only to sills with height equal and above 600 mm.

The weather tight door for emergency escape trunk shall be of quick-open type.

#### 3.3.2.2 Internal Accommodation Door

Stairway doors to be held open on magnetic catches and released by the fire alarm system.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Kind of Doors | Material and Type | Location |
| "A-60" class fire protection | "A-60" class approved, steel sash type | In accordance with SOLAS |
| "A-0" class fire protection | "A-0" class approved, steel sash type | In accordance with SOLAS |
| "B" class fire protection | "B" class approved, steel sash type | In accordance with SOLAS |
| Light type (P.V.C. film) | Steel sash hollow door with vent mesh | Private toilet |
| Sound proof type | Pontoon type steel door with sound insulation | Engine control room |

Notes:

* + 1. Self-closing door devices shall be fitted according to rules requirement.
    2. Door catcher with cushion shall be fitted on all doors except those with self-closing device.

Clear height of internal accommodation door to be abt.1,950mm above the surface deck covering except door of private toilet and the door between the two spaces that the deck covering's thickness difference is more than 90mm.

Clear width of internal accommodation door opening to be as shown in the following table.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Clear width (mm) | Location |
| 800 | Entrance to corridor, Galley, From Pantry to Officer’s mess room, Dry provision |
| 700 | Stairways, Fire control station, Lobby, Mess rooms, Ship office, Recreation room, Meeting room, escape in ER, Fire control station, entrance door to ER, |
| 600 | Private lavatory |
| 650 | All other internal accommodation doors |

#### 3.3.2.3 Hardware

All hardware shall be of marine type.

##### 3.3.2.3.1 Lock

All door handles shall be of lever type，***the springs to be moderately heavy type.***

All locks and latches shall have rim or mortise type casing to meet the requirements of particular installations.

Locks shall be furnished so that each lock will have a different key, and all locks except lavatory locks can be opened by a master key.

All living cabins shall have mortise type cylinder lock and latch set with thumb turn.

Public space, catering space, wheelhouse, fire control station, engine control room, laundry, changing room and inside lockers shall have mortise type cylinder lock and latch set.

Weather doors on A to F deck and wheelhouse to have mortise lock.

Public/deck toilet and hospital bathroom door shall have mortise type latch with "vacant" indicator. Bonded store door shall have padlock made of brass.

Weather deck steel doors shall have latch， padlock or cylinder lock where necessary.

General Anti-pirate locking device to be provided for all external doors.

Locking device only openable from inside shall be fitted at steel doors to accommodation area and engine room area from upper deck as per ISPS.

##### 3.3.2.3.2 Key

Three (3) sets of key shall be supplied for each lock set except "vacant" lock.

Keys shall be divided into user’s group in accordance with shipboard practice.

Key of each door to be different, doors of one room to use the same key.

Three (3) sets of master key shall be provided.

All keys shall be supplied with a plastic identification tag. A list of keys identifying the cabin and number shall be supplied by the Builder.

The tag shall be marked in English only.

##### 3.3.2.3.3 Door Closer

Door self-closing device shall be provided for the following locations except steel doors :

* + - * Engine room entrance
      * Stairway
      * Electric cable trunk, A.C. ventilation trunk and pipe tunnel in accommodation block
      * Public toilet
      * Inside passage entrance door on upper deck, A deck and B deck
      * Engine control room
      * Galley
      * Wheel house
      * A-class, B-class fire doors (if required by Class rules)

Door closers shall be of sufficient size to close the doors under all conditions of list and trim.

### 3.3.3 STAIRWAY AND STORM RAIL IN ACCOMMODATION QUARTER

##### 3.3.3.1 Stairway Dimension and Material

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Clear Breadth | 800mm |
| Inclination | Approx.45° ~ 50°to horizontal |
| Side frame | Steel, painted |
| Step | Steel, covered with 2mmthick vinyl sheet |
| Step guard (non-slip) | Copper |
| Hand rail | Stainless steel pipe about Φ42 |
| Stanchion | Stainless steel pipe about Φ20 |

##### 3.3.3.2 Storm Rail

Stainless steel (SUS 304) storm rail shall be provided at one side of the corridor at 1.0 m height above deck in accommodation quarter and front of wheelhouse according to the Builder’s practice.

## 3.4 FURNITURE AND UPHOLSTERY

### 3.4.1 FURNITURE

#### 3.4.1.1 General

The furniture and fittings shall be of strong construction for shipboard using and in harmony with decorative treatment of the space and shall be in accordance with the Builder’s practice.

Main furniture and fittings shall be as described in detail and the size and number of furniture may be slightly changed by the Cabin Arrangement Plan.

***All beds shall be arranged in direction of longitudinal and sofas in private rooms shall be arranged in direction of transverse as far as possible. If not they must be in opposite direction.***

***In Cabins and Public areas where entertainment appliances are provided must be supplied from individual power socket. An Extra power socket should also be provided at each area***.

The general features and size of furniture shall be as listed up in the following. Color scheme book shall be submitted to Buyer for approval.

The surface material of furniture in general shall be as follows.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Item | Material |
| Steel | Spray paint or chromium plating |
| Wood | Polyurethane finish laminated sheets |
| Chair | Wood (Living cabin, Conference room) |
| Fixed revolving steel chair (mess room) | Steel |

In general the furniture to be constructed of the plywood/chipboard cover with decoration plate and trimmed with high quality hardwood in all cabin classes and formaldehyde level to satisfy Chinese Furniture Standard melamine film in visible part only.

Top of all tables and other horizontal top surfaces to be finished with melamine laminate.

Chairs and movable sofas shall be provided with fastening device. Other furniture shall be fixed to wall, deck and/or ceiling.

#### 3.4.1.2 Dimension of Large Furniture

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Class | Bed | Wardrobe | Desk |
| Captain | 2,000 x 1,500 | 1,200 x 600 | 2,000 x 800 |
| Senior Officer | 2,000 x 1,200 | 800 x 600 | 1,800 x 700 |
| Junior Officer | 2,000 x 1,200 | 800 x 600 | 1,400 x 700 |
| Petty officer & Rating | 2,000 x 1,100 | 800 x 600 | 1,000 x 600 |

#### 3.4.1.3 Furniture

**The list below is for information. The final amount and arrangement to be according to cabin’s arrangement which approved by buyer.**

One (1) ***full size*** mirror to be provided in the wardrobe.

***All drawers and doors of furniture’s to be fitted with snap locks. Locks shall be provided for wardrobes and the uppermost tier of drawer for desk.***

***All beds shall be provided with two (2) drawers underneath (except for bed in hospital).***

***Heavy furniture normally will be standing type. If heavy furniture only mounting on wall reinforce plate will pre install inside the lining.***

***All edges of furniture must be rounded off with no sharp edges.***

***Life jacket and immersion suit to be fitted in a dedicated shelf in wardrobe.***

***All refrigerators should be using environmentally friendly gas.***

### 3.4.2 UPHOLSTERY

#### 3.4.2.1 Surface Material of Sofa and Chair

Upholstery for sofa and chair shall be as follows:

Woven fabric - Captain class cabins, Senior officer class cabins, Recreation room

Vinyl leather: Other cabins and other public spaces.

#### 3.4.2.2 Stuffing of Sofa, Chair and Mattress

Upholstery of mattress: Cotton cloth

Stuffing of mattress: Polyurethane sponge with coil spring

Stuffing of sofa and chair: Polyurethane sponge

#### 3.4.2.3 Curtain

|  |  |
| --- | --- |

## 3.6 STORE

### 3.6.1 REFRIGERATED PROVISION STORE

#### 3.6.1.1 General

Cold rooms to be equipped with lockable quarantine shelves or lockers.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Temperature (0C) | Volume (m3) |
| Lobby | No cooling | abt. 10 |
| Dry provision | Cooled by A/C | abt. 20 |
| Vegetable room | +4 | abt. 20 |
| Meat room | –18 | abt. 15 |
| Fish room | –18 | abt. 7 |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| L. T. cooling F.W. temperature | 36oC |
| Ambient temperature | 35oC |

Measurement of volume shall be taken to the inner surface of insulation and lining.

Volume of each compartment may be adjusted in accordance with detail design of the accommodation arrangement.

***In general, finished ceiling height of compartments shall be not less than 1.9 meters.***

#### 3.6.1.2 Insulation

Insulation for refrigerated store:

Side : 120 mm thick polyurethane foam(PUF)

Top : 120 mm thick PUF

Partition : 120 mm thick PUF

Bottom : 120 mm thick PUF + 12 mm thick plywood + 1.0 mm thick stainless steel plate

The polyurethane foam panel shall be coated with 0.6mm thick stainless steel sheet for visible parts and 0.6 mm thick galvanized steel sheet for invisible parts.

#### 3.6.1.3 Door

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Door type | : | Air-tight pontoon, hinged type. |
| Material | : | Stainless steel filled with PUF insulation. |
| Dimensions | : | Abt. 750mmx 1,700mm |

Necessary door fittings such as locking device, open able and unlocking device from inside and door holder, etc. shall be provided.

#### 3.6.1.4 Furnishing

Meat, fish and vegetable room shall be fitted with 2-tier shelves made of stainless steel.

Thermal expansion valve control panel shall be fitted near the chamber.

A remote reading thermometer shall be fitted for each room and an indicator shall be mounted in the passage in vicinity of the lobby. One (1) ozone generator shall be provided in vegetable room.

Alarm bell shall be fitted in galley with signal light outside the compartment and push button arranged in each chamber and lobby. Other details refer to "- Electric Part".

A meat chopping block and a sink with fresh hot and potable water supply shall be provided in lobby.

Plastic gratings shall be fitted on the floor.

Water seal scupper shall be provided for each compartment.

#### 3.6.1.5 Refrigerating Plant

The refrigerating system shall be of refrigerant R-407Cdirect expansion with automatic control device.

Two(2) sets of condensing unit shall be arranged in Air conditioning unit room(one as stand-by) and each unit shall be consisted of compressor and condenser and necessary accessories as per Maker’s standard.

Cooling water shall be supplied by low temperature cooling F.W. system in engine room.

The refrigerating plant shall be capable to maintain the specified temperatures with one(1) compressor working at full load not more than 16 hours per day. The other compressor shall serve as standby. Cooling down to specified temperatures shall be worked by two compressors. Ambient temperature of atmosphere shall be based on 35C and cooling water temperature of 36C. Compressors shall be automatically started and stopped to maintain the specified temperatures.

Each compartment shall be cooled by one (1) ceiling unit cooler. Diffuser shall consist of an aluminum fin cooling coil and an electric fan contained in an enameled metal case. Drain pan shall be fitted and drain pipe shall be led to the scupper in the chamber.

Unit cooler, drain pan and pipe shall be equipped with electric heating coils for defrosting (auto operation) for meat room and fish room.

Thermostat, pressure gauges, remote reading thermometers, necessary valves and safety valves, sight glass, and gas charging device, etc., shall be fitted completely.

De-frosting of diffusers shall be provided for meat room and fish room with electric heater with time controller.

Materials for compressors and condensers, etc. shall be in accordance with Maker's standard.
