## 5.2 FIRE FIGHTING SYSTEM

### 5.2.1 GENERAL

The following fixed fire-fighting systems shall be provided for the spaces as listed below.

Sea water system Exposed decks, Engine room, Steering gear room, Cargo hold, Paint store

Living quarters, and other working spaces

Fixed fresh water mist system Localized fire suppression in E/R

CO2 fixed system Engine room, Cargo hold, Galley hood

Portable fire extinguisher Living quarters and other working spaces, engine room, emergency generator room and emergency fire pump room

All fire-fighting system and equipment shall comply with the requirements of SOLAS.

Fire Control Plan shall be provided in accordance with Rule and Regulation and shall be stored in galvanized steel case on both sides of living quarters on upper deck.

Fire control station is shall be provided with controls for quick closing valves, E/R fans, CO2 releasing box for engine room, oil pumps etc.

***One fire detector for every laundry.***

### 5.2.2 SEA WATER FIRE FIGHTING SYSTEM

#### 5.2.2.1 Fire Main Line

Fire main line water would supplied from two (2) sets of the fire, bilge & G.S. pumps in E/R, and an emergency fire pump. The fire main line and brand line shall be led along the void and connected to fire hydrants on open deck.

Start/stop of the fire, bilge & general service pump shall be done remotely from engine control room, ship office, fire station, wheelhouse (only for fire & general service pump) and locally at pump side in accordance with rule requirement.

One (1) isolation valve with a pressure gauge shall be provided on the fire main. The pressure of fire main shall be indicated in the ECR in addition to the local one**.**

Sufficient number of drain cock shall be provided for fire main line to release the remaining water for anti-freezing use.

The system also shall be used for washing decks and for other purpose as follows:

1) For washing chain, nozzles shall be provided in each hawse pipe with one stop valve.

2) Power water for bilge eductor of chain locker & bosun store.

3） Power water for dangerous goods bilge eductor.

4） Power water for ballast stripping eductor.

5) Cooling for Windlass and mooring winch hydraulic unit

Two (2) sets of mobile water monitor with a dual-purpose spray/jet type nozzle shall be provided, and the minimum capacity of the monitor shall be 60 m3/h, at the pressure required by SOLAS regulation II-2/10.7.3, and in compliance with IMO Res.MSC.365(93) requirements.

For open deck containers, water mist lance as required by MSC.365 (93) to be provided.

#### 5.2.2.2 Fire Hydrant and Hose Rack/Box

Fire hydrant shall be so arranged that the jets of water may reach any part of the ship and any part of an empty cargo space, furthermore, such hydrants shall be positioned near the accesses to the protected spaces.

The nominal diameter of fire hydrant shall be DN50 mm for all areas.

Two (2) international shore connections shall be provided adjacent to the living quarters.

The fire hydrant shall be manually operated valve with hose coupling of brass.

Each fire hose outside machinery space shall be 18 m length complete with a coupling and a combined jet/water fog nozzle, which shall be stowed in steel cabinet for weather & outside of living quarters and fiberglass cabinet in the other enclosed spaces. In machinery space, the fire hose shall be 15m length.

Fire hydrants line and the hose racks/boxes shall be painted in red.

#### 5.2.2.3 Emergency Fire Pump

An electric motor driven emergency fire pump shall be installed in bow thruster & emergency fire pump room.

The electric power for emergency fire pump shall be served from the emergency switchboard.

The pump should be able to draw water and build up design pressure at ship ballast condition.

The pump shall be self-priming centrifugal type. For material of pump, refer to Machinery Chapter of the specification.

The emergency fire pump shall have independent sea chest and discharge to fire main line through non-return stop valve.

The emergency sea chest shall be below the waterline of lightest ballast condition.

#### 5.2.2.4 Sprinkling Water System for Paint Store and Garbage Store

The spraying sea water for the paint store and garbage store shall be supplied from fire main line and capable of being operating from outside as per Rule/Regulations.

Smoke detector shall be provided in the paint store as per Rule/Regulations.

#### 5.2.2.5 Water mist fire fighting system in E/R

Refer to “Chapter 6-Machinery, 6.11.8.2.2”.

### 5.2.3 CO2 FIRE EXTINGUISHING SYSTEM

A total flooding CO2 Fire Extinguishing system shall be provided for the engine room, cargo holds etc. in accordance with the requirements of the Rule and SOLAS.

CO2 bottle each containing 45 kg of CO2 shall be arranged in CO2 room.

CO2 fire extinguishing system should be designed that the releasing of CO2 bottles can be carried out by remote control method in fire control station for engine room, and in CO2 room for cargo hold and in accordance with MSC.339 (91) requirements. Manual or group release in CO2 room for cargo hold shall be in accordance with Class requirement.

The remote control system shall be interlock with audible and visual alarm.

CO2 line shall be led from CO2 bottles to each cargo hold and via 2-way valve on discharge line and solenoid valve on smoke suction line in CO2 room, which can be operated remotely from fire control station.

The engine room fans shall be stopped automatically by means of a limit switch in the release cabinet.

Adequate number of CO2 discharge nozzles shall be so arranged on the branch lines that CO2 gas may be efficiently discharged into cargo holds and engine room.

CO2 gas smoke suction line and discharge manifold shall be led in under deck void to each protected container hold, and smoke tubes shall be led to the detecting cabinet in the CO2 room.

Necessary accessories shall be provided in accordance with the requirements of Regulations and manufacturer’s standards.

An electric horn (Explosion-proof type when carry dangerous goods) shall be provided in each cargo hold for alarming CO2 discharge.

One (1) CO2 bottle with manual releasing valve shall be fitted in the gallery and releasing nozzles shall be connected to the exhaust duct of hood if necessary in accordance with the requirement of the SOLAS.

One (1) CO2 weighting device shall be provided and safety devices shall be provided in accordance with the requirements of Regulations and manufacturer’s standards.

Maker standard plate operation and distribution instruction (in English) for CO2 system shall be provided in CO2 room, wheelhouse and fire control station.

CO2 fire extinguishing system shall provide with compressed air connections.

CO2 gas leakage alarm shall be provided.

A smoke extraction fan unit shall be installed in the CO2 room, but the outlet of the extraction pipe shall be arranged far away from the normal crew working area.

### 5.2.4 PORTABLE FIRE EXTINGUISHER

Portable form, CO2 and/or dry power fire extinguishers shall be furnished and properly secured in accordance with the requirement of the SOLAS.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Type | Space |
| 5 kg CO2 type | Wheel house & chart space, electric equipment room, electrical workshop, galley, ER workshop, emergency generator room, engine room, air conditioning room, ship office and fire control station |
| 45L foam type | Engine room |
| 135L foam type | Engine room |
| 9L foam type or 6 kg dry powder type | Space where required by rules |

The number of portable fire extinguishers shall be decided in accordance with the rule requirement. Spare charges shall be stowed in the safety store in living quarters.

Survey card shall be fitted for each portable fire extinguisher.

### 5.2.5 FIREMAN OUTFIT

Fire-fighting apparatus shall be provided in accordance with the requirements of the Rule/Regulations as follows:

1. Two (2) sets of firefighter’s outfits including self-contained breathing apparatus in fire control station;
2. Two (2) two-way portable radiotelephone apparatus (as a headset in the mask);
3. Four (4) full protective clothing resistant to chemical attack for dangerous goods carriage;
4. Two (2) self-contained breathing apparatuses in addition to the above for dangerous goods carriage;

Heat protection suit shall be of heavy duty version with heat protection for gloves and boots and hood.

### 5.2.6 FIRE DETECTION AND ALARM SYSTEM

Indication of fire shall be provided on fire alarm panel in wheelhouse and extension alarm in fire control station in accordance with SOLAS.

***Comply with latest FSS Code. E.g Detector and Control panel are to be tested according to EN54(2001)***

Suitable numbers of fire/smoke detectors shall be provided in the machinery spaces, living quarters, alleyways, and staircase according to the requirement of the Rule/Regulations.

Smoke tube type fire detecting system shall be provided for cargo holds.

CO2 smoke suction line shall be led in each cargo hold, smoke detection with valve and suction fan shall be arranged in the CO2 bottle room, a repeater panel shall be in the wheel house.

Audible / visual alarm shall be provided according to the Rule.

Suitable numbers of push buttons shall be provided in access of every deck and passage ways and suitable spaces.

The details of the system refer to “Chapter 9 - Electric Part” of the Specification.

### 5.2.7 FIRE control STATION

A fire control station for fire-fighting system shall be arranged in living quarters.

Followings shall be controlled or stowed in:

* Emergency stop of the ventilation fans for E/R
* Emergency stop of fuel oil pumps and lubricating pumps in E/R
* Emergency quick-closing of valves on oil tanks in E/R
* Start/stop push button of the bilge, fire & G.S. pumps and emergency fire pump
* Fire alarm push button
* Fire alarm repeater panel
* Portable international shore connector
* Portable fire extinguisher as required by the Rule
* CO2 releasing box for engine room
* Auto telephone
* Others as per the Rule and Regulation

### 5.2.8 ESCAPE TRUCK FOR ENGINE ROOM

One (1) escape truck shall be provided on each floor of engine room and engine control room to a safe position outside engine room. Escape route of E/R workshop to be considered (additional one (1) if necessary)

### 5.2.9 MISCELLANEOUS

Fire-fighting equipment, such as axes, emergency escape breathing devices (EEBD), etc. shall be provided and stowed in the space in accordance with the Rules and Regulations in the Specification.

## 5.3 AIR CONDITIONING AND VENTILATION SYSTEM

### 5.3.1 AIR CONDITIONING SYSTEM

Air Conditioning System shall be provided to serve as ventilation, heating and/or cooling for all cabins, offices spaces, public spaces and hospital in this Specification.

The air condition system shall be of medium or high pressure, medium velocity, single duct system having a central heating and cooling plant.

The system shall consist of refrigerating plant and air handling unit with distribution duct.

One (1) set of water-cooled package air conditioner shall be provided for engine control room, and galley. The package air conditioners to be cooled by LT FW in the engine room.

Spot cooling shall be arranged in wheelhouse, chart room, catering space, and not be counted as air conditioned spaces with regard to temperature and relative humidity.

The fresh air shall be conditioned by air handling unit, and the conditioned air shall be supplied to the air conditioning spaces and spot air cooling/heating spaces.

The surplus air in conditioned space, except hospital, shall be exhausted into the corridor or main line pipe through the door louver and/or into the appropriate private sanitary space, if applicable, through the door gap.

The surplus air in corridor shall be exhausted naturally to weather.

No recirculation from hospital, catering space, dry provision store and sanitary space.

Diffuser shall not be located directly above bed or desk, as far as practicable.

One (1) set of portable type, refrigerant recovery unit shall be provided in accordance with Classification Society requirements.

Air intakes for accommodation ventilation shall not be situated near fuel/lube vents or be able to take in tainted air (air that smells of fuel fumes)

The doors to each cabin or wall where necessary, shall be fitted with ventilation shutter to allow exhausting air into the corridor.

1. Design condition:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Cooling | Heating |
| Outside | 35℃ 70%RH | -20℃ |
| Inside | 27℃ 50%RH | 20℃ 50%RH |
| Cooling F.W. temp | 36℃ |  |

The plant shall be designed to cool and/or heat the supply air and to maintain the above condition when the doors and windows are closed.

The fresh air ratio shall be 50% fresh air for summer and winter, and 100% fresh air for other seasons.

1. Air changing rate for air condition system

Air conditioning system shall be designed to have the following minimum air change rate based on the volume of each compartment.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Compartment | Air changes per hour | Remarks |
| Private space | 6 |  |
| Public space | 10 |  |
| Office space | 10 |  |
| Hospital | 10 |  |
| Catering space except galley | 15 | Spot A.C |
| Changing room | 6 | Spot A.C. |
| Wheelhouse/radio space/chart space | 15 | Spot A.C. |
| Dry provision store | 6 | Spot A.C. |
| Laundry | 5 | Spot A.C. |
| Bonded store | 5 | Spot A.C. |
| Elect. Equipment store | 5 | Spot A.C. |

1. Air conditioning plant

Two (2) sets of refrigerating plant, which to be R-407C direct expansion and electric motor driven, shall be installed, and each capacity shall be ***60%*** of total.

Each plant shall consist of:

One (1) – Compressor

Electric motor driven, reciprocating or scroll type with manual start/stop, automatic unloading

One (1) – Condenser

Horizontal straight shell and tube type,

One (1) - Gas dryer

Leakage detector also shall be provided.Air handling unit

One (1) set of air handling unit (100% capacity) shall be installed in air conditioning unit room.

The unit shall consist of:

One (1) - Ventilation fan

Single speed, electric motor driven, centrifugal type,

One (1) – Heating coil chamber.

One (1) - Cooling coil chamber,

One (1) - Humidifying fresh water spay nozzle for humidifying,

One (1) - Fresh air and air recirculation air mixing chamber with two (2) manual dampers,

One (1) - Removable air filter.

The accessories such as pressure gauge and thermometer shall be provided in accordance with the Maker’s standard.

Piping system

Cooling fresh water for condenser shall be supplied from the L.T. cooling fresh water system in engine room.

Temperature control system

Automatic temperature controller shall be fitted.

In summer, the supply air temperature from air handling unit shall be automatically controlled by expansion valve in AHU and compressor unloading mechanism in compressor.

In winter, steam regulating valve shall be controlled by a temperature sensor located in the main supply duct. Fresh water will be used for humidity.

In mild climates when cooling or heating is not required, the system to serve as mechanical ventilation for the accommodations, supplying fresh air only.

The temperature in each room shall be manually controlled by means of adjustment of air flow rate at each diffuser.

Ducting system

Fresh air for the air handling unit shall be drawn through the air supply head and shall be let to the central unit.

Recirculation air for the air handling unit shall be drawn through the grill provided on the wall or ceiling of the corridor space and shall be led to the air handling unit.

Air conditioning supply ducts shall be pre-insulated spiral or rectangle duct made of galvanized steel sheet.

The air conditioning supply ducts shall be carried into each room and terminated with ceiling type controllable diffuser and galvanized louvers in spot cooling spaces.

Necessary damper shall be fitted to main branches at easy accessible locations.

Non-return flaps and fire dampers shall be installed in accordance with the requirement of the rules.

Drainage of water shall be arranged from the lowest points of the ducts.

Easy access for inspection and service for fire closing and balancing dampers is to be provided.

Air supply line to hospital shall be provided with non-return damper and an individual exhaust fan.

Test and trial

The air handling unit shall be tested at the Maker's shop in accordance with the Maker's usual practice.

After the completion of air conditioning system, following tests shall be performed in accordance with Builder's practice.

1. Air volume test

2. Cooling or heating test

The air conditioning test shall be carried out as applicable in connection with testing season. When the heating or cooling is not applicable, only the running test shall be performed.

### 5.3.2 VENTILATION FOR CARGO HOLDS

For *No.1~No.*4cargo holds, when dangerous cargo to be loaded, two (2) sets of exhaust ventilation fan to be supplied. This exhaust ventilation with air change of two (2) times per hour based on empty hold for carrying dangerous cargo. The fans shall be explosion proof type.

Fans shall be vertical axial flow and single speed type. ***And fans for cargo hold shall be split type.***

The amount of fans to be according to the final design.

Remote start and stop for each fan shall be done in ship office.

One (1) hold fan monitor panel with running lamps and common buzzer for abnormal stop for cargo holds shall be provided in wheel house.

Ventilation ducts to be made of steel plate or galvanized spiral steel sheet for cargo hold.

Each ventilator shall be fitted with stainless steel wire net. Vent head shall be of mushroom ventilator type. Heights of ventilator openings above upper deck to be sufficient according to load line requirements.

The duct shall be designed to have the max. air flow of 15 m/s. The duct and vent head shall be painted same as surroundings.

### 5.3.3 VENTILATION FOR ACCOMMODATION AND OTHER SPACES

Mechanical supply and/or exhaust ventilation system shall be designed to have the following air change rate based on the volume of each compartment.

| Compartment | Supply | Exhaust |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Office space | \*1) | 10 |
| Hospital/hospital bath room | \*1) | 12 |
| Private lavatory | - | 10 |
| Public/deck toilet | - | 15 |
| Laundry | \*1) | 10 |
| Drying room | \*1) | 10 |
| Galley | AC30\*2) | 40 |
| Pantry | \*1) | 15 |
| Dry provision store | \*1) | 5 |
| CO2 room | - | 6 |
| Battery room | - | 5 |
| Paint store |  | 6 |
| Air conditioning unit room | - | 15 |
| Emergency generator room | 20(finally according the calculation) | - |
| Steering gear room combined with store space | 6 | - |
| Bow thruster and emergency fire pump room | 10(finally according the calculation) | - |
| Pipe duct in double bottom | 6 | - |

Remarks:

\*1) Conditioned air shall be supplied in accordance with the air change rate specified on 5.3.1.

\*2) Conditioned air for galley shall be supplied from the separate unit.

3) Hospital and galley shall have independently exhaust system.

4) AC: Spot A.C.

#### 5.3.3.1 Mechanical Ventilation

Ventilation Fan

Mechanical ventilating fan shall be A.C. electric motor driven, single speed, duct/axial or centrifugal type.

The electric motor for the paint store shall be of explosion proof type.

Start and stop of the fan shall be done remotely.

Materials of the fan shall be as Maker’s standard.

Mechanical ventilation duct in living quarters

Mechanical ventilation duct shall be single spiral or rectangular duct made of galvanized steel sheet.

Stainless steel canopy shall be provided over electric range in galley for exhaust. Canopy shall have stainless steel mesh and fire damper.

Ventilator shall be having stainless steel wire net grid.

The duct opening on weather side shall have a rat proof wire net, and stainless steel insert screens with steel cover.

Mechanical ventilation duct in other spaces

Gooseneck, mushroom or wall louver type ventilations shall be provided as a ventilation head on weather deck. The size and type of ventilator shall be decided in accordance with the Builder’s standard to comply with the Rules/Regulations.

Ventilators shall be of fabricated mild steel plate and painted same as surrounding. Coaming heights shall be in accordance with requirement of Rules/Regulations.

In general, trunk and duct shall be of fabricated mild steel and rectangular cross-section type and painted same as surrounding. Small duct shall be galvanized steel plate and rectangular or circle cross-section type as per practice.

Engine room ventilation shall be described in “Part VII- Machinery Part”.

#### 5.3.3.2 Natural Ventilation

The space which has no mechanical ventilation system shall be naturally ventilated through suitable mushroom ventilators, wall ventilators, and gooseneck ventilators or door louvers.

Natural ventilator heads leading to the stores and accommodation spaces shall be fitted with stainless steel rat-proof nets and those leading to living quarters shall be fitted with stainless steel wire net insect screen.

Natural ventilators shall be fitted with hinged type weather-tight closing device if required by the Rule.

Coaming height of ventilators shall be in compliance with Rule requirements and Builder’s practice.

# CHAPTER 6 MACHINERY

## 6.1 GENERAL

### 6.1.1 GENERAL

The vessel shall be designed and constructed as a single screw driven by a diesel engine located aft and in compliance with the requirements of Classification notation.

The propelling machinery shall consist of a low speed, direct reversible, high efficiency turbocharger engine, driving a fixed pitch propeller through a forged steel shafting.

The propeller shaft shall be turned clockwise viewed from aft of M.E. going ahead.

The central cooling F.W. system shall be provided.

The electric generating plant shall consist of three (3) sets of main diesel generators and one (1) set of emergency diesel generator.

The main engine shall be remotely controlled from the engine control room and wheelhouse and local control console and navigation bridge deck wings.

The steam generating plant shall be of one (1) set of composite boiler with exhaust gas section and oil fired section.

Open loop scrubber to be provided to satisfy the requirements of Global Sulfur Cap 2020

**An air-conditioned sound proof engine control room shall be provided in engine room and equipped with engine control device, main switchboard and other necessary monitoring equipment.**

**The ECR should have 2 Glass windows of the size 2200x600mm .**

The machinery and equipment in engine room shall be designed, constructed, installed or supplied according to the manufacturers and/or the Builder’s standard in compliance with the requirement of the Class and the Regulatory body as far as they are concerned.

**During design and construction of engine room, particular attention to be paid to ensure
that adequate space is provided for operation and maintenance of the mechanisms or
other arrangements.**

**Ensure that adequate space is provided for maintenance of the piping systems as far as
possible.**

**Eye plates to be provided for machinery equipment and pumps more than 50kg in weight.**

SI unit and bar unit to be adopted for design, construction of machinery and measuring units, such as power, pressure, temperature and flow etc.

Valves and cocks shall be according to GB, CBM, CB, JIS standard. Pipe dimension and material are of Chinese standard except those pipes/valves attached on imported equipment, which are to be Maker's standard. The connecting diameter of flange is according to ISO standard except those flanges attached on imported equipment, which are to be Maker's standard.

If there are minus differences between this Specification and actual machinery in respect of the description of machinery construction and piping systems, it to be in accordance with machinery Maker’s standard.

The materials and accessories of the machine and the equipment shall be in accordance with the requirements of Classification Society and Maker’s standard.

### 6.1.2 INSPECTION AND TEST

All inspection and tests for machinery shall be carried out in accordance with the Classification Society and Maker's inspection standard. The builder should notice the buyer, if the Buyer's representative cannot attend due to his own cause, these inspections and tests shall be entrusted to surveyor of the Classification Society and/or Builder's inspector, results of which shall be regarded as acceptance by the Buyer.

Data shall be recorded during these tests and the results shall be submitted to the Buyer. However, if the Buyer's representative cannot attend due to his own cause, these inspections and tests shall be entrusted to surveyor of the Classification Society and/or Builder's inspector, results of which shall be regarded as acceptance by the Buyer.

There will be a "items for inspection and test" document to be confirmed with Buyer in detail design stage.

**The Buyers representative will have the right to postpone any shop test if test procedures are not submitted in advance.**

#### 6.1.2.1 Main Engine Shop Test

The main engine shop test shall be performed according to the requirement of theclassification society and Maker’s standard.

The effective output of main engine shall be determined at various loads by means of hydraulic dynamometer.

Shop test shall be carried out with MDOin the presence of builder, Buyer Representation(s) and Surveyor(s) of the class.

The relevant pressure, temperature, and revolution, etc., for all test condition shall be measurement and record.

(1) Load Test

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Load | 25% | 50% | 75% | CSR | 100% | 110% |
| Hours | 1/2 | 1/2 | 1/2 | 1 | 1 | 1/2 |

(2) Governor function test at full load

(3) Fuel oil consumption measurement at all loads for reference (only CSR to be of guarantee point)

(4) Starting test and reversing test

(5) Minimum revolution test at no load (approx. 5 minutes)

(6) Astern running test at no load (min. 5 minutes)

(7) One cylinder cut off test (test load according to Maker's standard only for proto engine)

(8) Safety device confirmation before M/E shop test

(9) Overhaul inspections for necessary portions after shop test shall be carried out in accordance with Maker's usual practice and class requirement. One cylinder shall be dismantled completely for inspection.

#### 6.1.2.2 Generator Engine Shop Trial

The Generator engine shop trial will be done according to the requirement of the classification society and Maker’s standard.

The following tests shall be performed by using equipment, lubricating oil supplied by the manufacturer coupled together with the alternator.

(1) Load Test

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Load | 25% | 50% | 75% | 100% | 110% |
| Hours | 1/2 | 1/2 | 1/2 | 1 | 1/2 |

(2) Starting test at no load

(3) Emergency trip test and safety device test

(4) Governor test

(5) Fuel oil consumption measurement at 100% load

(6) Torsion vibration test recorded to be submitted for the first vessel

(7) Voltage regulation test

(8) Overhaul inspection shall be carried out in accordance with Maker's usual practice and class requirement. Overhaul of one cylinder unit per engine to be done as well as inspection of all cams and gear wheel drive.

Note: During test on board of Generator, PF (power factor) = 1.0 applied as test load.

#### 6.1.2.3 Other Aux. Machinery

The air compressors, pumps, ventilation fans, and other auxiliary machineries to be carefully tested in respect of performance and function at Maker's shop (if any) or on board in compliance with the requirement of Classification Society and Maker’s standard (if any).

For the machinery having the same capacity, performance test shall be carried out for only one set.

Above mentioned test shall be not applied to spare parts (if any), which the dimension test only shall be applied to.

### 6.1.3 FUEL OIL

HFO and LSHFO/ULSFO and MGO shall be on board as fuel.

The main engine shall be capable of burning HFO of up to viscosity of 700cSt/50˚C, max. density of 1,010kg/m3 at 15˚C, and MGO shall be used prior stopping for long time only.

The fuel oil piping system and equipment shall be designed with fuel oil viscosity of **380** cSt/50˚C.

The main generator engines shall burn HFO and LSHFO/ULSFOsame as for main engine including the running condition of start, stop, MGO will be used when the engine is expected to be inactive for a prolonged period with cold engine.

The emergency diesel generator shall be designed to burn MGO.

Same heavy fuel oil used in the main engine shall be used for oil fired section of the composite boiler, and cold starting of the boiler shall burn MGO.

However, when the ship is navigating to enter into a SOxemission control area, the burning fuel oil for engines and boiler shall be changed over to MGO or ULSFO (sulphur content 0.1 % m/m).

The change over from HFO to LSHFO/ULSFO or MGO or vice versa will be automatic type.

MGO cooler will be cooled by LT cooling fresh water.

MGO will not be purified, and MDO will be used instead of MGO for MGO system function test.

Fuel standard as follow:

HFO: ISO 8217-2017(E), Class RMK380, Viscosity is 380 cSt/50oC (Sulfur content < 3.5% m/m), density 1,010 kg/m3 at 15 oC.

MGO: ISO 8217-2017(E), Class DMZ, Viscosity is 3~6 cSt/40oC (Sulfur content <0.1% m/m)

LSHFO (Sulfur content < 0.5% m/m, viscosity 10~70 cSt/50oC) is new hybrid fuel type that don’t fit into the ISO 8217 standard, and will be based on the available specification data from the fuel supplier.

ULSFO (Sulfur content < 0.1% m/m, viscosity 10~60 cSt/50oC) is new hybrid fuel type that don’t fit into the ISO 8217 standard, and will be based on the available specification data from the fuel supplier.

### 6.1.4 DESIGN CONDITION

The main engine, generator engines and the aux. equipment including the shafting shall be so designed that the main engine is satisfactorily operated at the maximum continuous rating at sea water temperature of 32C, L.T.F.W. temperature of 36C, engine room ambient air temperature of 45C, barometric pressure of 0.1MPa and relative humidity of 60%.

The basic ideas or design condition in planning the machinery plant are to be as numerated below.

#### 6.1.4.1 Shafting and Propeller

The diameter of the shafts shall be determined by the Rule's requirements and to have margin refer to item6.2.3.

The propeller design refers to “Chapter 1 General paragraph 1.2.7.2”.

#### 6.1.4.2 Machinery Installation Aspects

The supporting chocks of main engine shall be made of epoxy chocks.

The generating engine shall be direct coupled to and mounted on a common bed with the generator. The common bed shall be resiliently mounted to ship’s structure as manufacture’s recommendation.

The steel liner or steel sheet shall be used for pumps and other aux. equipment.

#### 6.1.4.3 Electric Power

Refer to “Electric Chapter”.

#### 6.1.4.4 Steam

Necessary steam for ship's service shall be as follows.

Normal sea service Exh. gas section of the composite boiler

and oil fired section of the composite boiler if necessory.

Harbor in/out operation Oil fired section of the composite boiler

Port Oil fired section of the composite boiler

#### 6.1.4.5 Compressed Air

Two (2) main air reservoirs shall be able to start main engine consecutively at least twelve(12) times without replenishment, and total capacity of two (2) main air compressors shall be capable of recharging two (2) main air reservoirs within one (1) hour. The main air reservoir shall be also able to start generator engine normally.

One (1) aux. air reservoir for generator engines shall be provided and charged through the main air line from main air reservoir normally, while this reservoir shall be charged by the emergency air compressor which is electrically driven type in case of dead ship condition. The emergency air compressor motor shall be fed from the emergency switchboard.

#### 6.1.4.6 Heat Exchanger

(1) The coolers for main engine shall be designed on the basis of SMCR.

(2) The fouling margin for plate type cooler shall be of 10%.

1. The fouling margin for shell-tube type heat exchangers to be of 15%.

#### 6.1.4.7 Purifier

(1) For fuel oil

Two (2) self-cleaning type purifiers shall be provided for HFO/LSHFOcleaning. One (1) for working and the other as stand-by. **The purifiers can handle fuel density of 1,010 kg/m3.**

(2) For lube oil

One (1) self-cleaning type lube oil purifier shall be provided for main engine lube oil system.

One (1) self-cleaning type lube oil purifier shall be provided for generator engines.

**Lub. purifier must be possible to switch purifiers to Main Engine and Aux Engine sump.**

#### 6.1.4.8 Pump

Where two (2) pumps for M/E, G/E and boiler etc., service provided in one (1) system, one (1) shall be sufficient to handle the system and the other service as stand-by.

The specified capacity and motor output of rotary positive displacement pumps shall be designed on the basis of following viscosity.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Capacity cSt | Motor output cSt |
| Fuel oil circulating and supply pump | 25.8 | 1000 |
| HFO,LSHFO/ULSFO transfer pump | 25.8 | 1,000 |
| MGO transfer pump | 3.0 | 100 |
| Main lubricating oil pump | 25.8 | 260 |
| Lube oil transfer pump | 25.8 | 1,000 |

Neither spare propeller nor spare propeller shaft to be provided.

### 6.2.4 ELECTRIC GENERATING PLANT

(1) Generator engine

No. of set : Three (3)

Type : 4-stroke, single acting trunk piston medium speed engine

Output : As per Maker’s standard

Revolution : Max. 900 r/min

Generator : abt.1,250kWe, AC,450V, 3¢, 60 Hz (drip-proof Brushless type)

Fuel : HFO, LSHFO/ULSFO,MGO

(2) Emergency generator engine

No. of set : One (1)

Type : Four cycle, vertical, single acting, radiator cooled type diesel engine.

Output : As per Maker’s recommendation

Revolution : 1,800 r/min

Alternator : Abt.150 kWe, AC, 450V, 3¢, 60 Hz

Starting system : By battery and hydraulic or equivalent

Fuel : MGO

### 6.2.5 STEAM GENERATING PLANT

Composite boiler

No. of set : One (1)

Type : Cylindrical vertical type with pressure atomizedburner and feed water regulator (on/off control).

Evaporation

Oil fired section : Abt.1,800kg/h, final capacity to be decided acc. to steam balance.

Exhaust gas section : abt. 1,300 kg/h at CSR of M/E under ISO condition.

Steam state : 0.7 MPa (working) saturated

Feed water temperature : 80oC

Fuel : HFO, LSHFO/ULSFO,MGO

The exhaust gas section of the composite boiler also serves as M/E exhaust gas silencer and the noise attenuation shall be as per Maker’s standard.

Final capacity to be decided acc. to final selected maker’s calculation.

Control air dehydrator

### 6.2.7 COOLING WATER SYSTEM

### 6.2.9 FUEL SYSTEM

M/E & G/E F.O. supply module unit

Capacity : According to the requirement of M/E at SMCR and two(2) sets G/E at max output

Including fuel oil supply pumps, automatic filter and bypass filter (35 microns nominal), de-aeration tank, fuel oil booster pumps, steam heaters, viscometer, MGO cooler (cooled by L.T.F.W.), automatic change-over device between HFO and LSHFO/ULSFO and MGO, and other accessories, the supply/booster pumps and viscosity control to be suitable to MGO. One (1) MGO pump shall be fitted for emergency.

No. of set : One (1)

Type : M.D. screw

Capacity : 30 m3/h

Total press. : 0.4MPa

MGO transfer pump
