Abbreviations:

HC : steam heating coil

S : steam blow

I : insulated

ML : magnetic float level gauge

SP : self-powered level gauge

GL : glass level gauge

FL : float level gauge

PL : plain glass level gauge

SD : sounding pipe

HL : high level alarm

LL : low level alarm

AT : auto. temperature regulating

HT : high temperature alarm

RL : level remote measuring

HSP : High level stop

LST : Low level start

Notes:

(1) The final capacity for some pumps and aux. equipment serving M/E, G/E and boiler and so onsuch as cooling water pump, and plate cooler etc. may be adjusted after detail heat balance.

(2) The final capacity for the tanks may be adjusted after determination of hull line and position of the tank.

(3) The total pressure for screw pump and gear pump to be contained 0.05MPa suction head.

(4) AT with mark “\*” to be arranged for HFO and LSHFO/ULSFO bunker tanks within cargo hold area.

(5) The HFO tanks with mark “\*\*” to be meant the tanks to have inclined bottom.

(6) All tanks to be made of welded steel plate and well secured to the hull. Each tank shall be provided with necessary fittings such as inlet and outlet connections, drain, air vent, manhole or hand-hole, overflow, thermometer socket, steam blow-out connection, etc. all depending on the purposes for which they are intended.

(7) The M/E L.O. sump tank shall be fitted with heating coil only around the suction bell mouth.

(8) All of the oil tanks shall be provided with drip tray, as practicable.

## 6.3 MAIN ENGINE

### 6.3.1 GENERAL

The main engine shall be designed and manufactured under the license from MAN B&M.The particulars of main engine shall be as specified in Paragraph 6.2.1.

The direction of engine revolution shall be clockwise, looking from aft.

The main engine shall be remotely controlled from wheelhouse, navigation bridge deck wings and engine control room in the engine room.

The main engine shall be temporarily controlled from local operating console. The main engine output shall be valid at following conditions:

Atmospheric pressure: 0.1 MPa

Ambient temperature in E/R: 45oC

Sea water temperature: 32oC

L.T. fresh water temperature: 36oC

Relative humidity: 60%

The construction and materials of M/E shall be in accordance with Maker’s standard and to be complied with the requirement of Classification Society.

The main engine shall be completed with necessary fittings and accessories to develop the maximum continuous rating for propelling as described in Paragraph 6.3.2.

### 6.3.2 FITTINGS AND ACCESSORIES

The engine shall be completed with necessary fittings and accessories according to main engine Maker’s standard and the main body shall be included as follows:

1- Set of high efficiency exhaust turbo-charger**.**

2- Sets of electronically controlled auxiliary blowers complete with starters **for continuous running according to maker’s standard. Provide the lub. oil pump running to interlocked with the ME auxiliary blower.**

1- Set of air cooler with cleaning and drain pipes.

1- Set of turning gear with electric motor, starter and portable switch box with capture cable of 20m and pneumatic interlocking apparatus.

1- Air starting system.

1- Set of steam tracer piping for F.O. pipes on the engine.

1- Set of cleaning device for turbo charger. (According to turbo charger maker's standard)

1- Set of brackets for the engine platforms with gratings, handling and steps.

1- Set of steam connection for fire extinguish system of scavenging air space.

1- Set of pressure regulating valves for fuel oil return.

1-Set of oil mist detecting device.

1-Set of drain box for fuel oil leakage alarm

1- Set of integrated axial damper mounted at the forward end of the crankshaft

1- 2nd order moment compensator (if necessary), and the type of the compensator shall be according to the M/E maker 's standard.

1- Torsional vibration damper (if necessary subject to TV calculation and Rules)

1- Set of friction type engine stays

***1- Set of bearing wear monitoring***

***1- Set of Water in oil detection***

***1- Spare CCUs to be provided***

***1- The M/E hydraulic power lubricating oil system for FIVA and bearing lubricating system must be independent circuits and not connected to same source***

***Maker to provide data analysis support during guarantee period.***

***Turbo charger selection will be confirmed with Owner.***

ME components (rings, piston skirts, liners, exhaust valves, air cooler etc.) to be according to licensor's latest design recommendation.

***The spare of the main engine shall be according to maker standard and Class requirement.***

Revolution indicator and revolution counter (refer to Chapter 7, Automation 7.1.4.3.4)

Remark: If above fitting and accessories of main engine is not consistent with main engine standard scope range, maker standard shall prevail.

### 6.3.3 INSTALLATION

Epoxy resin chock shall be used for installation of the main engine.

## 6.4 SHAFTING AND PROPELLER

### 6.4.1 GENERAL

The shafting shall consist of one (1) intermediate shaft and one (1) propeller shaft, one (1) intermediate bearing, one (1) stern tube and sealing. The intermediate shaft shall be fitted with oil-lubricated plain bearing and propeller shaft shall be of oil-lubricated white metal bearing. Thrust shaft and thrust bearing shall be incorporated in main engine.

The shaft diameter, propeller diameter and the number of blades and other details shall be determined and designed in consideration of the main engine torsion vibration as well as hull vibration.

If the barred speed range exists in the operating speed range, the barred speed range shall be remarked on the revolution indicator. Barred speed range with automatic quick by-pass arrangement shall be allowed at nonessential range of shaft revolution.

The calculation sheets regarding the torsional vibration shall be submitted to Classification Society for approval.

The torsional vibration shall be measured during sea trial for the first vessel.

The length of propeller shaft shall be so designed that the shaft can be withdrawn and taken in from engine room side without removal of the main engine.

Spare propeller, spare propeller shaft and intermediate shaft not to be supplied.

### 6.4.2 INTERMEDIATE SHAFT

The intermediate shaft shall be made of forged high quality carbon steel with integral flanges at both ends*,* and coupled together with each shaft with parallel forged steel reamer bolts.

The shaft shall be machined all over and finished brightly in way of bearing where the diameter is increased abt.5mm. The shafting shall be electrically earthen to the hull; a shaft earthing device shall be fitted to the intermediate shaft.

### 6.4.3 PROPELLER SHAFT

The propeller shaft shall be made of forged high quality carbon steel with a solid flange coupling on fore end. The propeller shaft shall be smoothly machined all over and finished brightly in way of bearings where the diameter is increased abt. 5mm.

The after portion of the shaft shall be machined to 1/20 tap to fit the propeller hub and the end of the shaft shall be left-hand threaded to suit a propeller shaft nut.

Removal of the propeller shaft from the Vessel shall be carried out via a temporary opening cut in the shell plating when overhauling and the location shall be clearly marked. The location of temporary opening shall be given on approval drawing.

**Eye plates for lifting propeller and rudder to be fitted at stern.**

### 6.4.4 COUPLING

The diameter of the coupling bolts and the thickness of the coupling flanges of intermediate shaft and propeller shaft are to comply with the requirements of the Classification Society.

The fillet radius at the base of flanges is to comply with the requirements of the Classification Society.

### 6.4.5 INTERMEDIATE SHAFT BEARING

The intermediate shaft bearing shall be of the single oil disc type and of cast iron or cast steel pedestal, upper and lower half shells lined with white metal.

The bearing shall be provided with ample oil reservoir and cooling water jacket inside the pedestal, with end baffle to prevent loss of oil at both ends of bearing.

The bearing shall be central LT fresh-water cooled. And a bearing temperature sensor shall be provided and connected to ECR.

For checking the oil levels in the bearing housing, the bearing shall be fitted with a sounding bar.

The number of bearing may be adjusted at detail design stage as per final shaft alignment.

### 6.4.6 STERN TUBE AND STERN TUBE BEARING

#### 6.4.6.1 Stern tube assembly

The stern tube shall be of forge steel combined with steel plate tube and be secured by epoxy resin to the stern frame boss and bulkhead of the stern tube cooling water tank.

A steel plate rope guard shall be provided at the after end of the stern frame hub.

#### 6.4.6.2 Stern Tube Bearing

There are two (2) bearings in the stern tube, one at the stern frame hub and another bearing at the forward end of the stern tube.

The bearing shells shall be of cast iron lined with white metal and of oil retaining type.

The length of after stern tube bush is to comply with the requirements of Classification Society.

Two (2) temperature sensors shall be fitted on the aft. bearing to indicate the bearing temperature, one of them as stand-by.

The wear-down measuring gauge shall be provided.

The temperature sensors to be drawn out and replaced from engine room side. **Two remote reading temp. sensors for aft stern tube bearing to be installed. One of them to be as standby.**

#### 6.4.6.3 Stern Tube Seal

The oil seal assembly shall be fitted at forward end of the stern tube and the air seal assembly shall be fitted at aft end of the stern tube to prevent ingress of seawater or loss of lube oil.

Stern tube sealing shall be of non-split simplex type. The forward seal shall have two sealing rings and the aft seal shall have four sealing rings.

Net cutter shall be provided.

A split spacer ring for aft seal to be fitted for purpose of removal so that seal nest can be moved on shaft liner.

The renewing of stern tube sealing rings to be of possible without disconnecting the shafting or Propeller. The aft seal to be protected with welded type steel rope guard.

### 6.4.7 PROPELLER, FAIR WATER CAP AND PROPELLER NUT

The propeller is to be of fixed pitch, aerofoil section, right handed, nickel aluminum bronze, keyless type.

The propeller design to refer to the “Chapter 1 General paragraph 1.2.7.2”

**The surface roughness measurement and the static balancing test of the propeller to be carried out in accordance with the manufacturer's standards in compliance with the requirements of the Classification Society.**

The hub shall be bored to taper so that it may be accurately fitted to the taper end of the propeller shaft.

The propeller shall be force fitted to the propeller shaft and secured by hydraulic mounting tool and hydraulic nut with locking device.

A fair water cap of Ni-Al bronze is to be fitted over the propeller nut.

The fair water cap shall be drilled and to have connections with brass plugs for filling the void spaces with rust preventive grease.

After the propeller has been finished and inspected according to ISO 484 class 1 standard, the static balance of the propeller shall be checked.

**The shafting shall be so designed that the propeller can be dismounted without removal of the propeller shaft ,and the steering gear shall be able to turn suitable degree (with dismantle limit stopper/ram pin to release the rudder angle restriction) to enable propeller removal.**

***Propeller light running margin to 6 %.***

### 6.4.8 EARTHING DEVICE

An earthling device with shaft potential monitoring at intermediate shaft shall be provided which is capable of keeping the electrostatic voltage between crankshaft and hull below 50mV finally according to the M/E requirement.

**A digital shaft / hull mili-voltmeter with alarm connected to AMS to be provided.**

### 6.4.9 MATERIAL

#### 6.4.9.1 Shafting

Intermediate shaft Forged steel

Propeller shaft Forged steel

#### 6.4.9.2 Stern tube assembly

Stern tube assembly forge steel or/and steel plate

6.4.9.3 Bush

Bush Cast iron with white metal

The material for oil sealing device shall be viton type and accordance with the manufacturer's standard.

#### 6.4.9.4 Intermediate Shaft Bearing

Upper and lower shells Cast steel lined with white metal

Pedestal Cast iron

## 6.5 ELECTRIC GENERATOR ENGINE

### 6.5.1 GENERAL

The electric generating plant shall consist of three (3) sets of diesel generator and one (1) set of emergency diesel generator. The relevant data refer to Paragraph 7.2.3. Concerning electric alternator, refer to “Electric Part”.

Safety protecting and auto start device for three (3) main generator sets shall be installed according to the requirements of unattended machinery space. Emergency generator set shall be auto started, switched on and supply electric power in case of the power failure of main generator sets.

### 6.5.2 CONSTRUCTION FOR GENERATOR ENGINE

Generator engine

The design, construction, materials, and accessories shall be of Maker's standard in accordance with the requirements of the Classification Society.

Cooling medium shall be L.T. fresh water for cylinder jacket, cylinder cover, lubricating oil cooler and air cooler.

A governor shall be provided on the engine to regulate automatically the quantity of fuel oil supply at different loads. The governor shall be capable of holding the engine speed in accordance with requirement of Classification Society.

Emergency diesel generator engine

The design, construction, materials, and accessories are to be of Maker's standard in accordance with the requirements of the Classification Society.

The engine shall be a vertical, four cycle, single acting trunk piston, radiator-cooled marine diesel engine.

The engine shall be completed with self-contained cooling system and forced feed lubricating system.

The engine coupled with an alternator shall be installed on a common bed and resiliently mounted on the foundation as manufacture’s recommendation.

### 6.5.3 ACCESSORIES

For each main generator engine

1) Exhaust gas turbocharger as per Maker’s design 1 set

2) Air cooler (Charge air temp. to be auto-regulated if Maker can supply) 1 set

3) Governor 1

4) Fuel injection pump each 1/cyl.

5) H.T. Cool. F.W. pump (centrifugal type engine driven) 1

6) L.O. pump (gear type, engine driven) 1

7) F.O. filter 1

8) L.O. cooler 1

9) L.O. filter 1

10) L.O. pre-lubricating pump 1

11) Preheating device for the HT-circuit 1

12) Turning device according to maker's standard 1

13) Gauge board 1 set

14) Emergency stopping device 1 set

(over speed, L.O. low press., F.W. excessively high temp.)

15) Silencer 1

16) Exhaust expansion connection. 1

17)) Fuel oil leakage alarm 1

Each cylinder to be with local thermometers for exhaust gas and cooling water outlet temp as Maker’s standard.

**Turbocharger tachometer for Aux engine shall be provided in ECR.**

The other’s accessories of generator engine shall be in accordance with Maker's standard.

For emergency generator engine

All accessories and fitting shall be in accordance with Maker's standard.

## 6.6 STEAM GENERATING PLANT

### 6.6.1 GENERAL

The steam generating plant shall consist of one (1) composite boiler with oil fired section and exhaust gas section utilizing the heat of main engine exhaust gas. The exhaust gas section of the composite boiler shall act as main engine exhaust silencer and the noise attenuation shall be as per Maker’s standard.

The composite boiler shall be vertical cylinder welded construction smoke/water tube boiler.

The normal necessary steam at sea shall be generated by the exhaust gas section of the composite boiler, utilizing the exhaust gas heat of the main engine at CSR .

The construction of the composite boiler shall be in accordance with Maker’s standard and having adequate access for cleaning and inspection.

The fuel oil burning equipment and feed water regulating (on/off control) of the composite boiler shall be provided and operated automatically.

The exhaust gas section of the composite boiler shall be capable of dry-running in emergency condition in accordance with Maker’s recommendation.

The simultaneous operation of the oil fired section and exhaust gas section of the composite boiler shall be made when the vessel is operated in the lower temperature area or reduced power operation of the main engine.

Excess steam shall be led to the atmospheric condenser via a dump (F.W. cooled).

***Steam production by exhaust gas side of the composite boiler to be measured during sea trials.***

***Exhaust gas side of the composite boiler to be fitted with in and out thermometers and a gauge to measure the pressure drop across.***

***Boiler Hot well must be equipped with Oil monitor and salinity monitors as standard.***

***Boiler must also be able to operate on MGO EU directive 2005/53/EC.***

### 6.6.2 ACCESSORIES

The composite boiler shall be accordingly supplied with burner, boiler control panel, feed water regulator, water level gauge, safety valves, other valves and pressure gauges.

All accessories and fittings will be in accordance with Maker’s standard and requirement of Classification Society.

Chemical dosing unit, boiler water testing kit for measuring PH-value, oil detecting device and salinityalarm device shall be provided.

The feed water pumps and fuel oil supply pumps shall be provided in accordance with the Maker’s recommendation.Fresh water hose connection shall be provided adjacent to the composite boiler for water washing.

### 6.6.3 Materials

In accordance with manufacturer’s standard.

## 6.7 AUXILIARY MACHINERY

### 6.7.1 PUMPS

The relevant data of the pumps refer to 6.2.

Pump construction, material, accessories, spares and tools shall be in accordance with Maker's standard and in compliance with requirements of Classification Society.

The construction, materials and accessories for pumps being attached to other machinery such as generator engine, fresh water generator, etc. shall be in accordance with Maker's standard practice.

Positive displacement pumps are to have relief valves.

In generally, pump's motor shall be located above the lower floor plate; pumps shall be accessible for easy maintenance. Lifting eyes to be provided for above major pumps.

Horizontal pumps shall be mounted on common bed plates of fabricated steel or cast iron with the driving motor.

**Main L.O. pumps to be fitted with submerged bearings.**

#### 6.7.1.1 Centrifugal Pumps

##### 6.7.1.1.1 General

Electric motor of centrifugal pump shall not be overloaded at the service condition on board.

The pump casing shall be designed that the rotating member may be exposed for inspection or replacement without disturbing the pipe connections except the small pump with capacity less than 100 m3/h.

The shaft seal for main L.O. pump shall be in accordance with Maker’s standard.

All vertical pumps shall be driven through flexible coupling between impeller and motor shaft, or may have the thrust bearing in the driving motor and shall be driven through rigid coupling.

**Bottom bearing of vertical pumps, if provided, to be of internal water sleeve type**

**Shaft gland packings as per maker’s standard.**

**Each pump to be provided with suction and discharge valves except deep well pumps.**

Centrifugal pumps to be fittedwith mechanical seal except for deep well pumps which are fitted with sealing according to manufacturer’s standard. **Centrifugal pumps (Fire, bilge &G.S. pump, Ballast pump, clean drain tank pump, Emergency Fire Pump) to be fitted with vacuum pump for self- priming.**

***All seals to be Mechanical Seals unless specifically agreed by owners. Spare Mechanical seals to be provided for each type pump.***

***Motors of all pumps to be more requirement of the maximum rating of the pumps.***

##### 6.7.1.1.2 Materials

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Material | S.W. & bilge | F.W. | Boiler water feed |
| Casing | Bronze or Bronze alloy | Cast iron | Maker’s standard |
| Casing ring | Bronze or Bronze alloy | Bronze or  Bronze alloy | Maker’s standard |
| Impeller | bronze alloy for SW, bronze or bronze alloy for bilge | Bronze or Bronze alloy | Maker’s standard |
| Shaft | Stainless steel | Stainless steel | Maker’s standard |

#### 6.7.1.2 Gear and Screw Pump

##### 6.7.1.2.1 General

Gear and screws shall be accurately machined and thoroughly cleaned.

Each pump shall be directly coupled to a power end of driver via flexible or rigid coupling according to the Maker's standard.

Gear and screw pumps to develop rated capacity against rated discharge pressure without over loading of driving motors when handling with viscosity for which the pump is intended.

The safety valve shall be fitted on the pump casing.

In general, pumps shall be internally lubricated by the pumping fluid.

##### 6.7.1.2.2 Materials

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Material | Gear pump | Screw pump |
| Casing | Cast iron | Cast iron or steel plate |
| Gear | Carbon steel | - |
| Shaft | Carbon steel | - |
| Power rotor | - | Carbon steel |
| Idle rotor | - | Carbon steel or ductile cast iron |
| Gland seal | Mechanical seal | Mechanical seal |

#### 6.7.1.3 Piston Pump, Snake Pump and Membrane Pump

Construction and material shall be accordance with Maker's standard.

### 6.7.2 HEAT EXCHANGERS

The relevant data refer to 6.2.

The construction, materials and accessories for heat exchangers being attached to other machinery such as generator engine, fresh water generator, etc. shall be in accordance with Maker's standard practice.

**Sacrificial flange or pipe to be provided for central coolers and sea water pumps.**

**Pipes shall be so arranged that the heat exchangers can be overhauled with the min. removal of the connected pipes.**

#### 6.7.2.1 Plate Type Coolers

##### 6.7.2.1.1 General

The heat-exchanging surface shall consist of some of corrugated plates clamped together in a frame and sealed at edges by rubber gaskets.

The plates form a closed system of parallel two media between which heat is exchanged flow through alternate interpolate spaces.

**Heat exchangers shall generally be provided with glass tube thermometers and manometers at inlet and at outlet of both fluids, air vent cocks, drain cocks.**

The accessories shall be in accordance with Maker’s standard.

##### 6.7.2.1.2 Materials

Frame Mild steel,

Plate Titanium (For S.W.)

Stainless steel SUS316 or equivalent (For F.W. & oil)

Gasket Maker’s standard

#### 6.7.2.2 Shell Tube Type Coolers

##### 6.7.2.2.1 General

The tubes shall be expanded into the plates at both ends of the tubes. Tube bundle to be removable.

The cooling fluid shall pass through the tubes and the cooled fluid to flow outside of the tubes.

Each heat exchanger shall be provided with a relief valve (oil heater and fresh water heater) vent valve, drain valve, pressure gauge, thermometer, and protective anode according to its service.

One (1) soda cock and one (1) boiling steam valve to be provided as common use for shell and tube type coolers and connecting seats with blind flanges for soda cock and boiling steam valve to be fitted on each tubular cooler.

**Tubular type coolers shall be of such design which will relieve stresses due to restriction of thermal expansion on the shell side. Tubes are to be expanded into the tube at both ends of the tubes.**

##### 6.7.2.2.2 Materials

Tube Aluminum brass

Tube plate Naval brass

Shell Steel plate or steel pipe

Water box and cover Steel plate or cast iron with tar epoxy coating.

#### 6.7.2.3 Heaters

Each heater shall be designed for the following conditions to heat oil or water required for each service intended:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Item | Heating steam  Pressure (MPa) | Fluid temp (oC) | |
| Inlet | Outlet |
| Heavy Fuel oil heater for M/E & G/E | 0.7 | 90 | 150 |
| Heavy Fuel oil heater for purifier | 0.7 | 50 | 98 |
| Lub. oil heater for purifier | 0.7 | 40 | 90 |
| Calorifier | Steam & electric | 10 | 70 |
| M/E jacket F.W. pre-heater | 0.7 | 15 | 50 |

Heavy Fuel oil heater for boiler shall be according to maker’s standard.

The oil heaters should attach temperature gauge and safety valve.

**Pre-heater pump shall automatically stop when ME is started,the steam of the pre-heater to be manual control**

### 6.7.3 AIR COMPRESSOR AND AIR RESERVOIR

The air compressor and air reservoir are to be of sufficient capacity to meet the requirement of the Classification Society.

The construction, materials, accessories, spares and tools shall be in accordance with Maker's standard.

#### 6.7.3.1 Main air Compressor

The main air compressors shall be of single acting, two or three stages, fresh water cooled and piston type and shall be driven by electric motors.

Each main air compressor shall be fitted with unloaded, safety valve, air strainer, pressure gauge, fresh water cooler, drain cock and other necessary fittings. Each main compressor shall be provided with automatic and remote starting and stopping device and local manual controller.

**Low lub oil Pressure and Compressed air high temperature safety shall be provided as per maker’s standard.**

#### 6.7.3.2 Service Air Compressor

The air compressor to be of screw type, electric motor driven, air cooled, self-contained L.O. system, oil filter and oil separator.

Material, spares and tools to be in accordance with the manufacturer’s standard.

#### 6.7.3.3 Emergency Air Compressor

The emergency air compressor shall be of electric motor driven, air-cooled type and used for charging to the aux. air reservoir and starting the “dead ship”.

#### 6.7.3.4 Air Reservoir

The air reservoirs shall be of cylindrical type of welded steel plate, and complete with pressure gauge, safety valve, and drain connection. The main air reservoirs shall be fitted with manual drain valve and manhole.

The air reservoir drain connection shall be with double shut drain valves. Outlet of all safety valves for main air reservoir should be connected to open deck.

The air reservoirs shall be painted inside with anti-rusting.

The air reservoirs have ample construction and hydraulic test shall be in compliance with the requirement of Classification Society.

### 6.7.4 OIL PURIFIER

All purifier heaters will be as per maker’s standard.

**A working bench with two (2) wash basins (sinks) shall be provided in the purifier room if space available. Drains from each wash basin shall be led to the sludge tank.**

#### 6.7.4.1 Fuel Oil Purifier

Two (2) sets of HFO/LSHFO/ULSFO purifier shall be used for HFO/LSHFO/ULSFO, and arranged in the purifier area in engine room.

**FO purifiers to be provided with flexible feed and discharge lines. Flexible mounting(rubber cushions) to be provided for the FO purifiers. Heater unit for the purifiers to besteam supplied, equipped with steam trap, insulation, temperature gauges etc.**

**Each FO purifier shall be equipped with water monitoring system & sludge space monitoring system.**

One (1) purifier shall be running and the other as stand-by.

The independent supply pump with driving motor shall be provided for each purifier. **The heaters of two FO purifiers to be fully interchangeable.**

Materials and accessories shall be provided according to Maker's standard.

Each purifier shall be provided with necessary fittings such as a pressure gauge, a thermometer, abnormal flow detector, oil feed shut off valve, water transducer and etc.

Each fuel oil purifier shall run continuously and sludge discharge shall be carried out automatically by means of a timer and water transducer. Start and stop of the purifiers shall be manually and locally effected.

**Automatic control panel to be provided for each FO purifier.**

Each one (1) automatic control board with abnormal alarm shall be arranged near the purifiers.

One (1) “I” beam shall be fitted above all the purifiers for maintenance.

One (1)-cleaning table shall be provided with cold water, hot water, MGO pipes and valves and drain valve.

#### 6.7.4.2 Lubricating Oil Purifier

One (1) set of M/E L.O. purifier and one (1) set of G/E L.O. purifier shall be arranged in the purifier area in the engine room. G/E LO purifier shall be also as standby for ME

Each L.O. purifier shall be with independent supply pump.

Materials and accessories shall be provided according to Maker's standard.

Each purifier shall be provided with necessary fittings such as a flow indicator, pressure gauge, thermometer, abnormal flow detector, oil feed shut off valve and etc.

The purifier shall be run continuously and sludge discharge shall be carried out automatically by means of a timer. Start and stop of the purifier shall be manually and locally effected.

Each one (1) automatic control board with timer and an abnormal alarm shall be arranged near the purifier.

“I” beam reference with 6.7.4.1

### 6.7.5 FRESH WATER GENERATOR

The vacuum type fresh water generator, utilizing the waste heat of M/E jacket cooling F.W. shall be installed in engine room and shall be cooled by sea water.

The generator to be of plate type with titanium plates.

The fresh water generator shall produce rated capacity of fresh water not exceeding 10p.p.m. of salinity at rated vacuum and main engine jacket cooling F.W. temperature of 85C and cooling sea water temperature of 32C.

The fresh water generator shall consist of an evaporator, a condenser and complete with water ejector, ejector pump, distillate pump, salinity indicator, automatic alarm, water meter and other necessaries for operation.

Fresh water with high salinity shall be automatically discharged back to the fresh water generator or bilge.

A chemical injection system included dosage tank shall be provided.

**Main Engine to be tested during sea trial for one(1) hour without operation of fresh water generator in order to confirm that the jacket cooler capacity is sufficient for dissipating of main engine heat produced.**

The materials shall comply with the requirements of the Classification Society and Maker's standard.

### 6.7.6 ENGINE ROOM VENTILATING FANS

The relevant data refer to Paragraph 6.2.15.

Four (4) ventilating fans shall be provided the airflow for combustion of main engine, generator engines, boiler and for evacuation of heat emission from aux. equipment in engine room. The ventilating fan shall be vertical split type totally enclosed motor driven axial flow type.

Two (2) sets of them shall be reversible and the capacity and head is reduced when the fan shall be run at reverse rotation. **Safety timer to be provided to prevent immediate reversal of fan.**

The materials shall be as follows:

Casing : hot galvanized steel

Impeller : sea water resistant aluminum alloy casting or Maker’s standard

Shaft : Carbon steel

In addition to above, each one (1) exhaust fan for purifier area, and welding space in ER workshop shall be installed.

### 6.7.7 OILY BILGE SEPARATOR

Oily bilge separator shall be provided for handling the oily bilge water in engine room.

The performance is to meet the requirements of MARPOL & IMO MEPC 107 (49). The oil content of treated water shall be less than 15 ppm and oil content bilge alarm shall be provided. And T-valve with automatic function shall be used for return water to bilge water holding tank.

The construction, materials, accessories, spares and tools shall be in accordance with Maker's standard.

An oil content discharge monitoring shall be installed at outlet of clean bilge discharge pump.

***Give the capacity of treating the oil in water in the Oil water separator technical agreement.***

### 6.7.8 SEWAGE TREATMENT PLANT

One (1) sewage treatment plant of biological type shall be provided in engine room.

The construction, materials, accessories, spares and tools shall be in accordance with Maker's standard.

Soil pipe from hospital block shall be separately led to the sewage treatment plant.

One (1) set of unit type toilet shall be provided in engine room and sewage shall lead to the sewage collecting tank by gravity.

The performance shall meet the requirement of IMO.

**The grey and black water pipes should be sufficient inclined downwards for easy draining of water. Furthermore, horizontal led drain pipes should be avoided. Suitable access openings with blind flanges for cleaning, to be arranged as far as possible.**

**The plant to be provided *two* air blower(or air compressor) and an alternative air at 7kg/cm2 .**

### 6.7.9 INCINERATOR

The incinerator shall be in compliance with the requirements of MARPOL 73/78 Annex VI and MEPC 76 (40) and alarms for furnace high temperature, flue high temperature, initiation failure, blanking failure and low fuel oil pressure etc.

The incinerator shall be capable of burning solid waste and waste oil.

Exhaust pipe for incinerator shall be provided with suitable expansion joints.

The following accessories to be included:

Burner unit 1 set

Sludge oil circulating pump 1 set

Diesel oil pump 1 set

Sludge oil tank 1 set

Flue gas fan 1set

Flue gas damper 1 set

Other necessary accessories, fittings, spares and tools shall be according to Maker's standard.

## 6.8 MISCELLANEOUS EQUIPMENT AND OUTFITTING

Miscellaneous equipment and outfitting such as tanks, ventilating duct, ladders, floor plates, etc. shall be constructed and furnished in accordance with Builder's standard practice and shall be comply with the requirements of the Classification Society.

### 6.8.1 OVERHAULING AND REMOVAL OF MACHINERY

Overhauling equipment for main engine and auxiliary machinery shall be provided as mentioned below.

During designing and construction of the engine room, particular attention shall be paid to ensure sufficient space for operation and dismantling of machinery and equipment.

#### 6.8.1.1 Overhauling Crane of Main Engine

For overhauling cylinder piston and liner etc. of main engine, there is a crane on the overhead-lifting beam.

The crane shall be of marine trolley type with electric motor driven two speeds for hoisting, and single speed for traveling and traversing. The construction and materials shall be in accordance with Maker's standard.

The capacity of the engine room overhead crane is to be at least 4.0 t ***and can be hoist the heavisest spare part of the main engine.***

**Overhead lifting beam shall be securely supported to ship's structure and to extend the full length of the main engine**.

Lifting eyes or I-beam shall be provided for overhaul T/C of main engine in case E.R. crane can’t be utilized for overhauling.

**Facilities to be provided to visit the engine room crane if it stops at any position of its travel.**

**Source cable layout to be of a suspension type and long enough to reach the lower floor.**

**A cargo light to be fitted on the top of the overhead crane beam.**

#### 6.8.1.2 Shafting Removal

**One (1) lifting beam with two (2) trolley hooks of adequate capacity to hoist the propeller shaft (+25% margin) to be provided above the propeller shaft if the lifting beam installation available. If enable, builder provided eye plate with chain block.**

Necessary lifting eye plates shall be fitted above the shafting alley for lifting of the intermediate shaft and withdrawing the propeller shaft inboard. Removal of propeller shaft from the vessel shall be carried out via a temporary opening out in the shell plating which shall be marked by welding bead in approved colored scheme. Equipment and pipes arranged at that place shall be easily dismantled.

#### 6.8.1.3 Overhauling of Auxiliaries

Generator engines shall have adequately strength lifting beam to facilitate overhaul.

**Provided for the generator engines to be of sufficient capacity to hoist the alternator’s rotor.**

Lifting beam : 3 sets

Chain block with roller : 3 sets, manual type

Capacity : according to the generator Maker’s recommendation.

Oil purifiers shall have lifting beam using chain blocks to facilitate overhaul.

Lifting beam : 1 set

Chain block with roller : 1 set, manual type

Capacity : 1.0t

A lifting beam shall be provided for transport of the heavy parts from engine room to workshop.

Lifting beam : 1 set

Chain block with roller : 1 set, manual type

Capacity : 2.0 t

Other larger aux. equipment above shall have eye plates to facilitate overhaul.

#### 6.8.1.4 Heavy Element in/out Engine Room

Spare gears, tools and other machine parts and big strainers shall be carried in/out of engine room through the hatch on deck.

**A lifting beam shall be provided for transport of the heavy parts from spare landing hatch to workshop and E/R store shop.**

**One trolley to be provided to transport heaviest engine spare like liner.**

Lifting arrangements and transport ways from exposed deck to bottom floor in engine room shall ensure easy transport of heavy elements by or harbor crane.

**Lifting eyes to be provided for pieces of machinery weighting more than 50kg.**

**Lifting eyes with chain block to be provided for main SW filter.**

**Lifting beam to be provided for oil purifier to facilitate overhauling.**

### 6.8.2 TANKS IN ENGINE ROOM

Tanks in engine room shall be of welded steel plate, and provided with necessary fittings such as heating coils, thermal insulation, level measuring apparatus, thermometer socket, air escape pipe, overflow pipe, drain plug, hole for cleaning, valves, etc., to be according to tank purpose.

All of the oil tanks shall be provided with drip pans as practicable. Heating coils shall be provided for the following tanks:

Tank name Heating coil surface ratio

HFO, ULSFO/LSHFO settling tank 0.2m2/m3

HFO, ULSFO/LSHFO service tank 0.2m2/m3

M/E LO settling tank 0.1m2/m3

M/E LO sump tank around bell mouth

Fuel oil drain tank 0.1m2/m3

Sludge tank 0.25m2/m3

Fuel oil overflow tank 0.08m2/m3

G/E lub. oil settling tank 0.1m2/m3

Lub. oil drain tank 0.1m2/m3

Bilge tank 0.1 m2/m3

### 6.8.3 VENTILATING OF MACHINERY SPACE

The ventilating ducts shall be so arranged that air can be supplied to engine room where necessary such as for main engine, generator engines, composite boiler, workshop store and working space etc. All ducts shall be of steel plate or galvanized steel sheet.

Total capacity of ER supply fan shall be calculated according to “ISO8861Shipbuilding-Engine room ventilation in diesel engine ships – Design requirement and basis of calculation (1998(E)).

The ventilating ducts shall be of rectangular cross section and made with flange or welding sleeve connection to allow replacement for repair.

In general, min. height at main passage beneath the air duct shall be 2.0m (as far as possible). The thickness of ventilating duct shall be as follows:

The biggest side ≥800mm to be made of steel plate Q235-B, about 5.0mm thick;

600 mm ≤the biggest side< 800mm to be made of steel plate Q235-B, about 3.0mm thick; The biggest side < 600mm to be of 1.0mm galv. steel plate.

**The inside of main duct (not include galv. steel plate) to be painted with epoxy paint.**.

The air ducts shall be provided with adjustable dampers where necessary for proper ventilation keeping healthy conditions and even temperature distribution within the machinery space.

**Pneumatically controller fire dampers or ventilation inlet to be provided for engine room supply fans.**

The adjustable dampers in engine room shall be operated manually by chain if necessary.

The independent exhaust air duct shall be arranged for purifier area and ER workshop welding space. And the ventilating duct for purifier area should be fitted a fire damper.

**Exhaust duct to be provided over heavy fuel oil purifiers in the purifier’s space.**

**Exhaust duct to be provided in welding space of workshop.**

Ducts shall be securely supported or braced from ship's structure and shall be designed to avoid irregular bends or branches as far as practicable.

The pin, hinge, bolts and nuts in the fan casing and duct-connecting flange exposed to weather shall be stainless steel (SUS316 or brass).

Excess air from the engine room shall be discharged to atmosphere through louvers at the aft of the funnel.

The E.C.R. shall be air-conditioned and supplied with mechanical ventilation with damper.

The working ladders or step shall be provided for maintenance if necessary.

### 6.8.4 SILENCERS

The silencer shall be provided for generator engines and emergency generator engine.

### 6.8.5 ENGINE CONTROL ROOM, ENGINE ROOM WORKSHOP & STORES

#### 6.8.5.1 Engine Control Room

The engine control room shall be heat and sound insulated, and shall be provided with engine control, monitoring console and main switchboard etc. A unit cooler for air conditioning shall be also provided.

One (1) escape with a continuous fire shelter and vertical ladders to open deck shall be provided in compliance with the requirement of MSC 93.

A clear walkway shall be arranged between consoles and window bulkhead.

#### 6.8.5.2 E/R Workshop

A workshop shall be located in the engine room and provided with such as universal machine tool, etc. as listed in Section 6.2.15 and one (1) work bench, two (2) sets of vise, one (1) welding table, shelves, lockers, etc. lifting beam and a door with locking device shall be provided for the workshop. Workshop to be enclosed by steel wall.

Fuel valve test devices shall be located in workshop.

**One (1) tool board to be provided in workshop.**

Acetylene and oxygen bottles shall be installed outside the engine room and suitable piping with blow back valve shall be provided from bottle room to welding space in workshop.

One (1) escape with a continuous fire shelter and vertical ladders to open deck shall be provided in compliance with the requirement of MSC 93.

#### 6.8.5.3 Electrical Workshop

A separate electrical workshop shall be located in the engine room.

One (1) motor driven table driller, one (1) bench with vice, and one (1) test panel shall be provided.

Electrical Workshop shall be enclosed by steel wall.

#### 6.8.5.4 Store

Each one (1) engine store and electric store shall be arranged and suitable steel shelves laid wood plate shall be provided in the store. The electrical store will be isolated with electrical workshop by steel wire wall.

***There are six(6) drawer style storage to be installed in the engine store.***

### 6.8.6 LADDERS, HANDRAILS, GRATINGS AND FLOOR PLATES

The painted ladders, painted handrails, painted gratings and painted floor plates shall be provided in accordance with shipbuilder practice.

#### 6.8.6.1 Ladder

Main access ladders shall be led fore and aft wherever possible and to slope of 55~60 degrees from the horizontal, and width of main ladder shall be of 700mm and that of sub-ladders 500 mm.

Ladders to be inclined type, except where it is unavoidable, vertical ladder shall be used for unimportant access provision. Galvanized steel dust guard shall be fitted at underside of main ladders.

Treads shall be a non-slip type.

All ladders shall be attached at top and bottom by bolts to provide ready portability for overhaul of machinery when necessary.

#### 6.8.6.2 Handrail

Handrail shall be fitted at gratings, ladders and floors where necessary for the safety and convenience of operating personal. Handrails shall be of steel pipe carried in steel pipe stanchions and shall be fitted with portable section where required for overhauling machinery.

Handrails shall have a clear hand space of at least 50mm from adjacent equipment and bulkhead.

#### 6.8.6.3 Floor plate

In general, the flooring shall be checkered steel plate of about 4.5 mm in thickness, supported and fastened to suitable bars of angle frame by not less four (4) stainless steel or brass screws.

Removable sections shall be provided as required for proper access for handling and inspection of the equipment located under floor and for manholes.

Floor plates sections not to be larger than what can be handled by one man as far as practicable.

Coaming of height 50mm shall be provided around permanent openings.

**Opening in the checkered steel plate for valve access shall be cut by a tool on site.**

#### 6.8.6.4 Grating

Adequate grating of steel shall be provided for machinery space walkways, platforms and floors only where specifically required for ventilation and continuous visibility purposes. Gratings to be made of twisted bar and steel plate, suitable spaced and properly fitted in steel flat frames.

#### 6.8.6.5 Funnel

Ladder and grating also shall be installed in funnel. The flue louver shall be controlled outside the funnel by compressed air and also can be controlled by manual.

#### 6.8.6.6 Protection Device

All moving parts such as flywheel, coupling shall be protected by safety cover or hand rail.

### 6.8.7 DISTINGUISHING AND UNIT

In case of two or more sets of identical machinery units are installed, those machinery shall be distinguished by numbering. In general, the numbering shall be carried out in this way:

From up to down

From fore to aft.

From port to starboard

The measuring instruments used for equipment and piping shall be according to International Standard.

Name plates shall be made of brass plate and marked by etching and painted black for illustration plate, red for warning plate and valve name plate respectively.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Item | Language | Measuring unit |
| Instruments:  Thermometer  Temperature indicator  Pressure gauge  Compound gauge  Vacuum gauge  Level indicator  Electric indicator  Salinity indicator  Flow meter  Indication of tank volume  Measuring instruments | English | Metric or SI |
| Name plates & drawings:  Name plate (fitted to machinery) Plan for approval  Finished plan  Instruction book  Inspection record  Test record  Sea trial record | English | Metric or SI |
| Name plate (fitted to valve) | English |  |

## 6.9 INSULATION AND PAINTING

### 6.9.1 INSULATING

#### 6.9.1.1 General

The surface of the equipment, tanks and piping which shall treat or contain the fluid with temperature over 60C except for cooling F.W. piping and L.O. piping should be insulated.

Main engine, generator engines, boiler, incinerator and calorifier shall be insulated according to the Maker’s standard.

Where it is necessary to fit removable and replaceable insulation on flanges, fittings, and covers, etc. The tailor-made pads or blankets shall be used.

The outer face temperature after insulation shall be not exceeded by 60oC when the engine room temperature is 45C.

#### 6.9.1.2 Insulation for Thermal Equipment.

(1) Boiler and Heater

Maker will deliver the boiler with insulation.

The minimum thickness of insulation material for surfaces of large extent such as heaters, etc. shall be met the following requirements or according to the Maker’s standard.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Temperature range of internal fluid | Ceramic fibre moulding or rock wool |
| 60 to 155C | 25mm |
| 156 to 260C | 50mm |

(2) H.F.O., U.L.S.F.O./ L.S.H.F.O. Tanks

* HFO and LSHFO/ULSFO settling tanks
* HFO and LSHFO/ULSFO service tanks

In case of structure tank, front and side walls faced to engine room area only shall be insulated and to be covered with galvanized steel plate up to 2.3m in height from bottom of deck. The remaining upper part shall be covered with aluminum foil coated fiber glass cloth.

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Material | Dimension | Remark |
| 1 | Ceramic fibre moulding or rock wool | 25 mm |  |
| 2 | Steel plate | 0.5 mm | Galvanized |

(4) Silencers

The exhaust gas silencers for generator engine and emergency generator engine should be insulated with min. 50mm thickness of Ceramic fibre moulding or rock wool and covered with 0.5mm galvanized steel sheet.

#### 6.9.1.3 Insulation for exhaust gas piping

The exhaust gas piping and uptake in engine room shall be insulated and the requirements are as follows:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Name of equipment | Insulation | | Cover |
| Thickness (mm) | Material |
| Main engine | Pipe 75  Flange75 | Ceramic fibre moulding or rock wool | Glass cloth + galv. steel sheet 0.5mm thick |
| Generator engine | Pipe & flange 75 | Ditto | Ditto |
| Incinerator &  boiler | Pipe & flange 50 | Ditto | Ditto |

The exhaust gas piping and uptake from bottom to nav. deck above three (3) meters in funnel shall be insulated with thickness of 50mm and covered with galvanized steel sheet of 0.5mm thickness.

In all case where the pipe insulation contacts on the flanges and fittings, the insulation shall be suitably terminated to permit free removal of bolt and to allow for movement of the pipe at supports.

#### 6.9.1.4 Insulation for Thermal Fluid Piping

The following piping system should be insulated.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Name of pipe | DN  mm | Insulation | | Cover |
| Thickness  mm | Material |
| H.F.O.，/LSHFO/ULSFO | <50  >50  <10 | 30  40 | Mineral wool  Two layers of glass cloth | glass cloth  glass cloth |
| Steam, condense | <50  >50 | 30  40 | Mineral wool h | glass cloth |
| Hot water |  | 20 | Mineral wool | glass cloth |

In principle, the H.F.O. ,LSHFO/ULSFOpiping (including HFO,LSHFO/ULSFO transferring pipe line, HFO,LSHFO/ULSFO purifying pipe line, HFO,LSHFO/ULSFO service pipe line, HFO,LSHFO/ULSFO drain pipe line and HFO,LSHFO/ULSFO return pipe line) should be provided with steam tracing pipe and the connection of steam tracing pipe should close up to the flange of the H.F.O. ,LSHFO/ULSFO pipe.

The following pipes shall be insulated with glass cloth.

Boiler blow pipe

Exhaust steam pipe for safety valves

Drain pipe after steam drain valves and drain traps

### 6.9.2 PAINTING

Machinery and piping in engine room shall be painted except following parts.

1. Working surface of machinery, brass surface, and other parts, which are finished bright.

2. Surfaces of insulation, which is not covered with steel sheet or equal.

External surface of pipes and valves fitted below floor level (E/R grating of tank top) shall be painted with 2 coats anti-corrosion paint only.

**Emergency Exit path to be marked with Florescent paint at all platforms / levels.**

Other machinery and equipment shall be in accordance with Maker's standard.

The color of finished coat for external surface shall be in accordance with the following table. Maker's standard surface color shall prevail if there is conflict with the following table for individual equipment.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Name of machinery or equipment | Color (Yard proposal) |
| Diesel engine  Air compressor  Centrifugal pump  Screw and gear pump  Oil purifier (acc. to Maker’s standard)  Fan  Oily bilge separator  Sewage treatment plant  F.W. generator  Overhauling crane  Workshop machine  Intermediate shaft bearing  Steel box for spare parts  L.O. and F.W. coolers | Light blue green  (Munsell notation:  7.5 BG 7/2) |
| Turbocharger for main engine  Turbocharger for generator engine  Boiler  Incinerator  Oil heater  Atmospheric condenser | Silver |
| Air reservoir  Tanks not to be insulated  Pipes not to be insulated  Air trunk  Water pressure tank  Valves not to be insulated  Strainer  Top rail of hand rail  Ladder except step | White |

The piping shall be marked as per Buyer’s standard with color vinyl tapes or color paints to indicate the various mediums.

The medium flow direction shall be indicated by arrow shown outside the piping.

## 6.10 PIPING SCHEDULE IN ENGINE ROOM

### 6.10.1 GENERAL

Piping workmanship to satisfy the requirement of the Classification Society and this section concerned.

Piping is to be led as direct as practicable, with a minimum number of bends and with suitable number of flange joints for removal. Sleeve joints or butt welding joints shall be used where practicable.

All piping shall be supported according to good practice in order to prevent damages from vibrations and other causes.

Pipes to have suitable thickness for each service, and shall be tested in accordance with the requirement of the Classification Society.

Expansion shall be compensated for by means of bend except where otherwise described.

Pipes of galvanized steel or brass or copper shall be bent in cold process. In case that cold bending machine is not applicable, high frequency induction bender or hot bending process shall be used.

The radius of bends of steel pipes, in general, not to be less than 2.5 times the outside diameter except narrow space of structure or crowding of pipes, where steel bend pieces hall be used. Bends of copper pipes except coils shall be not less than twice the outside diameter as far as practicable.

Commercial bend pieces will be used as far as practicable.

For the following cases, butt welding connection or fabrication shall be carried out.

1. When the cold bending machine is not applicable.

2. Where welding piece such as tube turn or bend piece is used.

3. To make fabricated steel pipe of large diameter such as main engine exhaust pipe.

Oil piping and electric cables to the greatest possible extent shall be kept well clear of not to be installed close to steam lines and diesel engines exhaust pipes.

Water piping not to be installed close to diesel engines exhaust pipes as far as possible.

Piping in way of the machinery and equipment shall be arranged to permit overhaul of the unit with no dismantling of piping as far as practicable.

Where possible, piping at tank top level shall be arranged so that any length may be removed without disturbing adjacent pipelines.

Air pockets in pipe lines shall be avoided as far as practicable. Where pockets do occur, bosses with a cock or screwed plug for drainage are to be provided.

Pipes exposed to weather are to be fitted with drain plugs where necessary.

Where galvanized piping is specified, galvanizing shall be carried out after pipes are fabricated and flanges are attached, as far as practicable. Galvanized pipes shall be fitted with galvanized bolts, nuts and clamping devices.

All piping shall be cleaned and free of welding slag before installation.

Following piping system shall be flushed with the under-mentioned medium after being fitted on board, and these piping systems to be in whole accordance with maker recommendations.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| System | Application | Method |
| Lub. oil piping | Main engine line | To be circulated by flushing oil |
| Line from cylinder oil tank to engine | To be blown out by compressed air |
| Fuel oil piping | Main engine line  Diesel generator line | To be circulated by diesel oil |
| Boiler F.O. burning line  Incinerator fuel oil line | To be blown out by compressed air |
| Comp. air piping | Main engine starting air line Diesel generator starting air line Cont. air line | To be blown out by compressed air |
| Steam & condensate | Steam supply line  Condensate return line | Steam blow off |
| Hydraulic oil | Bow thruster  Steering gear | Flushing oil |
| Boiler feed water line |  | Compressed air blow off |
|  |  |  |
| Refrigerant piping (if necessary) | Refrigerate plant  AC plant | To be blown out by N2 gas |

***If flushing of pipes are done by yard supplied lub.oil, builder should present the lab test certificate done prior usage for flushing. Flushing lub. oil not to be reused.***

Where pipes pass through the water/oil tight bulkhead and deck, penetration pieces of two flanges with double plate and sleeve joint are to be used.

Piping is to be marked with color vinyl tape or paint for easy recognition. Color marking for various pipe systems shall be according to ISO standard.

After finishing of steel pipes, the acid pickling and neutralizing shall be carried out for the following pipes before installation on board and coated inside of pipes with suitable oil for rust protection. Pipes after acid pickling shall be well covered at ends to keep clean.

a. Lubricating oil pipes except oil bilge pipe and air vent pipe.

b. Fuel oil service pipes for main engine, diesel generator and boiler burning line only.

c. Hydraulic oil steel pipe.

Liquid pipe lines shall be kept away from the switchboard and other electrical equipment.

Where the piping is unavoidable and flanges to be led above the electrical appliances, the welded joint to be provided.

All detachable pipe connections and valves of fuel oil piping shall be at a safe distance from boiler, exhaust pipes or other heated surface.

All connecting dimension of flanges shall be according to ISO standard. Asbestos material is not to be used for gasket and insulation.

Brass or stainless steel name plates with engraved letters are to be referred to piping system drawings for all valves, pumps, heat exchangers etc.

### 6.10.2 VALVE AND FITTING

All valves and cocks shall be in accordance with Chinese standard, but the connecting dimension of flange shall be in accordance with ISO standard.

In general, stop valves, gate valves and angle valves shall be used for all piping system unless specially specified. Butterfly valves shall be used for the pipe lines of 80 mm bores and above where applicable for fresh water, sea water, lubricating oil, fuel oil and others in accordance with Builder’s practice.

The material of the butterfly valve shall be as follows:

Body Cast steel for ship side valves, cast iron for others

Disc Aluminum bronze

Seat Synthetic rubber (NBR) spindle stainless steel

The wafer type butterfly valve shall be adopted except ship side valves, which are to be of flanged type or lugged type. That in ER (DN250mm above) to be lugged type.

All butterfly valves (except oil valve) shall be provided with synthetic rubber (NBR) lining or renewable NBR seat except that fluoro rubber lining shall be used for high temperature fresh water cooling system.

Butterfly valves for oil piping line shall be applied to oil resistance material instead of NBR seat.

***Manually operated butterfly valve shall be provided with mechanical indicator (open or close) actuated by the revolution of the hand wheel or hand notch***

In case where drain traps are served continuously, a by- pass line shall be provided.

Each pressure reducing valve is to be provided on its discharge side with a pressure gauge and a safety valve having sufficient discharge capacity to prevent excessive pressure in the low pressure line.

Temperature control valves are to be provided with a manually operated handle. In case where manual handle is not fitted, a suitable by-pass line is to be provided.

Valves are to be fitted as extensively as possible instead of cocks.

Cocks may be used for low pressure gauge and drain lines.

Remote quick-closing valves in fuel oil lines are to be of pneumatic type. These valves are to be capable of being operated locally.

Valves below engine room floor are to be arranged for easy access with wheel spindle upward vertically near to floor plate as far as possible.

Suitable handles having engraved brass name plate with arrow indicator in English are to be fitted to each manually operated valve.

### 6.10.3 VELOCITIES IN PIPE LINES

The fluid velocities in pipelines shall be as per follows:

Sea water cooling line, suction side: abt. 2.5m/s

Sea water cooling line, discharge side: abt.3.5m/s

Fresh cooling water line: abt.3m/s

ballast and bilge line : abt. 3 m/s for steel pipes

FO(excluding filling line): abt. 2.0m/s

LO(excluding filling line): abt. 2.0m/s
