# CHAPTER 8 ELECTRIC PART

## **8.1** GENERAL

## **8.1.1** GENERAL

The whole electrical installation shall comply with IEC and ISO standard, and to meet relative rules, regulations and convention which are listed in the “Part I General” of the Specifications.

Electric works on the vessel shall be carried out in accordance with these Specifications and Builder's practice.

Electric equipment and function shall be satisfied with specification and related recent rule.

Earth wire for equipment in/outside shall be prepared as per IEC standard.

More than terminal or connector with protective cover in electric panel shall be applied in order to prevent electrical shock of the operator.

Enough working space and door stopper shall be prepared when door of electric equipment open.

Pipe joints near side electric equipment shall be provided by sleeve or equivalent method for electric equipment protection. No piping or components containing liquids (including drains) shall be arranged inside rooms where switchboards, transformers, batteries, rectifiers, variable frequency controllers, etc. are installed. If piping passing through cannot be avoided, piping welding joints (sleeves) must be used, and shields must be installed above the electrical equipment / panels.

Final electric connection diagram with pocket shall be prepared in the panel door for easy maintenance.

If any items in the hull or machinery Specification necessitate the installation of electrical equipment not mentioned in this part, such equipment shall be provided by Builder.

Voltage and Frequency:

All electric equipment to function at variations of:

Frequency: ±5% at the continuous load condition

±10% at the transient load condition

Voltage: +6/-10% at the continuous load condition

±20% at the transient load condition

An ambient temperature of 45deg.C shall be assumed for electrical equipment in all spaces. Where ambient temperature is in excess of these values, the temperature specified by the Rule shall not be exceeded.

The meters to be of Class 1.5 and to have scale of the following range with red color mark at rated value.

Voltmeter: 0 to abt. 120% of rated voltage

Ammeter: 0 to abt. 130% of rated current

Wattmeter: -15% (reverse power) to abt. 130% of rated wattage

Frequency meter: 55 - 65 Hz

The type and construction of electrical equipment incorporated or packed with the appliances, shall be in accordance with the manufacturers' standard unless specially described and may be changed by their Maker’s type or model changes.

All electrical machines and apparatus delivered to the shipyard and waiting installation are to be kept in a clean, dry and well ventilation store.

Electric equipment will be inspected and tested in accordance with the Rule, the Regulations and the Builder's usual practice.

Trial

The trials for all electrical equipment in manufacturer’s shop and or on board shall be carried out according to the requirements of Classification Society and the Builder’s standard and approved by Buyer.

**“Trials program for electrical equipment” shall be provided for *Owners* review one month before sea trial.**

After installations on board have been finished, all electrical equipment shall be tested to demonstrate their condition for satisfactory operation in accordance with the requirement of Rules and the detail design document of “Trials program for electrical equipment”.

## **8.1.2** ARRANGEMENT OF EQUIPMENT

The arrangement of the electrical equipment throughout the Vessel shall be such as to provide ready and safe access to all parts for inspection, maintenance and repair as far as practicable.

All electrical equipment shall be so located that as far as practicable they are not exposed to risk of mechanical injury or damage from water, steam, oil or excessive heat and where inflammable gases cannot accumulate. Where necessarily exposed to such risks, the equipment shall be suitably constructed or enclosed.

**All junction boxes shall be clearly marked with name by the drawings, necessary access hatches and space around repairing and etc. shall be considered**.

Where electrical equipment is installed in the hazardous area such as battery store or paint store or cargo hold carried dangerous goods in, the equipment shall be of explosion proof type or intrinsically safe type.

## **8.1.3** NAME PLATE

***Flame retardant and*** non-corrosive material are to be used for nameplates, labels, etc. ***Nameplates on open decks shall be made of brass or stainless steel***.

All nameplates are to be fixed with screws or rivets. ***The nameplates shall include at least item number and functional description***

Type of plate shall be as follows:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| - | Rotating machine | : | ***Flame retardant and non***-corrosive metal plate |
| - | Controller and panel | : | Plastic plate or Maker’ standard, except  non-corrosive metal plate for those exposed to weather |
| - | Others | : | Maker’s standard |

The letter on the nameplate shall be in English. The fitting type of nameplate should be screw fitting or according to maker’s standard.

The caution plates shall be in English.

## **8.1.4** PAINTING COLORS

Metal surfaces of the enclosure of electrical equipment shall be painted with the following colors or according to the Buyer’s specified.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Generators, motors | Munsell code 7.5BG 7/2 |
| Transformers | Munsell code 7.5BG 7/2 |
| Switchboards, distribution panels and starter boards, engine control console etc. | Munsell code 7.5BG 7/2 |
| Bridge control console | Munsell code 7.5BG 7/2 |
| Interior communication, navigation and radio equipment | Manufacturer's standards |
| General alarm and other emergency operating equipment | Munsell code 5R4/13 (Red) |
| Others | Manufacturer's standard |

Interior metal surfaces of electrical equipment shall be painted with manufacturer's standard colors.

Resin made surface of electrical equipment shall be of manufacturer's standard colors.

Emergency lights to be provided with red mark.

## **8.1.5** MARK AND ARRANGEMENT OF BUS BAR

Bus bars and connections of major power equipment shall be marked with tapes, paints, letters or equivalent and shall be arranged as follows:

(A) A.C. system

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Source side** | **Load side** | **Color** | **Arrangement** | | |
| Phase R | Phase U | Black | Left | Top | Front |
| Phase S | Phase V | Brown | to | | |
| Phase T | Phase W | Grey | Right | Bottom | Back |

(B) DC. system

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Pole** | **Color** | **Arrangement** | | |
| Positive (+) | Brown | Left | Top | Front |
| to | | | | |
| Negative (-) | Blue | Right | Bottom | Back |

## **8.1.6** EQUIPMENT AND MATERIAL

Electrical equipment and material shall be marine use one in general.

***Control box with contact and emergency stop box (bunker station) on the open deck to be provided with space heater. Not including switches, reefer container sockets junction boxes, navigation and radio equipment.***

Fuse, terminal and lamp shall be as mentioned below, except for those of special equipment such as navigation instrument, radio equipment and other electronic equipment shall be of Maker’s standard.

Fuse In general, tubular or screw type fuse to be used except special type fuses for electronic equipment.

Terminal Solderless type except for small electric terminal for lighting fixtures, switch and branch box etc.

Lamp

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Purpose |  |
| For fluorescent lamp | General light | Two pin type |
| For incandescent lamp | General light, floodlight and  signal light | .  E-27 (≤200 W) |
| Pilot lamp of switchboard,  starter, console, etc. | Manufacturer’s standard |
| Floodlight and searchlight | E-40 (>200 W) |
| For sodium and halogen lamp | Floodlight | E-40, ***Manufacturer’s standard*** |

Electrical equipment and wiring shall in general not to be installed in hazardous areas unless essential for operational purposes. The type of equipment and installation requirements shall comply with class rules.

*Breaker*

(A) Air Circuit Breaker (ACB)

Air circuit breakers may be used for protection of main generators, bow thruster. Air circuit breaker (ACB) to be of 3-pole hand and automatic operated, trip free, with breaker operation facilities in the main contact isolated position.Air circuit breakers (ACB) in Main and Emergency Switchboards shall be with draw-able type.

(B) Moulded Case Circuit Breaker (MCCB)

Moulded case circuit breaker will be used for protection of feeder circuits and may be fitted with magnetic instant trip, thermal trip, or shunt trip coil and/or under voltage trip coil depending on each application.Moulded Case Circuit Breakers (MCCB) is to be of plug-in type in Main- and Emergency Switchboards.

Miniature circuit breaker (MCB) will be used for protection of feeder circuits in lighting system and domestic equipment.

(C) Bus-tie switch (as per Maker)

Due to total electrical power of generators to be very large, bus bar and bus-tie switch of MSB must have enough capacity as per rules and Manufacturer’s standard.

## **8.2** WIRING

## **8.2.1** WIRING SYSTEM

**All cables shall be marked at both ends with the cable reference numbers as per drawings. Marks shall be flame retardant with impressed letters. The individual conductor ends in the cables shall be marked with closed ring marks. All internal wiring in switchboards, panels, consoles, etc. shall also be marked with closed rings at both ends with reference numbers as per drawings. (according to maker standard)**

The distribution system shall consist of three-phase AC. three-wire insulated system, single phase AC. two-wire insulated system and DC two-wire insulated system.

The distribution system shall be as follows:

General power system:

1) AC 440 V system: 3 PH, 60 Hz, 3-wire insulated system

2) AC 220 V system: 3 PH, 60 Hz, 3-wire insulated system and single phase two-wire insulated system

3) DC 24 V system: 2-wire insulated system.

Galley and domestic equipment (large capacity AC440V):

AC 440 V/220 V, 3 PH/1PH, 60 Hz, 3-wire/2 wires

Lighting main circuit:

AC 220 V, 3 PH, 60 Hz, 3-wire

Branch circuits of lighting, small capacity domestic equipment:

AC 220 V, 1 PH, 60 Hz, 2-wire

Nautical instruments and radio equipment:

AC 220 V, 3 PH /1 PH, 3 wire/2 wire, 60 Hz, and DC 24 V 2-wire

Interior communication and alarm system and automation:

AC 220V, 1 PH, 60 Hz, 2-wire or DC 24 V, 2-wire

Bow thruster motor:

AC 440 V, 3 PH, 60 Hz

Reefer container:

AC 440 V, 3 PH, 60 Hz

The distribution system shall be insulated against hull throughout the vessel except for ground detecting circuits, secondary circuits of potential and current transformers will be earthed at switchboard or control panel.

The voltage for some portable equipment such as portable control box for turning gear motor and traveling crane and so on should be lower than AC 50 V using two (2) windings type transformer of which the secondary winding shall not be earthed.

The metal frame or body for portable equipment shall be earthed by the earth connection, if the voltage for portable equipment is AC 220 V.

## **8.2.2** CABLE APPLICATION

All cables accepted by the Classification Society shall be provided.

In general, electric cable shall be of IEC marine cable (IEC 60092 series) ,and flame retardant type tested according to IEC 60332-1 and IEC 60332-3 Category, low smoke and halogen-free or equivalent type that has been approved by the Classification Society, except special cable which including: coaxial cable, compensate cable and LAN net cable etc.Cables in accommodation spaces to be of XLPE insulated, Metallic halide free sheathed (extruded or lapped).

Cables shall be of EP rubber or XLPE insulated, metal wire braided with polyolefin (PO) or polychloroprene rubber (PCP) covering.

Cables for lighting system in accommodation area shall be of EP rubber or XLPE insulated with polyolefin (PO) polychloroprene rubber (PCP)) covering.

For portable appliances, cables to be of flexible rubber insulated and polyvinyl chloride (PVC) or polychloroprene rubber (PCP) sheathed, and for table lamps to be of flexible vinyl cord.

The other insulating material cables may also be adopted, but permissive operating temperatures of cable conductor should be 90 oC.

Kind and size of cables supplied by manufacturers together with equipment to be accordance with manufacturer’s standard.

All cables throughout the vessel, except special cables such as coaxial cables, compensating cables, network cables, cables supplied together with equipment, etc. will be type approved by Classification Society.

## **8.2.3** CABLE INSTALLATION

All cables shall be installed according to builder's practice and in compliance with the requirement of the Classification Society.

In general, cables shall run in groups and parallel and be fixed on steel hangers or trays.

Where the cables are exposed to mechanical damage, they shall be protected with steel pipe or steel cover.

Cables installed on mast or post on upper deck to be laid in galvanized steel pipe up to about 1m height from the deck.

The cables installed under the engine room lower floor shall be protected with flexible conduit or steel pipe or steel cover.

Cables passing through water-tight decks or bulkheads, ***Heat shrunk for all*** water-tight cable glands or other appropriate methods shall be employed.

Cables passing through beams, non-water-tight decks and bulkheads etc., suitable bushing or coaming with round edge shall be used for their protection.

The cables in living quarters shall be secured by nylon straps and plastic covered stainless steel straps, at wet space and exposed weather space, only plastic covered stainless steel straps to be used, unless the cables secured by conduit or steel pipe.

Penetration of fire protection bulkheads or decks of steel structures shall be protected by pipes, cable glands or coaming stuffed with fire retardant compound according to the fire protection class and number of cables.

In rooms and inner passages, where lining walls over steel walls and ceiling over overhead decks are provided, cables shall be concealed behind the lining walls as far as practicable.

***Signal cables shall be always separated from power cables. Yard to describe same in shipyard standard for electrical practices; Sharp bend of cables not allowed.***

The cabletrays to be galvanized in general, except ***hanger to be the builder's practice,inside water ballast tanks, PVC pipe with stainless clamps can be adopted by builder’s practice***.

Foundation for electrical equipment, small outfitting materials and fittings will be blasted and painted in general.

The support of cable trays & electric equipment brackets should be welded directly on deck plate, frames, girders and bulkhead.

The installation of cable trays and electric equipment brackets will be in accordance with Builder’s actual practice.

## **8.3** PRIMARY SOURCE

## **8.3.1** GENERAL

Three(3) sets of main generator AC 450 V, 3 PH, 60 Hz, each driven by diesel engine shall be installed in the engine room with the shaft parallel to ship's centerline.

One (1) set of emergency diesel generator AC 450 V, 3 PH, 60 Hz shall be installed in the emergency generator room. The emergency generator shall be used for supplying the loads such as radio equipment, interior communication equipment, nautical instruments, emergency lights, one set steering gear and emergency fire pump, one engine room fan, the emergency air compressor, etc. when the main power station fails.

## **8.3.2** MAIN GENERATORS

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Type: | Drip-proof, self-ventilated type with air filter, and the air filter as per Maker’s standard |
| Output: | abt. 1,250 kW x 3 sets (DG) |
| Voltage: | AC 450 V |
| Phase: | 3 PH |
| Frequency: | 60 Hz |
| Power factor: | 0.8 (lagging) |
| Rating: | Continuous at full load |
| Revolution: | 900 r/min or as per Maker’s standard； |
| Insulation: | Class “F” |
| Exciting system: | Brushless, self-excitation |
| Protection: | With differential protection function |
| Enclosure: | IP 23 |

Note:

Protection grade IP 23 of main generators will be suitable in respect of water based fire- fighting system and will be certified by Classification Society.

Other particulars and construction of the main generators shall be in accordance with manufacturers' standard.

Each main generator shall have a space heater within the generator frame to prevent the condensation of moisture while the generator is stopped.

An automatic voltage regulator for each main generator shall be provided and located in MSB.

The main generator bearing type and lubrication function shall be manufacturers' standard. Temperature sensor shall be provided for bearing of the generator. Two temperature sensors shall be fitted in the stator winding of each phase of generators for alarm, one for working and the other for spare.

The main generators shall be capable of parallel operation. However, main generators neither to be run in parallel with emergency generator nor the shore source.

Each main generator shall be used as follows:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | Without reefer container | With reefer containers |
| Normal sea going | DG x 1 | DG x 2 |
| Arrival or departure with bow thruster | DG x 2 | DG x 3 |
| Cargo handling | DG x 1 | DG x 3 |
| Rest in port | DG x 1 | DG x 2 |

The reefer container load for electric power balance may be considered as follows:

Total 220 sets of reefer containers socket(CEE type, 32A) on deck .

The reefer containers power demand for electric power balance shall be determined as follows:(4.5 kW/FEU x 220 RFEU = 990 kW.)

If bow thruster cannot be operated with ship's loads including reefer containers, some of reefer container loads to be off manually during bow thruster operation at port in/out condition.

If dangerous goods loaded on deck, the feeder breaker in main switch board must be locked and take off power source of reefer containers by locking device at ship office.

***Proper procedure to be provided. System must then automatically block start of Bow Thruster till load is brought down to acceptable limits.***.

## **8.3.3** EMERGENCY GENERATOR

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Type: | Drip-proof, self-ventilated type |
| Output: | Abt. 150 kW |
| Voltage: | AC 450 V |
| Phase: | 3 PH |
| Frequency: | 60 Hz |
| Power factor: | 0.8 (lagging) |
| Rating: | Continuous at full load |
| Revolution: | 1,800 r/min； |
| Insulation: | Class “F” |
| Exciting system: | Brushless, self-excitation |
| Protection class: | IP 23 |

Other construction and characteristics of the emergency generator shall be in accordance with the manufacturer's standard.

Two starting methods will be provided as per rule and manufacturer's standard such as to be used by one(1) set battery and hydraulic device or other equivalent differ starting method.

The emergency generator shall have a space heater within the generator frame to prevent condensation of moisture while the generator is stopped.

An automatic voltage regulator for emergency generator shall be provided.

This generator shall be started automatically in case of occurrence of the power failure of the main power supply and shall automatically supply electric power to the emergency loads.

After restoration of electric power from the main generator, the power supply system shall be automatically disconnected from the emergency generator and connect to the main generator. The emergency generator engine shall be automatically stopped with time delay.

Emergency generator can’t be run in parallel with main generators.

## **8.3.4** MAIN SWITCHBOARD

In case that the contents in the following parts of this section differ from manufacturer's standard for specific equipment Makers’ standard shall be applied

in general.

***IEC standards or wording “national standards” for the Main Switchboard.(8.3.4 Main Sitchboard) to be reference., such as rule: IEC61111***

## **8.3.4.1** General

The main switchboard to be consist of: (or according to manufacturer's standard)

Three(3) -- Generator control panels

One (1) -- Synchronizing & bus-tie panel

One (1) -- Bow thruster feeder panel

Two (2) -- AC 440 V feeder panels (or four panels as per manufacturer)

Two (2) -- Group starter panels (or four panels as per manufacturer )

One (1) -- AC 220 V feeder panel

***One (1) -- Empty cold-iron panel for AMP ready in future***

Two (2) --Reefer container panels

Each generator panel and bow thruster feeder panel to be protected by a three pole air circuit breaker (ACB).

The main switchboard, for receiving power from main generators and for the power distribution, shall be installed in engine control room with clear maintenance access to the front and rear of the panel as per rules, insulating mat shall be provided at front and rear of the main switchboard.

The main switchboard shall be multi cubicle, metal enclosed self-supporting, dead front type (IP20) with hinged front panels that can be opened without disturbing installed equipment and complete with necessary fittings and instruments.

Between cubicles shall be closed by flame retarding insulating material to prevent fire hazard passing to adjacent.

All bolts, screws etc., used in connection of current carrying conductors shall be adequately locked with lock nuts and spring washers or as manufacturer's standard.

The top and each side of the switchboard shall be protected with steel plate and suitable hand rail shall be provided at front and rear. The main switchboard shall have hinged front doors and removable rear side covers. Main cable shall entry through cable hole from under side.

The preferential tripping system shall be provided and so arranged that in the event of the main generators becoming overloaded the non-essential loads are disconnected automatically before the generators' circuit breaker is opened. The preferential tripping arrangement shall be in two stages sequential (the first stage to be general non-essential loads and the second reefer containers), as necessary.

Voltage circuits for control and instrumentation to be earth free and protected by double pole fuse.

Air circuit breakers (ACB) shall be of electrically operated trip free type and controlled by a control switch and additionally a manual operating handle shall be provided.

All AC440V out-going feeder circuits and shore source circuit to be protected by a three pole molded case circuit breaker (MCCB) with over-load trip and instantaneous trip on each pole, except for steering gear motor circuit which to be only equipped with an instantaneous trip. And all AC 220V out-going feeder circuits to be protected by a three/ two pole molded case circuit breaker (MCCB) or three/two pole miniature type circuit breaker (MCB) with over-load trip and instantaneous trip on each pole.

Each feeder circuit on the main switchboard shall be distinctly marked by label giving service name of each circuit and frame/set current for the circuit breaker.

The molded case circuit breaker (MCCB) for feeder circuits of motors as described in item 6-3.3 and 6-3.6 shall be provided with a shunt trip coil for emergency stop or preferential trip.

In case that the contents in the following each panel of this section differ from manufacturer's standard for specific equipment, manufacturer's standard shall be applied in general.

**Certified insulation mat *(IEC61111)* to be provided in front and back of MSB and in front of ESB**

***The accuracy of meter to be within 1.5 (error: within 1.5% of full scale), except the meters for motor starter for which class 2.5 shall be applied.***

***Air from ventilation ducts shall not be discharged directly on the switchboard.***

***The bus bar of main switchboard shall be provided with bus-tie switch (manual control)***

## **8.3.4.2** Generator control panel

For proper operation and maintenance, the following instruments and apparatus shall be provided for each generator panel:

1 - Air circuit breaker (ACB)

1 - AC ammeter

1 - Change-over switch for AC ammeter (for each phase of generator)

1 - AC voltmeter

1 - Change-over switch for AC voltmeter (between each line of generator)

1 – Power factor meter

1 – Running hour meter

1 - Frequency meter

1 - Manual voltage regulator.

1 - ACB open/close control switch (or push button)

1 - Switch for space heater

1 - ACB close indicating lamp (green)

1 - ACB open indicating lamp (red)

1 - Space heater indicating lamp (orange)

1 - Running hour meter

**1 – set standby indicator light in blue**

Etc.

And other necessary equipment;

***The generators system must automatically block start of Bow Thruster till the load is brought down to acceptable limits.***

The following apparatus shall be provided:

* - MSB preferential & emergency stop circuit source fail
* Preferential trip
* Low/high voltage
* Low frequency
* Insulation low for AC 440V circuit
* Insulation low for AC 220V circuit in main switchboard
* 1- Lamp test switch/alarm reset button

And other necessary equipment;

## **8.3.4.4** AC440 V Feeder Panel

The following device shall be provided for AC440 V feeder panel:

Necessary quantity - module case circuit breakers (MCCB) (with abt. 10% spare breakers for AC440V load only). All MCCB shall be of plug-in type.

\*1 -Molded case type circuit breaker(MCCB) for shore supply

\*1 -Shore supply indicating lamp (white lamp) and kWh meter

\*1 -Insulation monitor with alarm lamp for checking AC440 V system

\*1-Ammeter, it will be share with other equipment.

## **8.3.4.5** AC 220 V Feeder Panel

The following device shall be provided for AC 220 V feeder panel:

Necessary quantity - Miniature circuit breakers (MCB, with abt. 10% spare breakers based on amount of circuit breakers on feed panel);

1 - Insulation monitor with alarm lamp for checking AC 220 V system

1 - AC ammeter

1 - Change-over switch for AC ammeter (for each phase of power transformer secondary circuit)

1 - AC voltmeter

1 - Change-over switch for AC voltmeter (between each phase of power transformer secondary circuit)

And other necessary equipment;

## **8.3.4.6** Bow Thruster Feeder Panel

The bow thruster panel including:

1 –Air circuit breaker (ACB) (draw-out type)

1 –ACB open/close control switch (or push button)

1 –ACB close indicating lamp

1 –ACB open indicating lamp

1 –Ammeter

And other necessary equipment

## **8.3.4.7** Group Start Panels

The starters for the essential pumps and ventilators in the engine room shall be assembled into group starter panels. Each unit (fixed type) to have circuit breaker, AC 440V/220V transformer, contactor, thermal relay, indicating pilot, push buttons, ammeter and running hour meter etc. which to be of fixed type.

Automation change-over function shall be provided for primary essential duplicate pumps.

The exact item and layout of starter unit shall be determined later during detail design.

**Following items to be agreed for detail design:**

**The main switch is to be lockable by pad lock (to inhibit start).**

**When starter is not visible at the motor, a separate start/stop switch shall be installed near the motor.**

**Starters for redundant motors shall be installed in different GSP’s, supplied from the different sections of the main switchboard.**

## **8.3.5** EMERGENCY SWITCHBOARD

In case that the contents in the following each panel of this section differ from manufacturer's standard for specific equipment, Manufacturer's standard shall be applied in general.

Emergency switchboard shall be installed in emergency generator room.

In principle, the construction of the emergency switchboard shall be similar to the main switchboard, but service access at front.

The emergency generator shall be protected by a three-pole air circuit breaker (ACB), which to be of draw-out type.

Interlock circuit shall be provided between emergency generator ACB and the space heater circuit.

**A socket of portable welding machine shall be supplied in the ECR, which shall be powered from the ESB.**

The switchboard shall be consisted of the following:

## **8.3.5.1** Generator Panel

1 -Air circuit breaker (ACB) (draw-out type)

1 -AC ammeter

1 -AC voltmeter

1 -Change-over switch for AC voltmeter (between each phase of generator)

1 -Frequency meter

1 -kW meter

1 -Bus tie for link with the main switchboard

1 –Running hour meter

1 -Switch for space heater

1 -Generator running indicating lamp (white)

1 -ACB close indicating lamp (green)

1 -ACB open indicating lamp (red)

1 -Space heater indicating lamp (orange)

1 -Manual voltage adjuster (if necessary)

1 -Red lamp for ACB abnormal trip

And other necessary equipment

Each panel:

1 - Insulation monitor with alarm lamp (for AC 440V & 220V).

1 - AC ammeter

1 - Change-over switch for AC. ammeter (for each phase of emergency power transformer secondary circuit)

1 - AC voltmeter

1 - Change-over switch for AC voltmeter (between each phase of emergency power transformer secondary circuit)

1 - Mega-ohm meter with change-over switch

## **8.3.6** SHORE CONNECTION BOX

One (1) set of shore connection box for receiving AC 440V volts, 400 amperes, 3 phase 60 Hz shore source shall be provided and wired to the main switchboard (MSB).

The box shall be of drip-proof type with a three (3) pole moulded case circuit breaker (MCCB), connecting terminals and phase sequence indicator; and:

**1 - White lamp for shore source alive**

**1 - Green lamp for shore MCCB closed**

**1 - White lamp for shore MCCB open**

**1 - Voltmeter for shore power**

**1 - Ammeter for shore power**

**Interlocking shall be arranged to disable any parallel operation with the ship’s generators.**

The shore connection box shall be of wall mounted type and shall be installed near emergency generator room or other suitable place.

On the bulkhead of laid room, a hole with water tight cover shall be provided for passing through the shore connection cables.

## ***8.3.7*** *AMP ready*

***MSB with additional empty panel(cold-ironing) , and cable tray shall be installed which shall route from the cold-ironing panel to the port side on upper deck of AMP ready position with water tight penetration; packaged container solution with all other AMP device will be separated and supplied by the Buyer (refer to the installation of 40ft container which will include relevant transformer and AMP connection box inside). Appropriate space for future AMP device ready shall be considered on board.***

***MV transformer and cable reel shall not be installed on board. The Buyer will rent the container, which shall be contained with MV transformer(1.6MVA) and reel.***

***The cable for shore connection shall not be supplied by the Builder***

## **8.3.8** TEST PANEL

One (1) set of wall mounted type electrical test panel shall be installed in the electrical workshop. The panel shall be provided with following devices: (or according to manufacturer's standard) switches, pilot lamps, voltmeter and ammeter.

| Each one (1) | Receptacle of non-water-tight and water-tight for AC 220V, 10A |

## **8.4** SECONDARY SOURCE

## **8.4.1** TRANSFORMERS

1. For General Service

Two (2) sets of 3 phase main transformer (i.e. d-d or y-y) shall be installed in the engine room. One (1) transformer shall be capable of supplying to all AC220V service so that only one (1) transformer is for working and the other is for spare. Working transformer manually changing-over shall be provided only.

Principal particulars shall be as follows:

Type: Drip-proof, dry type

Output: Abt.99 kVA (as per final E-balance)

Number: 2 (one as stand-by)

Voltage: AC 450/230V

Frequency: 60 Hz

Insulation: Class F

Rating: Continuous

Cooling: Natural-cooling

1. For Emergency Service

Two (2) sets of 3 phase transformers (i.e. d-y11) shall be installed in the emergency generator room for emergency service. One (1) transformer shall be capable of supplying all emergency service so that only one (1) transformer is for working and the other is for spare. Working transformer manually changing-over shall be provided.

Principal particulars shall be as follows:

Type: Drip-proof, dry type

Output: Abt. 50 kVA (as per final E-balance)

Number: 2 (one as stand-by)

Voltage: AC 450/230 V

Frequency: 60 Hz

Insulation: Class F

Rating: Continuous

Cooling: Natural-cooling

1. For Galley Service

One (1) set of 3 phase transformers (i.e. y-d11) shall be installed in galley room or near place for galley service. The transformer shall be double wiring and capable of supplying all AC440V & AC220Vservice.

Principal particulars shall be as follows:

Type: Drip-proof, dry type

Output: Abt. 99 kVA (450V 65kVA / 230V 30kVA) (as per final E-balance)

Number: 1

Voltage: AC 450/450V/ 230 V

Frequency: 60 Hz

Insulation: Class F

Rating: Continuous

Cooling: Natural-cooling

## **8.4.2** STORAGE BATTERIES AND BATTERY CHARGING BOARD

## **8.4.2.1** For General Use and for Engine Room Area

The maintenance free lead-acid type batteries to be installed as follows:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | No. of set | Capacity  (Ah) | Voltage  (V) | Rating | Location |
| For general service | 1 | 200 | 24 | 10 hours | Engine room |
| 1 | 200 | 24 | 10 hours | Battery room |
| For automation system | Manufacturer's standard | | | | Engine room |
| For radio equipment | Manufacturer's standard | | | | Radio space |
| For emergency generator starting | Manufacturer’s standard | | | | Emergency generator room |

Each one (1) set of charging and discharging board for general service batteries and engine room battery may be of floating charging type.

All necessary charging apparatus i.e. source switch, transformer, voltage adjuster, silicon rectifier, voltmeter, ammeter, indicating lamps, miniature circuit breaker (MCB), fuses, etc. to be provided.

24V DC distribution board (with feeder breakers, insulation monitor, ammeter, voltmeter and other necessary fittings;

**A safety factor of 1.3 is to be used for the calculation of the capacity of all batteries to compensate for capacity loss caused by ageing.**

**1. All battery chargers are to be capable of supplying the total load of all consumers and simultaneously charge totally empty batteries.**

**2. Chargers are to be able to operate with batteries disconnected. A low voltage alarm for the battery and battery charger output is to be provided in AMS.**

## **8.4.2.2** Other

Battery for emergency generator engine starting and for radio emergency source shall be provided according to the Rules and Manufacturer's standard.

Emergency generator engine starting battery shall be charged by a charger supplied by emergency’s generator maker.

Radio battery shall be charged by a charger incorporated in radio console.

The power socket, cables with plugs etc. for life boat and rescue boat battery charging shall be equipped (if necessary) and the chargers shall be fixed on boat.

## **8.5** DISTRIBUTION SYSTEM

## **8.5.1** ELECTRIC DISTRIBUTION

In general, separate main feeders shall be fed from the main switchboard to essential pump motors, bow thruster, each reefer power distribution panel, each power distribution panel, and one (1) of steering gear motor and other large capacity services.

Motors of which starters are assembled into the group starter panels, however, shall be connected to the AC 440 V feeder bus bar of the main switchboard.

Non-essential services and other small motors shall be connected to each distribution board or local group starter board fed from the main switchboard.

Separate feeders shall also be fed from the emergency switchboard to one (1) of the steering gear motor, one (1) set of the E/R exhaust fan and emergency fire pump motor, emergency air compressor motor, generator engine pre-lub. oil pump etc.

The general lighting system and AC 220 V general consumers shall be fed from AC 220 V feeder panel of the main switchboard.

Emergency lighting system and AC 220 V system of radio equipment and nautical instruments shall be fed from AC 220 V feeder panel of the emergency switchboard.

DC 24V system of alarm, DC 24V emergency lighting, some interior communication equipment and nautical instruments shall be fed from the battery charging & discharging board.

## **8.5.2** SECTION AND DISTRIBUTION BOARDS

All section boards and distribution boards shall be enclosed with steel sheet case.

***Certified rubber insulation mats (IEC61111) shall be provided around reefer container distribution panels.***

Distribution boards and section boards fitted in the living quarters and other similar places shall be of non-water-proof type, and those fitted in the engine room, steering gear room, stores and other similar places shall be of drip-proof type.

Reefer container distribution panels shall be fitted in under deck passageway of cargo hold region and shall be non-water-proof type.

In general, distribution boards and section boards shall be equipped with two or three pole miniature circuit breaker (MCB).

An electric circuit drawing shall be provided in a vinyl envelope in each distribution boards or boxes.

The circuit label shall be fitted on the inside of each board door.

## **8.5.3** CONNECTION BOXES AND BRANCH BOXES

All boxes shall be of drip-proof or water-proof construction depending on their locations. The water-proof type connection box exposed to weather deck to be brass-made or stainless steel.

## **8.5.4** RECEPTACLE FOR REEFER CONTAINER

Total 220 reefer container sockets (CEE type, 32A) will be provided on open deck.

Suitable number multi-gong type receptacle box shall be installed on operation platform.. Each gang should include circuit breaker, and power receptacle etc. these receptacle box shall be connected to some reefer distribution panels, each reefer distribution panel shall be fed from the main switchboard.

One (1) set of reefer container monitoring system, which to be of power cable data transmission (PCT) type with operating and display (24” TFT) unit shall be installed in ship office.

The communication between the PCT system and loading computer shall be established, therefore, necessary hardware and software shall be provided.

**Where the water-proof socket outlets on upper deck are exposed to rain, sea water splashes, etc. the socket outlet to be protected with sheet steel casing. But Reefer container sockets below hatch coaming no need protection.**

**Each individual reefer socket shall be capable of being switched on/off.**

## **8.6** ELECTRIC MOTOR AND CONTROL GEAR

## **8.6.1** GENERAL

The specification described in this section shall be applied to the power motors and their control equipment except for following electrical equipment which are constructed according the maker's standards:

(1) Galley and laundry equipment

(2) Governor motors

(3) Instrumentation and automation equipment

(4) Motors and their control equipment supplied as a complete set with auxiliaries machinery such as deck machinery, aux. blower, turning gear, small and household appliances etc.

## **8.6.2** MOTORS

## **8.6.2.1** General

All motors, unless otherwise specified, shall be marine type squirrel cage induction motors.

Motors shall be designed for AC 440 V, 3 phase, 60 Hz, except for that the motors of 0.5 kW rating and less may be of AC 220 V, 3 phase or single phase type according to manufacturer's standard.

Enclosure of motors shall be generally provided as follows:

Water-proof type (IP 56) for motors exposed to weather.

Totally enclosed type (IP 44) for steering gear, emergency fire pump and motors in engine room, provision refrigerating room, purifier area, galley and similar spaces.

Drip-proof type (IP 23) used for motors in accommodation and other dry spaces.

The enclosed type (IP23) will be for bow thruster motor.

Space heater shall be provided for all motors on open deck and motors of steering gear, emergency fire pump, M/E turning gear, bow thruster and motor rated power over 10 kW in engine room.

## **8.6.2.2** Insulation and terminal box

In general, class “B” or “F” insulation shall be adopted, except special service motors for which insulation are in accordance with the manufacturer's standard.

In general, all motors shall be provided with waterproof terminal box of cast iron or steel plate construction with gland and removable cover. All terminals shall be marked.

## **8.6.3** STARTERS

## **8.6.3.1** General

All motors with reversible feature (eg. ER Vent fans) shall have timer interlock to prevent immediate reversal.

In general, starters shall be of magnetic control type with thermal protect device except for that small motors (0.5 kW and less) may be manually operated by line switch or miniature circuit breaker (MCB).

In general, motors shall be arranged to start direct on-line (DOL), but for 100 kW and above large capacity motors, star – delta starting, auto-transformer starting reduced voltage starting means shall be adopted.

In general, voltage for control circuits shall be isolated from main power source via transformer.

The wiring diagram of starter shall be fitted on the back of each starter door.

In general, starters located out of sight the motors shall have local interlock type with running indication lamp start/stop push button box near respective motors, except for the E/R fans, accommodation fans and cargo hold fans.

Starters for motors of steering gear and those for essential services will be provided with under voltage release protection (UVR) will permit these motors being restarted automatically on restoration of main power, and starters for other motors to be provided with under voltage protection (UVP) feature.

**All motors with reversible feature (eg. ER Vent fans) shall have timer interlock to prevent immediate reversal.**

(A) Group Starter Board:

In general, starters shall be assembled in group starter boards as far as practicable.

The group starter board shall be in combination with starters according to their location and/or purpose.

These group starter boards shall be of bulkhead type or floor mounting type and shall be installed near the respective motors as far as practicable.

Each starter unit to be fixed type and built into one enclosed metal box of drip-proof construction with hinged door***.* Starters for redundant motors shall be installed in different GSP’s, supplied from the different sections of the main switchboard*.***

(B) Individual Starter Cabinets:

Starters which are not contained in the group starter board shall be mounted in the drip-proof metal cabinet.

The cabinet shall be arranged for bulkhead mounting type near the respective motor.

## **8.6.3.2** Ammeters and Running Hour Counters

Ammeters will be equipped on the starters for important motors in MSB and motor of 15 kW and above.

The running hour counters will be equipped on the starters for important motors in MSB and motor of 7.5 kW and above.

The ammeter on the starter shall be of overload type, the rated value shall be marked in red color.

## **8.6.3.3** Emergency Stop Device

1. For fire

All ventilating fans and oil pumps shall be capable of being stopped in case fire.

Emergency stop push button shall be provided for each group and their locations shall be as follows:

(a) Fuel oil pumps, lub. oil pumps, oil purifiers and ventilation fans in the engine room.

Emergency stop push button box shall be provided in the entrance of engine room, fire control station

(b) Ventilating fans in accommodation and cargo hold:

Each one (1) emergency stop push button box shall be provided in the wheelhouse and fire control station for stopping accommodation fans and cargo hold ventilating fans.

1. Other

Emergency stop button for engine room bilge pump and sludge pump include other system which may connect to shore cause potential pollution shall be provided on upper deck (port and starboard) according to the requirement of USCG Regulation.

**Emergency stop device shall have self-monitoring features like power failure and cable break. Emergency stop push button to be fitted with plastic covers. Box to be red painted**

Sea water discharge pumps having a water discharge outlet beneath the life boat stowing place above light ballast waterline, if any, shall be stopped in case of boat launching at the location of boat launch.

## **8.6.3.4** Steering Gear Motors

The steering gear motors shall be IP44 squirrel cage type and which power fed by separate feeder circuits, one (1) from main switchboard and another one (1) from emergency switchboard, according to the requirements of the Rules.

The feeder cables shall be run so as to minimize the probability of simultaneous failure of both feeders.

Both independent motor starters shall be located in the steering gear room. The motors can be controlled locally or from the bridge.

The steering gear alarm shall be installed on wheelhouse and in the ECR in accordance with the requirements of the rules.

## **8.6.3.5** Bow Thruster Motor and Control

Bow thruster motor shall be interlocked with bow thruster room fan and the pitch of blades is in zero position.

The motor shall be of single speed and non-reversible type. The motor rating is S2-30 min as per manufacturer’s manual.

The motor can be started/stopped from local starter and wheelhouse and can be emergency stopped from both bridge wings. The running indication shall be provided in wheelhouse.

PT100 temperature sensors will be supplied in main motor winding.

The starter for bow thruster is located in bow thruster room or suitable place,**BT starter to be in upper deck level of BT room and not in the same level as BT motor..**

Bow thruster pitch order & response signal will be supplied to VDR system from bow thruster remote control system.

Adjustable timer shall be provided in the starter to prevent immediate re-starting of bow thruster.

**Load indicator to be provided in wheel house panel. MSB Bow Thruster Feeder Panel to include Running indication and Abnormal Condition Lights.**

Following shall be provided for the control of bow thruster.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Location | Start/stop | Pitch control & indicator | Em'cy stop | Ammeter |
| Starter | O | - | - | O |
| Wheelhouse control panel | O | O | O | - |
| Wing control panels  (fixed type) | - | O | O | - |
| Local (motor side) | O | *-* | *-* | - |

## **8.6.3.6** Cargo Hold Fans Control

In general, each one starter shall be provided for each cargo hold fan, which can be combined in one group starter board together at suitable place; the power shall be feed from the MSB.

## **8.6.3.7** Preferential Tripping Arrangement

Preferential tripping arrangement shall be as follows:

First stage unload:

* Galley and laundry powers;
* Air conditioner compressor room warmers etc.
* Ventilation fan for accommodation
* Lathe, drilling machine, tool grinder
* Air conditioner for engine control room;

Second stage unload:

* Reefer containers

## **8.6.4** ELECTRIC WARMER FOR ROOM (AC 220 V)

Electric warmers for room shall be installed as follows:

2 x 2 kW – Steering gear room

2 x 2 kW - Emergency generator RM

2 x 2 kW – Bow thruster room

1 x 2 kW - Bosun store

2 x 2 kW- Wheelhouse

1 x 0.5 kW - Each public toilet

1 x 2 kW – Hospital

## **8.7** LIGHTING SYSTEM

## **8.7.1** GENERAL

The vessel shall be adequately illuminated throughout with fluorescent lights ***or energy saving light*** and supplemented by incandescent lights. Lighting fixtures for flood lighting shall be of halogen type lamps.

In general, incandescent lamps must be used as little as possible unless otherwise specified.

The lighting system shall be divided into normal lighting, emergency lighting.

Machinery space light should be arranged/supplied in such a manner that the failure of anyone branch circuit not to cause any space to be entirely dark.

In general, emergency lights shall be arranged without local switches, except for wheelhouse and crew cabins.

All emergency lights must be marked with a red mark.

***Anti-vibration mountings to be used in areas subject to local vibration (if necessary), except hanging type lighting fixtures.***

***The general features and dimensioning of lighting fixtures, switches and receptacles to be submitted for Owner's approval. Quantity and size of lighting fixtures, switches and receptacles may be changed in accordance with Owner's approved General Arr't of Electrical Equipment during plan approval procedure.***

***a) The lighting fixtures fitted in the weather part to be water-proof and to have the body of cast brass or brass plate or stainless steel or synthetic resin.***

***b) Lighting fixtures fitted under the risk of mechanical damages to be protected with guards for (energy saving tube) lights and polycarbonate globes for fluorescent lights.***

***c) For protection guards, steel guards to be used for the lamps fitted indoor space and brass guards for the lamps exposed to weather***

***Incandescent Lamps to be replaced by energy saving tube wherever is feasible.***

Emergency light may be normally used as part of the general lighting system and 1/3 quantity at least in the following rooms & spaces :.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Wheelhouse | Inner and outer passages |
| Electric equipment room | Stairs in accommodation |
| Emergency generator room | Workshop |
| Hospital | Engine control room |
| Offices | Engine room |
| Public rooms | Steering gear room |
| Public toilet and deck toilet | Emergency fire pump room |
| Navigating light and signal lights | Chart light |
| Fire control station | Navigation Equipment |

In general the enclosure of the lighting fixtures and fittings shall be of the following type dependent on their location:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Waterproof type:  (IP 55) | Spaces exposed to the weather, pipe funnel, refrigerated chamber, E/R below floor, oil purifier area, machinery spaces, store room, laundry, bow thruster room etc. wet spaces. |
| Enclosed type (IP 34 or 44) | Galley and pantry |
| Non-waterproof type:  (IP 22) | All cabin, mess room, engine control room, wheelhouse, control room and office etc. dry spaces. |
| Explosion proof type: | Battery room, paint store, acetylene bottle store and other dangerous spaces. |
