## **8.7.8** PORTABLE LAMPS

Total ten (10) sets of 24 V, 60 W portable working lamps (no-explosion proof type) with protection cover shall be provided. Each portable lamp shall have flexible cord of fifteen (15) meters with plug.

Five (5) sets of explosion proof type, chargeable, portable battery lamp shall be provided.

## **8.7.9** CONTROL OF LIGHTING

The ceiling lights in the engine room shall be generally controlled by miniature circuit breakers (MCB) of the distribution boards in the engine room.

In mess rooms, recreation room, wheelhouse and engine control room etc. spaces, in case multiple access are arranged, the two-pole two-way switches shall be installed in each entrance for control the ceiling lights in common.

The lights in workshops and engine & electrical stores shall be controlled by a switch located near the respective entrances.

The lights in the machinery compartments such as steering gear room, emergency generator room, etc. shall be controlled by a switch located near respective entrances.

Cargo hold lights shall be controlled by switches on main deck suitable location.

**Cargo hold light (except inside C/H) and outside lights shall be controlled by switches in the wheelhouse.**

The lights in the living quarters, public spaces, stores, etc. shall be controlled by respective switches located near the entrances in general.

The lights in the inner passages shall be controlled by the circuit breakers of the distribution boards.

The lights for the outside passages shall be controlled from the wheelhouse.

The outside floodlights shall be controlled by respective switches on the group switch board in the wheelhouse.

The lights in the stair case of the wheelhouse entrances shall be controlled by a door limit switch (if necessary) also.

The lights of the explosion-proof type shall be controlled by respective switches located in the safety place.

The lighting fixture in pipe duct shall be controlled (on/off) from the pipe duct entrance in engine room.

**Emergency lights shall be arranged without local switches, except for wheelhouse and crew cabins.**

## **8.7.10** SWITCHES

Switches in living quarters shall be of non-water-proof type, and switches in the machinery spaces, galley, laundry, toilets etc. shall be water-proof type in general.

Switches shall be constructed for wall mounting in general, and flush type switches shall be provided for the spaces where woody linings are fitted.

The switch for cold provision stores lighting shall be with a red indicating lamp to indicate when the inside lights are on.

Switches for berth lights and desk lights shall be fitted on their own fixtures.

In general, all tumbler switches and rotary switches for lighting branch circuits shall be of two-pole type.

## **8.7.11** RECEPTACLES

## **8.7.11.1** Non-water-proof Type Receptacles

Non-waterproof receptacles for small electric appliances shall be of, two (2) poles with earth contact type AC 220 V, 10 ampere capacity and shall be fitted as follows:

At least two (2) free receptacles shall be provided respectively in wheelhouse, chart space, radio space, mess room, hospital, engine control room, all crew's cabins, offices, inner passageway and other public room, at least 4 for after wall of wheelhouse.

In addition, each one (1) receptacle of two (2) poles, DC 24 V shall be provided at the rear of the main switchboard and the emergency switchboard.

## **8.7.11.2** Water-proof Type Receptacles

AC 220 V/24 V water-proof, two (2) poles with earthling contact, with switch receptacles boxes shall be fitted in steering gear room (2 sets), engine room (10 sets), bosun store (1 set), outside of ref. provision chamber (1 set), and emergency generator room (1 set), etc. used for portable lamps or tools.

Receptacles fitted in weather space shall be of brass-made

Two (2) AC 440 V receptacles for electric welding will be provided. One in E/R workshop, one in the bosun store forward.

Two (2) AC220V/10A receptacles protected by water-tight boxes will be provided for reefer container maintenance in each side of the reefer container cargo bay.

## **8.8** NAVIGATION LIGHTS AND SIGNAL LIGHTS

## **8.8.1** NAVIGATION LIGHTS

The following navigation lights shall be of double lamp type and connected to a panel with control switches and indicating lamps graphically arranged, audible and visible signal alarm, and this panel shall be incorporated into the wheelhouse control console.

Navigation lamps should be installed according the requirement of Rules. Navigation lights and its controller should meet the performance standard requirement MSC.253 (83) and as per rules.

Two separate feeder circuits shall be provided for the panel, one (1) from the AC 220V feeder panel of main switchboard directly and one (1) from the AC 220 V feeder panel of emergency switchboard directly.

Two (2) - Mast head lights AC. 220 V, 60-65 W

Two (2) - Side lights AC. 220 V, 60-65 W

One (1) - Stern light AC. 220 V, 60-65 W

## **8.8.1.1** Anchor Lights: (AC 220 V)

Each one (1) 60 W anchor light of lamp fixed type shall be fitted at the forward and after end of the vessel.

The source of anchor lights will be from navigation light control panel.

## **8.8.1.2** "Not-Under-Command" Lights: (AC 220 V)

Two (2) 60 W red all round lamps shall be fitted on the radar mast.

The source of NUC lights will from navigation light control panel.

## **8.8.1.3** Manoeuvring/Morse Signal Lamp: (AC 220 V)

A Manoeuvring/Morse signal lamp shall be mounted on the top of radar mast and four (4) keys shall be located at both bridge wings and on front wall of wheelhouse.

The Manoeuvring/Morse signal lamp shall also be controlled by the ship's horn system.

The control method of the Morse & manoeuvreing signal lamp should also meet the performance standard requirement MSC.253 (83) and as per Rules.

**The source of maneuvering/morse signal lights shall from navigation light control panel.**

## **8.8.2** Signal lights

## **8.8.2.1** Daylight Signal Lamp (DC 24 V)

One (1) set of portable type daylight signal lamp (60 W) shall be provided with battery and charger.

One (1) source receptacles shall be installed on each bridge wing.

## **8.8.2.2** SUEZ CANAL SIGNAL LIGHTS & SEARCHLIGHTS (AC 220 V)

One (1) set of 60 W fixed type Suez Canal signal light shall be provided, that is six (6) red, five (5) white and two (2) green. These signal lights shall be controlled by respective switches graphically arranged on the signal light control panel in the wheelhouse control console.

One (1) set of receptacle with switch used for Suez Canal searchlight (searchlight 3kW, ***Owner*** supply) shall be installed on the fore part.

Each one AC 220V 1000 W searchlights (with manual operation rotatable bracket) shall be installed on both wings of bridge deck.

## **8.8.2.3** SUEZ CANAL STERN LIGHT (AC 220 V)

One (1) set of 40 W fixed type red stern light shall be provided as the Suez Canal stern signal light.

## **8.8.2.4** DANGEROUS CARGO LOADING LIGHT (AC 220 V)

One (1) flash type red dangerous cargo loading light (40 W) shall be fitted on radar mast.

## **8.8.2.5** Panama CANAL Stering LIGHT (AC 220 V)

25W blue steering lights shall be fitted on the foremast behind and controlled from wheelhouse through dimmer switch.

## **8.8.2.6** Singapore strait lighT (AC 220 V)

One (1) set of Singapore strait light for vessel passing traffic separation scheme TSS (three all-round green lights 60W).

## **8.9** INTERIOR COMMUNICATION, ALARM AND MEASURING SYSTEM

## **8.9.1** SOUND POWER TELEPHONE

One (1) set of selective calling type sound power telephone system shall be provided as follows:

1- Wheelhouse

1- Emergency generator room

1- Fire control station

1- Steering gear room

1- Bow thruster room

1- Engine control room/main engine side.

1- Fuel oil filling station (one portable telephone and two sockets).

The sound power telephone in engine room, steering gear room, bow thruster room and emergency generator room shall be of anti-noise type (head set type).

## **8.9.2** AUTOMATIC TELEPHONE (AC 220 V & DC 24 V)

One (1) set of forty-eight (48) line automatic telephone system shall be provided. The number and location of telephone to be properly corrected according to the final general arrangement without capacity upgraded; Parallel connection shall be adopted for the engine room, workshop, and ECR.

Automatic telephone to be interfaced with Inmarsat Fleet broadband system for incoming and outgoing calls as per Maker’s standard.

The telephone sets shall be arranged in crew’s room, offices, public spaces, all control station, hospital, galley, steering gear room and other spaces where necessary for operation..

The telephone sets shall be adopted desk type, wall type or flush type according to their installed location.

The general telephone number list shall be supplied by builder and located beside each phone (paper with plastic coated).

The automatic telephone system shall be connected to the public addresser system to enable paging announcement spoken from wheelhouse, captain’s cabin, chief engineer’s cabin;

One (1) telephone socket shall be provided at each side on upper deck to connect with shore telephone line. The automatic telephone system shall be capable of receiving call from shore by this socket.

The priority function for the following sets shall be provided:

* Wheelhouse
* Captain cabin
* Engine control room
* **Fire control station**

**Automatic telephone to be interfaced with satellite VSAT for incoming and outgoing calls as per Maker standard. Extensions that can make and receive VSAT calls shall be as per instructions during plan approval.**

## **8.9.3** HOSPITAL CALL SYSTEM (DC 24 V)

One (1) set of calling bell system shall be provided as follows: Call push button Hospital (on berth side)

Buzzer with lamp Wheelhouse **& 2nd Officer cabin**

## **8.9.4** ENGINEER CALL SYSTEM (AC 220 V)

One (1) engineer call function shall be done in engine control console, each one (1) set of watch cabin panel with acknowledge push button shall be provided in chief engineer’s, 2nd engineer’s, 3rd engineer’s, 4th engineer’s, electrician’s cabin and recreation**,** Officer mess rooms.

**Patrol man in engine room call alarm to be provided.**

The system may be combined with both dead man alarm system and E/R monitoring & alarm system, i.e. this call system can be combined into extension alarm system.

## **8.9.5** Bridge navigation WATCH alarm SYSTEM（BNWAS）

One (1) set of bridge navigation watch alarm system (BNWAS) will be supplied according to requirements of the IMO Res.MSC.128 (75).

One (1) main unit shall be installed in wheelhouse control console and each one (1) set of signal box with acknowledge push button shall be provided in wheel house and both wing of the bridge, alarm signal of notification shall be provided in Captain, Chief off., 2nd off., 3rd off. cabin, Officer mess room and ship's office, recreation room and Gymnasium..

## **8.9.6** Refrigerated Chamber ALARM

One (1) set of refrigerated provision chamber alarm device shall be provided. Each one (1) switch with indicator shall be fitted in the refrigerated chamber and a bell with red lamp shall be fitted in the galley & a buzzer with lamp shall be fitted in wheelhouse so as to signal when a person is locked in.

## **8.9.7** ENGINE ROOM CO2 ALARM

One (1) set of engine room CO2 alarm system shall be provided for warning before CO2 extinguishing gas flooding into the engine room, and shall consist of an activated switch in the CO2 room, some horns with rotating lamp in engine room (signal light columns) and bells with lamp in engine control room.

**Engine room CO2 alarm sound shall be distinguished separately. The CO2 alarm is to be sent to AMS and VDR (direct to VDR).**

**The fire resistant type cable should be used in this system.**

## **8.9.8** EMERGENCY GENERAL ALARM SYSTEM

An electrically operated sounding alarm system consisting of bells and sirens, as appropriate, shall be provided with general alarm signals which shall be clearly audible in all conditions throughout the entire accommodation, navigating bridge, machinery space, and normal crew working spaces of the vessel.

The system with signal unit shall be used for sounding fire and general emergency alarm signal.

The system may be manually operated call points installed at the following locations:

* W/H control console
* Fire control station
* Embarkation

The general emergency alarm may be interface with public address system and in accordance with the Class requirement.

For the engine room and steering gear room, the light signal column shall be used for the alarm device. For main deck area, ship’s horns shall be used for this purpose.

The general emergency alarm may be interfaced with public address system also.

***“ Ref. SOLAS Ch. III Reg. 6 Clause 4.2”***

## **8.9.9** E/R SIGNALING AND ALARM SYSTEM (LIGHT COLUMN)

Signaling and alarm system (alarm lighting column) shall be provided in engine room, alarming engine room staff if specified alarm condition happen or telephone is calling in engine room or in ECR.

In engine room, include boiler, AC room, steering gear room, suitable amount of signal light panels shall be installed, with the following illuminated signaling/alarm identification signs according to IMO Resolution:

- Fire alarm – red globe with “FIRE” sign

- General alarm – green globe with “ALARM” sign

- CO2 alarm – red globe with “CO2” sign

- Engine failure alarm – amber globe with “FAILURE” sign

- Telephone communication call – white globe with “TELEPHONE” sign

- Telegraph alarm – white globe with “TELEGRAPH” sign

- Dead man alarm – amber globe with DEAD MAN ALARM sign

Simultaneously with alarm display in signal light panels, rotating lights (with red or amber globe) and electric sirens shall be actuated.

Telephone calling signal shall be stopped automatically if no acknowledgement follows in abt. 4 min.

The quantity and position of columns shall be an example which can be changed by the final designing:

4- Upper platform in E/R

4- Lower platform in E/R

2- Floor in E/R

1- Steering gear room

1- Purifier room

1- Engine casing

A mini column panel for alarm shall be installed in the engine control room.

Abt : 14 pieces.

Power supply – AC 220 V from emergency mains;

***"Ref. Appendix of "Code on Alerts and Indicators, (2009)"***

## **8.9.10** ELECTRIC TACHOMETER FOR MAIN ENGINE

One (1) set of electric tachometer system shall be provided, measuring and indicating the speed in revolution per minute and the direction of rotation.

One (1) set transmitter shall be attached to the main engine and each one (1) receiver shall be installed as follows:

* Wheelhouse ceiling console (with separate dimmer)
* Both bridge wings wall type (with dimmer)
* C/Engineer’s day room
* Engine control console
* M/E machinery side

One (1) revolution counter and one (1) running hour counter shall be installed in the engine control console.

Illumination with dimmer switch shall be provided for the tachometer receivers in wheelhouse ceiling console and bridge wings.

## **8.9.11** RUDDER ANGLE INDICATOR

One (1) set of electrical rudder angle indicator system shall be provided as follows:

* One (1) transmitter with link bar stick in the steering gear room
* One (1) three (3) face type indicator in the wheelhouse
* One (1) indicator on wheelhouse ceiling console
* One (1) indicator in the engine control console
* Each one (1) indicator of watertight type on both bridge wings
* One (1) indicator in the steering gear room
* One (1) indicator on the navigation control console

Illumination with dimmer switch shall be provided for the rudder angle indicators in the wheelhouse and bridge wings.

## **8.9.12** PUBLIC ADDRESS WITH TALK BACK SYSTEM

One set of public addresser with talk back system shall be provided as follows:

One (1) - About 200 watts double amplifier ,the control panel/talk back shall be in the WHC.

Six (6) - Talk back station, each one (1) at the bridge wings, life boat embarkation station, ECR, forecastle deck and main deck after.

One (1) - 50 watts of water-proof type speaker, on the compass deck forward.

Eight(8) - 10 watts of water-proof type speakers, each one (1) on the forecastle deck, life boat embarkation stations, main deck after, four(4) in the engine room;

Fourteen (14) - 5 watts of water-proof type speakers, each one (1) at steering gear room, galley, AC room, CO2 room, E/R workshop, emergency generator room, bow thruster room and purifier room

Necessary quantity – 2 watts speakers of indoor type, in the engine control room, pantry, mess room, gymnasium, each lavatory and inner passage of each deck and other cabin if necessary (The speakers for inner passages shall of double face type).

The switches for selection of the speaker group shall be provided on the control panels and the speakers shall be grouped as follows:

- Compass deck

- Upper deck fore and aft

- Accommodation

- Engine room

- Emergency

The system to be arranged to operate in following orders of priority:

1st -Emergency broadcasting

2nd -Emergency general alarm

3rd -Broadcasting or paging from telephone

4th -Broadcasting of entertainment programs

Note:

1. Talk back system maybe is separated type and to be in accordance with Maker’s standard.

2. The public address system maybe is changed according to final selected Maker's standard.

3. Radio tuner and CD player to be provided r. Any entertainment system to be automatically turned off when the general alarm system is activated.

## **8.9.13** SHIP'S HORNS

One whistle system with air horn, electric motor horn complete with automatic fog signal control unit shall be provided.

Air horn with magnetic valve shall be mounted on the radar mast; electric motor horn shall be mounted on the fore mast; one (1) time controller shall be in the wheelhouse control console.

Manual operation facility shall be provided for the air horn.

The horn shall be capable of automatic blowing for fog signal by means of time controller; it may be operated by push button switches also as following:

2- water tight type for wings;

2- for bridge console near the OOW seat;

2- at the front bulk of wheelhouse where the OOW usually stay for watching

In addition, the air horn on the radar mast shall be operated by mechanical pull from the wheelhouse or one DC 24V solenoid valve to be provided for emergency operation purpose.

The horn light may be used in common with Morse signal light also. And the light control function will meet requirement of IMO MSC.253 (83)

Electric heaters for the air horn and electric motor horn shall be provided.

## **8.9.14** FIRE DETECTING AND ALARM SYSTEM

(1) One (1) set of ***fixed addressable type fire detection and fire alarm system shall be so installed and arranged as to provide smoke detection in all corridors, stairways and escape routes within accommodation spaces as per the SOLAS IC requirement:***

One (1) - Fire alarm panel in the wheelhouse

One (1) –Fire alarm repeater in fire control station

One (1) –Fire alarm repeater in ECR

Heat detector - in galley, recreation room and engine room

Smoke detector - in passage, stair of accommodation, laundry, engine room, steering gear room and other machinery space; Smoke detector in E/R workshop shall be with blocking time controller (0~2 hours)

Push button - in passage near the exit, wheelhouse, engine control room, entrance to the E/R, steering gear room, emergency generator room etc.;

**Fire detection and alarm system shall be independent and not to be combined with fixed water mist fire fighting system in engine room.**

I.S. type smoke detector shall be provided in paint store, battery store, and other dangerous area.

Emergency batteries to be built in fire alarm panel, when main net failure, the emergency batteries to support the system working normally as per rules.

**Stairway doors closer shall be connected to fire alarm system for automatic closing after 2 mins of fire alarm.**

**The fire alarm signal to be sent to VDR.**

(2) One set of smoke detection and alarm system for cargo hold shall be provided as follows:

Detecting and monitor panel: CO2 room

Exhaust fan motor box: Suitable location

Some smoke sample intake: Suitable location in cargo hold

Detecting and monitor repeater: Wheelhouse

Both systems should interface with the VDR.

## **8.9.15** FIXED GAS DETECTION SYSTEM

None

## **8.9.16** ELECTRIC CRYSTAL CLOCK

One (1) set of electric crystal clock system shall be provided as follows:

1 -Master clock with slave clock control panel in chart space.

The master clock unit shall be incorporated with GMT and local time indication and slave clock control device such as advance and reverse control switch etc.

The Master clock shall be interfaced with DGPS.

Two hands slave clock:

Decorative type: Each captain class day room

Mess room

Recreation room

Gymnasium

Chief. Officer

Second engineer day room

**Ship office**

Ordinary type: Each one (1) double side type in corridor for each deck of accommodation

Each office

Hospital

Pantry

Galley

Three hands slave clock: Wheelhouse control console,

Engine control room

Three hands slave clock (UTC type): Radio space

## **8.9.17** PC LOCAL AREA NETWORK

1- LAN system (***Owner*** supply; 10 stand socket, ***CAT.6 type*** cable wiring ***and sockets shall*** be supplied by the Builder only)

**This system to be connected to VSAT.**

## **8.9.18** E/R local water mist alarm system

One (1) set fire alarm control panel of local water mist system shall be in the fire control station.

One (1) set local pumps unit and starters in E/R.

One (1) set repeater panel in wheelhouse control console and alarms connected to the AMS

Other flame detector, manually operated call points, flash lamp & sirens etc. will be provided in each local mist area (i.e. M/E, A/E, F.O. purifier, boiler area etc.) as per rule.

## **8.10** NAUTICAL INSTRUMENT

Equipment and arrangement of nautical instrument will be supplied as per the rules requirement.

## **8.10.1** Magnetic Compass (AC 220 V, DC 24 V)

One set of transmitting type magnetic compass (TMC) with reflector binnacle shall be installed. Transmitting magnetic compass signal should be connected to auto pilot.

Accessory to be provided as per the Maker’s standard.

Heading signal of TMC should be sent to the steering unit for auto steering and off-course alarm in the event of a gyrocompass failure.

One (1) spare bowl will be provided. Heading signal of TMC should be sent to the steering unit for auto steering and off-course alarm.

A length of bypass tube and facilities shall be considered as per the maker’s standard if the binnacle had to locate a distance from the top of the helmsman position in the wheelhouse.

Dimmer at bridge console for magnetic compass lamps of both DC24V and AC220V shall be provided.

## **8.10.2** GYRO COMPASS (AC 220 V, DC 24 V)

One (1) set of gyro-compass shall be installed as follows:

1 – Master compass

1 – Digital repeater on W/H front ceiling console

1 – Bearing repeater with pedestal on each bridge wings

1 –Bearing repeater in steering stand of W/H

1 – Repeater in steering gear room

1 – Digital indication in captain’s day room

1 – Course recorder (only heading signal to be recorded) in chart space of W/H

1 – Rate of turn indicator on W/H front ceiling console

1 – Set of azimuth mirror and azimuth circle

1 – Repeater of heading type for conning position 1.of PANAMA required.(acc.rules)

Heading output signals shall be sent to Inmarsat- Fleetboard Band if necessary, VDR, AIS, ECDIS, radars and auto-pilot etc. External signals from the speed log, DGPS etc. shall be received.

The rate of turn signal shall sent to the ECDIS

## **8.10.3** AUTO PILOT (AC 220 V, DC 24 V)

One (1) complete set of adaptive auto-pilot shall be installed consisting of:

One (1) - Steering stand in the wheelhouse, which might be combined with the bridge consoles;

The steering stand shall be equipped with a steering mode select switch in order to select the operation mode of automatic steering or electric hand steering with follow-up or non follow-up control. Non follow-up control units for both bridge wings shall be provided.

The steering stand shall be provided with power failure alarm and off course alarm.

The feedback unit shall be arranged in steering gear room with level link rod as per the maker’s standard .

Auto pilot override tiller to be provided in main console on wheelhouse.

The heading signal from the magnetic compass and gyro compass shall be connect in the autopilot separately.

## **8.10.4** ECHO SOUNDER (AC 220 V)

One (1) set of echo sounder with necessary accessories shall be installed as follows:

1- Transducer in bottom of fwd working frequency type of transducer to be 200 kHz according to Maker’s standard,

***(Option: 1- Transducer in bottom of stern, and the bridge screen at the same time can display the depth of F/A);***

1- Main display in the chart space

1- Display in wheelhouse ceiling panel.

The maximum depth range scale is 300 meters or as per Maker’s standard and signal shall be transmitted to VDR and ECDIS.

## **8.10.5** SPEED LOG (AC 220 V)

The speed log must meet the requirement of Resolution MSC.334 (90).

***(Option:Speed log on the bridge display screen, there are speed of water or speed of ground, were displayed the direction of flow and arrows of velocity indicator.)***

One (1) set of Doppler speed log shall be provided as follows:

1- Transducer with gate valve fitted in ship forward bottom

1- Electronic unit in fore room

1- Main unit in chart space

**1**- Speed indicator at wheelhouse ceiling console

The speed signal shall be sent to two radars, AIS and VDR and autopilot etc.

## **8.10.6** RADAR PLANT (AC 440 V/AC 220 V)

Two (2) sets of marine raster scan radar equipment shall be provided ***at wheehlouse, (Option:both Radars were installed the Uninterruptible Power System(UPS) )***

***(Option: A monitoring screen in the Master’s room, and there should be a switch to change the screen to the S/band or X/band.)***

The particulars to be as follows:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | No.1 | No.2 |
| Frequency band: | X-band | S-band |
| Peak output power: | abt.25 kW | abt.30 kW |
| Min. Display area | 340 mm x 340 mm  at least | 340 mm x 340 mm  at least |
| Display mode | relative/true motion | relative/true motion |
| Scanner size | 7~ 9 feet | 12 feet |
| Performance monitor | fitted | fitted |
| ARPA | with | with |

The data from AIS shall be capable of being displayed on TFT of both radars.

Gyro, AIS, speed log and DGPS signals shall be sent to X-band and S-band radar.

Both screens will be at least24" color TFT screens.

Above radars performance standard should be to meet IMO resolution MSC.192 (79).

## **8.10.7** ELECTRONIC CHART DISPLAY & INFORMATION SYSTEM (AC 220 V)

Electronic chart display & information system (ECDIS) will fully comply with the latest standards and resolutions of IMO, IHO, and IEC. The electronic chart is compatible with ENC (S57 Edition 3) charts, C-MAP, ARCS charts etc. The electronic chart can be overlaid with a variety of navigation data such as radar images, position, heading, speed, and others to facilitate safe and efficient navigation.

Two (2) independent set of ECDIS (master & back-up) shall be provided; (Option:both ECDIS were installed the Uninterruptible Power System(UPS)}

(Option:A monitoring screen shall be arranged in the Master’s room, which may be combined with the one screen of radar in the room (if it were be)

They shall be supplied via navigation power distribution box which to be fed from MSB and ESB auto-changeable.

The ECDIS shall have following main functions:

Electronic chart;

Radar image superimposition;

Continuous monitoring vessel position;

Route planning and route monitoring etc.

Display of ECDIS to be 24".

External signals from echo sounder, anemometer, AIS, DGPS, gyrocompass, speed log and radars etc. shall be received.

## **8.10.8** DGPS NAVIGATOR

Two (2) sets of DGPS navigator with necessary accessories shall be provided: one set in wheelhouse control console and one set on the chart table.

Each 1 - Main display unit in chart space and on WHC

2 - Antenna on the after mast or compass deck

1 - Signal distribution box in wheelhouse

The GPS signal shall be sent to the following equipment: Inmarast-Fleet broadband , Inmarast-C, MF/HF DSC, VHF DSC, Radars, speed log, Echo sounder, VDR , gyro-compass,ballast water treatment, scrubber and other systems requirement etc.

## **8.10.9** ANEMOMETER and ANEMOSCOPE (AC 220 V)

One (1) set of anemometer of propeller type ***(Option: ultrasonic type)***shall be provided.

1-Transmitter on the radar mast

1-Wind speed and direction indicator with illumination on the W/H ceiling console

Interface facility to ECDIS shall be provided.

## **8.10.10** WINDOW WIPER and CVS (AC 220 V)

Abt. ***Three(3)*** sets of window wipers with heater ***and Two(2) CVS*** shall be installed on the front windows of the wheelhouse according to rules requirements. (Refer to Accommodation Part)

The wiper shall be of horizontal movement type. Speed controller at the bridge console shall be provided for each window wiper.

***Each CVS controller shall be located at the lower part of front bulkhead***

## **8.10.11** VOYAGE DATA RECORDER VDR (AC 220 V, DC 24 V)

One (1) set of voyage data recorder system VDR which performance standard will meet the requirement of Resolution MSC.333 (90) shall be provided as follows:

One (1) main electronics unit for data acquisition and recording shall be installed in the suitable space of bridge deck.

One (1) capsule (black box, auto floating type) ***and*** One (1) capsule (black box, fixed type) shall be fixed on compass deck and shall be capable of being removed but secure against tampering.

Interface box and power supply unit shall be provided. ***The data shall be easy download without any special needs to a hard drive and can be play back on a normal PC.***

Six (6) sets of microphones to be provided, two (2) outdoor type microphones on both bridge wings and four (4) indoor type microphones in the wheelhouse.

VDR extension backup cable for captain day room computer will be provided and the computer shall be supplied by ***Owner***.

Gyro compass, speed log, echo sounder, at least 2 stations radar video, DGPS, rudder order, engine order, wind speed and direction, VHF communication audio, alarm and other information requirement by rules shall be sent to the VDR.

## **8.10.12** AUTOMATIC IDENTIFY SYSTEM (ais) (DC 24 V)

One (1) set of AIS with necessary accessories shall be provided.

One (1) set antenna shall be installed on compass deck and one (1) controller shall be installed in the wheelhouse.

One (1) interface for communicating between AIS and pilot’s computer shall be provided, and one (1) power receptacle with supply AC 110 V (USA type socket) for pilot’s computer shall also be provided.

AIS shall interface with Radar and ECDIS units to display the AIS information on Radar’s TFT and ECDIS display.

Gyro and DGPS signal and other information requirement by rules shall be sent to AIS. The system may be fed from DC 24 V and AC 220 V.

## **8.10.13** WHEELHOUSE CONTROL CONSOLE (WHC)

In case that the contents in the following parts of this section differ from Maker’s standard for specific equipment, Makers’ standard shall be applied in general.

The wheelhouse control console should consist of three parts, the navigation signal console (NSC), bridge maneuvering console (BMC) and steering stand. The following equipment specified in other part shall be installed at the consoles but not limit to.

## **8.10.13.1** Navigation Signal Console:

* Navigation light panel
* Signal light panel
* Outside light control panel
* Distribution boards for lighting, nautical equipment
* Emergency stop switch for the accommodation fans
* Emergency stop switch for the cargo hold fans
* Remote start and stop buttons for fire/G.S. pump and emergency fire pump
* Dimmer switches
* Hold fan emergency stop switch
* Hospital alarm buzzer
* Refrigerated chamber alarm buzzer with lamp
* And other necessary equipment
* AIS display unit
* X band radar display unit
* Extension alarm panel with group alarm indication
* General alarm control panel
* Window wiper controller (possible by the designing)
* Gyro compass component
* S-band radar display unit
* VDR control panel
* Engine order telegraph logger
* No.2 DGPS receiver
* No.2 VHF radiotelephone
* Bridge navigation watch alarm system (BNWAS)
* ECDIS
* Remote distress alarm push button for GMDSS
* Other necessary facilities

## **8.10.13.2** Bridge Maneuvering Console (BMC)：

* Main engine remote control unit
* Maneuvering lever and telegraph
* Bow thruster control unit
* ECDIS (with conning function)Auto telephone set
* Ship’s horn controller
* Automatic telephone and common battery telephone sets
* Public address control unit. Dimmer switches
* And other necessary equipment
* No.1 VHF radiotelephone

The wheelhouse control console shall be supplied from the AC 220 V normal supply system, the AC 220 V emergency supply system and the DC 24 V supply system.

## **8.10.15** MEASURING INSTRUMENT PANEL

One (1) measuring instrument panel shall be provided at the wheelhouse ceiling console and following equipment shall be mounted:

* Electric slave clock
* Digital type gyro compass repeater
* Revolution indicator for ME
* Anemometer
* Ship’s speed indicator
* Depth indicator of echo sounder
* Rate of turn indicator

## **8.10.16** CHART TABLE

One (1) chart table to be provided in the wheelhouse and following instruments to be mounted:

* Master clock with slave clock control panel
* Speed log indicator master panel
* No.1 DGPS
* Weather facsimile recorder
* Chart table lights with dimmer
* Course recorder
* Echo sounder main unit
* Navtex receiver

## **8.10.17** RADIO TABLE

One (1) radio and safety plan table to be provided in wheelhouse and the following instruments to be mounted:

* Data terminal for Inmarsat C
* Printer for Inmarsat C
* MF/HF radio controller
* Battery charger
* Low voltage power distribution box

## **8.10.18** STEERING STAND

One (1) steering stand to be provided as following:

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| 1 | - | Gyro repeater |
| 1 | - | Heading monitor |
| 1 | - | Steering gear alarm panel |
| 1 | - | Dimmer switches |

The steering stand can be combined into the wheelhouse control console; a UHF handset of hand-free type shall be prepared for the intercom with the docking workstation.

## **8.11** RADIO COMMUNICATION EQUIPMENT

## **8.11.1** GENERAL

Radio communication equipment shall comply with the International Telecommunication Radio Regulations and the SOLAS Convention (GMDSS) for A1, A2, A3 sea area and adopt shore-based maintenance.

## **8.11.2** MF/HF RADIO EQUIPMENT (AC 220 V, DC 24 V)

One (1) set of MF/HF radio equipment shall be installed in radio space.

1- 250W MF/HF transmitter

1- Self-supporting Tx antenna

1- MF/HF receiver

1- MF/HF receiving whip antenna

1- MF/HF DSC terminal

1- MF/HF DSC receiver and whip antenna

1- Radio controller

1- Battery charger

1- Set of necessary accessories according to Maker’s standard

## **8.11.3** VHF RADIO TELEPHONE

Two (2) sets of VHF radiotelephone of DSC with 57 channels and USA channel shall be installed in wheelhouse control console.

Each set including:

1-VHF telephone with DSC and whip antenna

1-VHF DSC watch receiver (channel 70) with antenna

The No.1 VHF shall be installed at Navigation Signal Console in hands reach area near the OOW seat, with one(1) remote control handset at the front bulk of wheelhouse.

No.2 VHF shall be installed at Navigation Console in hands reach area near the OOW seat, with slave sockets for both wings .

One (1) portable handset will be provided for both wings.

DC 24V Power should be fed from the radio battery.

## **8.11.4** SATELLITE COMMUNICATION SYSTEM

(1) INMARSAT-Feet Broadband FB 500 (AC 220 V)

One (1) set INMARSAT Fleet broad band 500 standard will be installed, consisting of:

1- Main unit

1- Telephone (in captain day room)

1- Facsimile in radio space

1- Antenna on compass deck

1- AC/DC power supply unit

(2) INMARSAT-C (AC 220 V / DC 24 V)

Two (2) sets of standard-C satellite communication SES with EGC reception (One of them may be combined with LRIT and SSAS function), each one shall be provided as follows:

1-Main unit

1-Terminal unit

1-Printer

1. Antenna

DC 24 V Power shall be fed from the radio battery.

## **8.11.5** NAVTEX RECEIVER

One (1) set of Navtex receiver (518 kHz & 490 kHz) with printer shall be provided in chart space. The system to be fed from DC 24 V and AC 220 V. Printer is according to maker’s standard.

## **8.11.6** UHF handset

Six (6) sets of portable UHF handset (400 MHz, including two explosive type, one hand-free type with certificate) and rechargeable battery and charger and holster, microphone shall be provided.

## **8.11.7** WEATHER FACSIMILE RECORDER

One (1) set of weather facsimile recorder shall be provided in chart space

## **8.11.8** SATELLITE EPIRB

One (1) set of self-float type emergency position indicating radio beacon operating on 406/121.5 MHz shall be fitted at the open part of bridge deck.

## **8.11.9** RADAR TRANSPONDER

Two (2) sets of radar transponder operating on 9 GHz shall be provided. Four(4) brackets shall be supplied, which two of them shall be installed in the lifeboats.

## **8.11.10** TWO-WAY RADIOTELEPHONE APPARATUS

Three (3) sets of two-way VHF with battery charger and 3 sets of primary batteries shall be provided as per the rules.

## **8.11.11** SHIP SECURITY ALERT SYSTEM (SSAS)

One (1) set of ship security alert system in compliance with the requirement of SOLAS will be installed. SSAS may be combined with Inmarsat C system.

Each one (1) security alert button shall be installed at wheelhouse and captain day room. The system will be fed from DC 24 V and AC 220 V.

## **8.11.12** Long range Identification and Tracking (LRIT)

One (1) set long range identification and tracking system (LRIT) will be provided.

LRIT may be combined with Inmarsat C system.

## **8.11.13** BROADCAST & TELEVISION RECEIVING ANTENNA SYSTEM (AC 220 V)

One (1) set of broadcast & TV receiving antenna system shall be provided as follows:

1 – Omni-direction type antenna for TV/FM/AM

Each 1 – Antenna outlet for radio and TV receiver in each private room, office, hospital, mess room and recreation room.

This system should be compatible for future SAT TV jumping in.

**In Cabins and Public areas where entertainment appliances are provided, an extra power socket should also be provided at each area.**

Broadcast receivers and TV sets etc. shall be supplied by ***Owner***, the Builder shall be in assistant to fix and secure the TV sets by practice.

## 8.11.14 vsat

Owner supply One set VSAT, shipyard in charge of cable and cable bracket installation.
